import { z } from "zod";

export const organizationStatusSchema = z.enum(["active", "inactive", "trial"]);
export const profileRoleSchema = z.enum([
  "platform_admin",
  "organization_admin",
  "professional",
  "teacher",
  "parent",
  "guardian",
]);
export const profileStatusSchema = z.enum(["active", "inactive", "invited"]);
export const membershipRoleSchema = z.enum([
  "owner",
  "admin",
  "professional",
  "teacher",
  "guardian_viewer",
]);

export const createOrganizationSchema = z.object({
  slug: z
    .string()
    .min(3)
    .max(50)
    .regex(
      /^[a-z0-9-]+$/,
      "Slug must use lowercase letters, numbers, and hyphens.",
    ),
  legalName: z.string().min(3).max(160),
  displayName: z.string().min(3).max(160),
  status: organizationStatusSchema.default("active"),
});

export const createProfileSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  fullName: z.string().min(3).max(160),
  role: profileRoleSchema,
  status: profileStatusSchema.default("active"),
  externalAuthId: z.string().min(1).max(160).optional(),
});

export const createMembershipSchema = z.object({
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  profileId: z.string().uuid(),
  membershipRole: membershipRoleSchema,
  isDefault: z.boolean().default(false),
});

export type CreateOrganizationInput = z.output<typeof createOrganizationSchema>;
export type CreateProfileInput = z.output<typeof createProfileSchema>;
export type CreateMembershipInput = z.output<typeof createMembershipSchema>;

export interface OrganizationSummary {
  id: string;
  slug: string;
  legalName: string;
  displayName: string;
  status: z.infer<typeof organizationStatusSchema>;
  logoUrl: string | null;
  memberCount: number;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface ProfileSummary {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  fullName: string;
  role: z.infer<typeof profileRoleSchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof profileStatusSchema>;
  preferredLocale: string | null;
  organizationCount: number;
  externalAuthId: string | null;
  createdAt: string;
}

export const updateProfileSchema = z.object({
  role: profileRoleSchema.optional(),
  status: profileStatusSchema.optional(),
  preferredLocale: z.string().min(2).max(10).nullable().optional(),
});

export const updateOrganizationSchema = z.object({
  logoUrl: z.string().url().nullable().optional(),
  displayName: z.string().min(3).max(160).optional(),
  status: organizationStatusSchema.optional(),
});

export type UpdateProfileInput = z.output<typeof updateProfileSchema>;
export type UpdateOrganizationInput = z.output<typeof updateOrganizationSchema>;

export interface MembershipSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  profileId: string;
  profileName: string;
  membershipRole: z.infer<typeof membershipRoleSchema>;
  isDefault: boolean;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface TenantCoreSnapshot {
  database: {
    status: "up" | "down";
    error: string | null;
  };
  stats: {
    organizations: number;
    profiles: number;
    memberships: number;
  };
  organizations: OrganizationSummary[];
  profiles: ProfileSummary[];
  memberships: MembershipSummary[];
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/scheduling/contracts.ts ---
import { z } from "zod";

export const availabilityModalitySchema = z.enum([
  "in_person",
  "telehealth",
  "hybrid",
]);
export const availabilityStatusSchema = z.enum(["open", "booked", "blocked"]);
export const appointmentTypeSchema = z.enum([
  "therapy_session",
  "school_meeting",
  "parent_guidance",
  "assessment",
  "follow_up",
]);
export const appointmentStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "scheduled",
  "confirmed",
  "completed",
  "cancelled",
  "no_show",
]);
export const appointmentChannelSchema = z.enum([
  "in_person",
  "telehealth",
  "hybrid",
]);
export const calendarSyncStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "not_synced",
  "pending",
  "synced",
  "error",
]);
export const reminderStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "not_scheduled",
  "scheduled",
  "sent",
  "skipped",
]);
export const calendarConnectionStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "connected",
  "error",
  "revoked",
]);
export const calendarSyncDirectionSchema = z.enum([
  "push",
  "pull",
  "bidirectional",
]);
export const calendarSyncJobStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "completed",
  "partial",
  "failed",
]);

export const createAvailabilitySlotSchema = z
  .object({
    organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
    professionalProfileId: z.string().uuid(),
    modality: availabilityModalitySchema.default("in_person"),
    status: availabilityStatusSchema.default("open"),
    locationLabel: z.string().min(3).max(160).optional(),
    notes: z.string().min(5).max(1200).optional(),
    startsAt: z.string().datetime(),
    endsAt: z.string().datetime(),
  })
  .refine(
    (value) =>
      new Date(value.startsAt).getTime() < new Date(value.endsAt).getTime(),
    {
      message: "Availability slot end must be after start.",
      path: ["endsAt"],
    },
  );

export const createAppointmentSchema = z
  .object({
    organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
    studentId: z.string().uuid(),
    availabilitySlotId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
    professionalProfileId: z.string().uuid(),
    requestedByProfileId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
    appointmentType: appointmentTypeSchema.default("therapy_session"),
    status: appointmentStatusSchema.default("scheduled"),
    channel: appointmentChannelSchema.default("in_person"),
    calendarSyncStatus: calendarSyncStatusSchema.default("not_synced"),
    reminderStatus: reminderStatusSchema.default("not_scheduled"),
    title: z.string().min(5).max(180),
    notes: z.string().min(5).max(1200).optional(),
    startsAt: z.string().datetime(),
    endsAt: z.string().datetime(),
  })
  .refine(
    (value) =>
      new Date(value.startsAt).getTime() < new Date(value.endsAt).getTime(),
    {
      message: "Appointment end must be after start.",
      path: ["endsAt"],
    },
  );

export const createCalendarConnectionSchema = z.object({
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  profileId: z.string().uuid(),
  providerKey: z.string().min(3).max(120).default("google_calendar"),
  externalCalendarId: z.string().min(3).max(200),
  syncStatus: calendarConnectionStatusSchema.default("connected"),
  scopes: z.array(z.string().min(1)).default(["calendar.events"]),
  metadata: z.record(z.string(), z.unknown()).optional(),
  lastSyncedAt: z.string().datetime().optional(),
});

export const runCalendarSyncJobSchema = z.object({
  connectionId: z.string().uuid(),
  triggeredByProfileId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  direction: calendarSyncDirectionSchema.default("bidirectional"),
  status: calendarSyncJobStatusSchema.default("completed"),
  appointmentsScanned: z.coerce.number().int().min(0).default(0),
  appointmentsSynced: z.coerce.number().int().min(0).default(0),
  notes: z.string().min(3).max(240).optional(),
  completedAt: z.string().datetime().optional(),
});

export type CreateAvailabilitySlotInput = z.output<
  typeof createAvailabilitySlotSchema
>;
export type CreateAppointmentInput = z.output<typeof createAppointmentSchema>;
export type CreateCalendarConnectionInput = z.output<
  typeof createCalendarConnectionSchema
>;
export type RunCalendarSyncJobInput = z.output<typeof runCalendarSyncJobSchema>;

export interface SchedulingReference {
  id: string;
  displayName: string;
}

export interface AvailabilitySlotSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  professionalProfileId: string;
  professionalProfileName: string;
  modality: z.infer<typeof availabilityModalitySchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof availabilityStatusSchema>;
  locationLabel: string | null;
  notes: string | null;
  startsAt: string;
  endsAt: string;
}

export interface AppointmentSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  studentId: string;
  studentCode: string;
  studentName: string;
  professionalProfileId: string;
  professionalProfileName: string;
  requestedByProfileName: string | null;
  availabilitySlotLabel: string | null;
  appointmentType: z.infer<typeof appointmentTypeSchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof appointmentStatusSchema>;
  channel: z.infer<typeof appointmentChannelSchema>;
  calendarSyncStatus: z.infer<typeof calendarSyncStatusSchema>;
  reminderStatus: z.infer<typeof reminderStatusSchema>;
  title: string;
  notes: string | null;
  startsAt: string;
  endsAt: string;
}

export interface CalendarConnectionSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  profileId: string;
  profileName: string;
  providerKey: string;
  externalCalendarId: string;
  syncStatus: z.infer<typeof calendarConnectionStatusSchema>;
  scopes: string[];
  metadata: Record<string, unknown>;
  lastSyncedAt: string | null;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface CalendarSyncJobSummary {
  id: string;
  connectionId: string;
  providerKey: string;
  externalCalendarId: string;
  triggeredByProfileName: string | null;
  direction: z.infer<typeof calendarSyncDirectionSchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof calendarSyncJobStatusSchema>;
  appointmentsScanned: number;
  appointmentsSynced: number;
  notes: string | null;
  completedAt: string | null;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface SchedulingSnapshot {
  database: {
    status: "up" | "down";
    error: string | null;
  };
  stats: {
    availabilitySlots: number;
    openSlots: number;
    appointments: number;
    scheduledAppointments: number;
    completedAppointments: number;
  };
  availabilitySlots: AvailabilitySlotSummary[];
  appointments: AppointmentSummary[];
  calendarConnections: CalendarConnectionSummary[];
  organizations: SchedulingReference[];
  students: SchedulingReference[];
  professionalProfiles: SchedulingReference[];
  availabilityReferences: SchedulingReference[];
}

import { z } from "zod";
import type {
  OrganizationSummary,
  ProfileSummary,
} from "@/src/lib/tenant-core/contracts";

export const roleScopeSchema = z.enum(["platform", "organization", "case"]);
export const onboardingPersonaSchema = z.enum([
  "platform_admin",
  "organization_admin",
  "director",
  "pie_coordinator",
  "professional",
  "external_therapist",
  "teacher",
  "parent",
  "guardian",
]);
export const onboardingStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "not_started",
  "in_progress",
  "completed",
  "blocked",
]);

export const createProfileOnboardingSchema = z.object({
  profileId: z.string().uuid(),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  personaType: onboardingPersonaSchema,
  status: onboardingStatusSchema.default("not_started"),
  currentStep: z.string().trim().min(1).max(120).optional(),
  completedSteps: z.array(z.string().trim().min(1).max(80)).default([]),
  metadata: z.record(z.unknown()).default({}),
});

export type CreateProfileOnboardingInput = z.output<
  typeof createProfileOnboardingSchema
>;

export interface RoleSummary {
  id: string;
  code: string;
  displayName: string;
  description: string | null;
  scope: z.infer<typeof roleScopeSchema>;
  active: boolean;
  permissionCount: number;
  permissionCodes: string[];
}

export interface PermissionSummary {
  id: string;
  code: string;
  domain: string;
  action: string;
  description: string | null;
}

export interface RoleAssignmentSummary {
  id: string;
  profileId: string;
  profileName: string;
  organizationId: string | null;
  organizationName: string | null;
  roleCode: string;
  roleDisplayName: string;
  source: string;
  active: boolean;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface ProfileOnboardingProgressSummary {
  id: string;
  profileId: string;
  profileName: string;
  organizationId: string | null;
  organizationName: string | null;
  personaType: z.infer<typeof onboardingPersonaSchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof onboardingStatusSchema>;
  currentStep: string | null;
  completedSteps: string[];
  metadata: Record<string, unknown>;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface AccessControlSnapshot {
  database: {
    status: "up" | "down";
    error: string | null;
  };
  stats: {
    roles: number;
    permissions: number;
    assignments: number;
    onboarding: number;
  };
  roles: RoleSummary[];
  permissions: PermissionSummary[];
  assignments: RoleAssignmentSummary[];
  onboarding: ProfileOnboardingProgressSummary[];
  moduleCatalog: LocalModuleDefinition[];
  moduleToggles: OrganizationModuleToggleSummary[];
  localRoleViews: OrganizationLocalRoleViewSummary[];
  organizations: OrganizationSummary[];
  profiles: ProfileSummary[];
}

export const organizationModuleKeySchema = z.enum([
  "student_core",
  "school_compliance",
  "care_coordination",
  "clinical_core",
  "scheduling",
  "billing",
  "interoperability",
  "ai_reports",
  "family_premium",
]);

export const localRoleViewSchema = z.enum([
  "director",
  "pie_coordinator",
  "teacher",
  "external_therapist",
  "guardian_family",
  "super_admin",
]);

export const upsertOrganizationModuleToggleSchema = z.object({
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  moduleKey: organizationModuleKeySchema,
  enabled: z.boolean().default(true),
  managedByProfileId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  metadata: z.record(z.unknown()).default({}),
});

export const upsertOrganizationLocalRoleViewSchema = z.object({
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  profileId: z.string().uuid(),
  viewKey: localRoleViewSchema,
  active: z.boolean().default(true),
  metadata: z.record(z.unknown()).default({}),
});

export type UpsertOrganizationModuleToggleInput = z.output<
  typeof upsertOrganizationModuleToggleSchema
>;
export type UpsertOrganizationLocalRoleViewInput = z.output<
  typeof upsertOrganizationLocalRoleViewSchema
>;

export interface LocalModuleDefinition {
  key: z.infer<typeof organizationModuleKeySchema>;
  displayName: string;
  audience: string;
  description: string | null;
}

export interface OrganizationModuleToggleSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;

import { z } from "zod";

export const studentStatusSchema = z.enum(["active", "inactive", "archived"]);
export const enrollmentTypeSchema = z.enum(["school", "clinical"]);
export const enrollmentStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "active",
  "inactive",
  "completed",
]);
export const careTeamRoleSchema = z.enum([
  "teacher",
  "professional",
  "school_admin",
  "care_coordinator",
  "guardian",
]);
export const careTeamVisibilityScopeSchema = z.enum(["full", "restricted"]);
export const supportNeedCategorySchema = z.enum([
  "communication",
  "behavioral",
  "sensory",
  "academic",
  "social",
  "daily_living",
  "regulation",
]);
export const supportNeedPrioritySchema = z.enum([
  "low",
  "medium",
  "high",
  "critical",
]);
export const supportNeedStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "active",
  "resolved",
  "monitoring",
]);
export const caseReviewTypeSchema = z.enum([
  "multidisciplinary",
  "clinical",
  "compliance",
  "family_follow_up",
]);
export const caseReviewStatusSchema = z.enum(["open", "in_review", "closed"]);

export const createStudentSchema = z.object({
  canonicalCode: z
    .string()
    .min(3)
    .max(80)
    .regex(
      /^[A-Z0-9-]+$/,
      "Canonical code must use uppercase letters, numbers, and hyphens.",
    ),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  firstName: z.string().min(2).max(100),
  lastName: z.string().min(2).max(100),
  preferredName: z.string().min(1).max(100).optional(),
  birthDate: z
    .string()
    .regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)
    .optional(),
  status: studentStatusSchema.default("active"),
  baselineSummary: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  primaryGuardianProfileId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  schoolOrganizationId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  gradeLevel: z.string().max(100).optional(),
});

export const createStudentEnrollmentSchema = z.object({
  studentId: z.string().uuid(),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  enrollmentType: enrollmentTypeSchema,
  enrollmentStatus: enrollmentStatusSchema.default("active"),
  gradeLevel: z.string().max(100).optional(),
  programName: z.string().max(160).optional(),
  startDate: z
    .string()
    .regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)
    .optional(),
  endDate: z
    .string()
    .regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)
    .optional(),
});

export const createStudentCareTeamMemberSchema = z.object({
  studentId: z.string().uuid(),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  profileId: z.string().uuid(),
  teamRole: careTeamRoleSchema,
  visibilityScope: careTeamVisibilityScopeSchema.default("full"),
  active: z.boolean().default(true),
});

export const createStudentSupportNeedSchema = z.object({
  studentId: z.string().uuid(),
  category: supportNeedCategorySchema,
  description: z.string().min(8).max(800),
  priority: supportNeedPrioritySchema.default("medium"),
  status: supportNeedStatusSchema.default("active"),
});

export const createStudentCaseReviewSchema = z.object({
  studentId: z.string().uuid(),
  organizationId: z.string().uuid(),
  createdByProfileId: z.string().uuid().optional(),
  reviewType: caseReviewTypeSchema.default("multidisciplinary"),
  status: caseReviewStatusSchema.default("open"),
  title: z.string().min(4).max(160),
  summary: z.string().min(12).max(1500).optional(),
  decisions: z.array(z.string().min(2).max(280)).max(12).default([]),
  nextReviewAt: z.string().datetime().optional(),
  closedAt: z.string().datetime().optional(),
});

export type CreateStudentInput = z.output<typeof createStudentSchema>;
export type CreateStudentEnrollmentInput = z.output<
  typeof createStudentEnrollmentSchema
>;
export type CreateStudentCareTeamMemberInput = z.output<
  typeof createStudentCareTeamMemberSchema
>;
export type CreateStudentSupportNeedInput = z.output<
  typeof createStudentSupportNeedSchema
>;
export type CreateStudentCaseReviewInput = z.output<
  typeof createStudentCaseReviewSchema
>;

export interface StudentSummary {
  id: string;
  canonicalCode: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  firstName: string;
  lastName: string;
  preferredName: string | null;
  birthDate: string | null;
  status: z.infer<typeof studentStatusSchema>;
  baselineSummary: string | null;
  primaryGuardianName: string | null;
  schoolEnrollmentName: string | null;
  careTeamCount: number;
  supportNeedCount: number;
  createdAt: string;
}

}

export interface StudentCareTeamMemberSummary {

  canonicalCode: string;

  organizationName: string;

  teamRole: z.infer<typeof careTeamRoleSchema>;
  visibilityScope: z.infer<typeof careTeamVisibilityScopeSchema>;
  active: boolean;

}

export interface StudentSupportNeedSummary {
  id: string;
  studentId: string;
  studentName: string;
  canonicalCode: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  category: z.infer<typeof supportNeedCategorySchema>;
  priority: z.infer<typeof supportNeedPrioritySchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof supportNeedStatusSchema>;
  description: string;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface StudentTimelineItem {
  id: string;
  studentId: string;
  canonicalCode: string;
  studentName: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  domain:
    | "student-core"
    | "school-compliance"
    | "care-coordination"
    | "clinical-core"
    | "scheduling";
  eventType: string;

export interface StudentAuditLogSummary {
  id: string;
  studentId: string;

  targetProfileName: string | null;
  resourceType: string;
  resourceId: string;
  action: string;
  purpose: string | null;
  outcome: "allowed" | "denied";
  ipAddress: string | null;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface StudentCaseReviewSummary {
  id: string;
  studentId: string;
  canonicalCode: string;
  studentName: string;
  organizationId: string;
  organizationName: string;
  createdByProfileName: string | null;
  reviewType: z.infer<typeof caseReviewTypeSchema>;
  status: z.infer<typeof caseReviewStatusSchema>;

  decisions: string[];
  nextReviewAt: string | null;
  closedAt: string | null;
  createdAt: string;
}

export interface StudentCoreSnapshot {
  database: {
    status: "up" | "down";
    error: string | null;
  };
  stats: {
    students: number;
    schoolEnrollments: number;
    familyLinks: number;
    careTeamLinks: number;
  };

  careTeamMembers: StudentCareTeamMemberSummary[];
  supportNeeds: StudentSupportNeedSummary[];
  caseReviews: StudentCaseReviewSummary[];
  timeline: StudentTimelineItem[];
  auditLogs: StudentAuditLogSummary[];
  organizations: Array<{ id: string; displayName: string }>;
  guardianProfiles: Array<{ id: string; fullName: string; email: string }>;
  careTeamProfiles: Array<{
    id: string;
    fullName: string;
    email: string;
    role: string;
    organizationName: string | null;
  }>;
}

import { z } from "zod";

export const bookingServiceModalitySchema = z.enum([
  "in_person",
  "telehealth",
  "hybrid",
]);

export const bookingServiceStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "draft",
  "active",
  "paused",
  "archived",
]);

export const bookingPublicProfileStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "draft",
  "published",
  "hidden",
]);

export const bookingReservationStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "pending_payment",
  "pending_confirmation",
  "confirmed",
  "cancelled",
  "rescheduled",
  "completed",
  "no_show",
  "expired",
]);

export interface BookingServiceSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  code: string;
  title: string;
  description: string | null;
  status: z.infer<typeof bookingServiceStatusSchema>;
  modality: z.infer<typeof bookingServiceModalitySchema>;
  durationMinutes: number;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface BookingPublicProfileSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  slug: string;
  title: string;
  description: string | null;
  status: z.infer<typeof bookingPublicProfileStatusSchema>;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface BookingReservationSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  publicReference: string;
  appointmentId: string | null;
  studentId: string | null;
  serviceId: string;
  customerName: string;
  customerEmail: string;
  status: z.infer<typeof bookingReservationStatusSchema>;
  startsAt: string;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export const updateBookingReservationSchema = z.object({
  reservationId: z.string().uuid(),
  status: bookingReservationStatusSchema,
  startsAt: z.string().datetime().optional(),
  note: z.string().trim().max(500).optional().nullable(),
});

export type UpdateBookingReservationInput = z.output<
  typeof updateBookingReservationSchema
>;

export const createBookingServiceSchema = z.object({
  code: z.string().trim().min(2).max(50),
  title: z.string().trim().min(3).max(120),
  description: z.string().trim().max(1000).optional().nullable(),
  status: bookingServiceStatusSchema.default("draft"),
  modality: bookingServiceModalitySchema.default("in_person"),
  durationMinutes: z.number().int().min(5).max(1440),
});

export type CreateBookingServiceInput = z.output<
  typeof createBookingServiceSchema
>;

export const createBookingReservationSchema = z.object({
  serviceId: z.string().uuid(),
  providerSlug: z.string().trim().min(2).max(50),
  customerName: z.string().trim().min(2).max(120),
  customerEmail: z.string().email().max(120),
  startsAt: z.string().datetime(),
});

export type CreateBookingReservationInput = z.output<
  typeof createBookingReservationSchema
>;

export const bookingCheckoutStatusSchema = z.enum([
  "created",
  "pending",
  "paid",
  "failed",
  "expired",
  "refunded",
]);

export const bookingPackStatusSchema = z.enum(["active", "archived"]);

export interface BookingPackSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  code: string;
  title: string;
  description: string | null;
  sessionCount: number;
  price: number;
  status: z.infer<typeof bookingPackStatusSchema>;
}

export interface BookingWalletSummary {
  id: string;
  organizationId: string;
  customerEmail: string;
  studentId: string | null;
  balanceSessions: number;
  balanceCredits: number;
  status: string;
}

export const createBookingPackSchema = z.object({
  code: z.string().trim().min(2).max(50),
  title: z.string().trim().min(3).max(120),
  description: z.string().trim().max(1000).optional().nullable(),
  sessionCount: z.number().int().min(1),
  price: z.number().int().min(0),
});

export type CreateBookingPackInput = z.output<typeof createBookingPackSchema>;

export interface BookingCommerceMetricsSummary {
  organizationId: string | null;
  activePublicProfiles: number;
  activeServices: number;
  reservationsLast30Days: number;
  pendingReservations: number;
  confirmedReservations: number;
  paidCheckoutsLast30Days: number;
  pendingCheckouts: number;
  activePacks: number;
  activeWallets: number;
  // Conversion funnel: confirmed / total reservations (last 30 days)
  confirmationRatePct: number;
  // Payment funnel: paid checkouts / confirmed reservations (last 30 days)
  paymentRatePct: number;
  // Pending reminders ready to dispatch
  pendingReminders: number;
}

export function getMessages(locale: string) {
  return isLocale(locale)
    ? localeMessages[locale]
    : localeMessages[defaultLocale];
}

export const locales = ["es", "en", "fr", "pt"] as const;

export type Locale = (typeof locales)[number];

export const defaultLocale: Locale = "es";

export const localeLabels: Record<Locale, string> = {
  es: "Español",
  en: "English",
  fr: "Français",
  pt: "Português",
};

export function isLocale(value: string): value is Locale {
  return locales.includes(value as Locale);
}

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/content/lead-magnets.ts ---
import "server-only";

import { readFile } from "node:fs/promises";
import path from "node:path";

export type LeadMagnet = {
  slug: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  filename: string;
  contentType: string;
  body: string;
};

const leadMagnetRoot = path.join(process.cwd(), "cms", "lead-magnets");

function parseFrontmatter(source: string) {
  if (!source.startsWith("---")) {
    return { attributes: {}, body: source.trim() };
  }

  const end = source.indexOf("\n---", 3);
  if (end === -1) {
    return { attributes: {}, body: source.trim() };
  }

  const frontmatter = source.slice(3, end).trim();
  const body = source.slice(end + 4).trim();
  const attributes: Record<string, string> = {};

  for (const line of frontmatter.split("\n")) {
    const separatorIndex = line.indexOf(":");
    if (separatorIndex === -1) continue;
    const key = line.slice(0, separatorIndex).trim();
    const value = line.slice(separatorIndex + 1).trim();
    attributes[key] = value.replace(/^"(.*)"$/, "$1");
  }

  return { attributes, body };
}

export async function getLeadMagnetBySlug(slug: string) {
  try {
    const source = await readFile(
      path.join(leadMagnetRoot, `${slug}.md`),
      "utf8",
    );
    const { attributes, body } = parseFrontmatter(source);

    return {
      slug,
      title: attributes.title ?? slug,
      description: attributes.description ?? "",
      filename: attributes.filename ?? `${slug}.md`,
      contentType: attributes.contentType ?? "text/markdown; charset=utf-8",
      body,
    } satisfies LeadMagnet;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/content/blog.ts ---
import "server-only";

import { readFile, readdir } from "node:fs/promises";
import path from "node:path";

export type BlogPostSummary = {
  slug: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  excerpt: string;
  category: string;
  publishedAt: string;
  readingTime: string;
  locale: string;
  ogImage: string;
  campaignKey: string;
  leadTags: string[];
  subscriptionTitle: string;
  subscriptionBody: string;
  subscriptionButtonLabel: string;
  ctaTitle: string;
  ctaBody: string;
  ctaButtonLabel: string;
  whatsappShareText: string;
  leadMagnetSlug: string | null;
  leadMagnetLabel: string | null;
};

export type BlogContentBlock =
  | { type: "heading"; level: 2 | 3; text: string }
  | { type: "paragraph"; text: string }
  | { type: "list"; items: string[] };

export type BlogPost = BlogPostSummary & {
  body: string;
  blocks: BlogContentBlock[];
};

const blogRoot = path.join(process.cwd(), "cms", "blog");

function parseFrontmatter(source: string) {
  if (!source.startsWith("---")) {
    return { attributes: {}, body: source.trim() };
  }

  const end = source.indexOf("\n---", 3);
  if (end === -1) {
    return { attributes: {}, body: source.trim() };
  }

  const frontmatter = source.slice(3, end).trim();
  const body = source.slice(end + 4).trim();
  const attributes: Record<string, string> = {};

  for (const line of frontmatter.split("\n")) {
    const separatorIndex = line.indexOf(":");
    if (separatorIndex === -1) continue;
    const key = line.slice(0, separatorIndex).trim();
    const value = line.slice(separatorIndex + 1).trim();
    attributes[key] = value.replace(/^"(.*)"$/, "$1");
  }

  return { attributes, body };
}

function parseCsv(value: string | undefined) {
  if (!value) {
    return [];
  }

  return value
    .split(",")
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function parseMarkdownBlocks(markdown: string): BlogContentBlock[] {
  const chunks = markdown
    .split(/\n{2,}/)
    .map((chunk) => chunk.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);

  return chunks.map((chunk) => {
    if (chunk.startsWith("## ")) {
      return {
        type: "heading",
        level: 2 as const,
        text: chunk.slice(3).trim(),
      };
    }

    if (chunk.startsWith("### ")) {
      return {
        type: "heading",
        level: 3 as const,
        text: chunk.slice(4).trim(),
      };
    }

    const lines = chunk
      .split("\n")
      .map((line) => line.trim())
      .filter(Boolean);
    if (lines.every((line) => line.startsWith("- "))) {
      return {
        type: "list",
        items: lines.map((line) => line.slice(2).trim()),
      };
    }

    return {
      type: "paragraph",
      text: lines.join(" "),
    };
  });
}

function normalizeSummary(
  slug: string,
  attributes: Record<string, string>,
  body: string,
): BlogPostSummary {
  const publishedAt =
    attributes.date ?? attributes.publishedAt ?? new Date().toISOString();
  const leadTags = parseCsv(attributes.leadTags);

  return {
    slug,
    title: attributes.title ?? slug,
    description: attributes.description ?? "",
    excerpt: attributes.excerpt ?? body.slice(0, 180),
    category: attributes.category ?? "Blog",
    publishedAt,
    readingTime: attributes.readingTime ?? "5 min",
    locale: attributes.locale ?? "es",
    ogImage: attributes.ogImage ?? "/og/syncrond-blog-default.png",
    campaignKey: attributes.campaignKey ?? "blog-newsletter",
    leadTags: leadTags.length > 0 ? leadTags : ["blog"],
    subscriptionTitle:
      attributes.subscriptionTitle ??
      "Recibe contenidos útiles para tu institución",
    subscriptionBody:
      attributes.subscriptionBody ??
      "Suscríbete al boletín de TEA Connect para recibir guías sobre Ley TEA, DEC y trabajo coordinado con equipos PIE.",
    subscriptionButtonLabel:
      attributes.subscriptionButtonLabel ?? "Unirme al boletín",
    ctaTitle: attributes.ctaTitle ?? "Convierte este contenido en una acción",
    ctaBody:
      attributes.ctaBody ??
      "Si este tema te toca directamente, déjanos tu correo y te enviaremos el siguiente material aplicable.",
    ctaButtonLabel: attributes.ctaButtonLabel ?? "Seguir recibiendo recursos",
    whatsappShareText:
      attributes.whatsappShareText ??
      `${attributes.title ?? slug}\n${attributes.description ?? ""}`.trim(),
    leadMagnetSlug: attributes.leadMagnetSlug ?? null,
    leadMagnetLabel: attributes.leadMagnetLabel ?? null,
  };
}

export async function listBlogPosts(locale: string) {
  const entries = await readdir(blogRoot);
  const posts = await Promise.all(
    entries
      .filter((entry) => entry.endsWith(".md"))
      .map(async (entry) => {
        const source = await readFile(path.join(blogRoot, entry), "utf8");
        const { attributes, body } = parseFrontmatter(source);
        return normalizeSummary(entry.replace(/\.md$/, ""), attributes, body);
      }),
  );

  return posts
    .filter((post) => post.locale === locale || post.locale === "es")
    .sort((left, right) => right.publishedAt.localeCompare(left.publishedAt));
}

export async function getBlogPostBySlug(locale: string, slug: string) {
  const preferredFiles = [`${slug}.${locale}.md`, `${slug}.md`];

  for (const file of preferredFiles) {
    try {
      const source = await readFile(path.join(blogRoot, file), "utf8");
      const { attributes, body } = parseFrontmatter(source);
      const summary = normalizeSummary(slug, attributes, body);

      return {
        ...summary,
        body,
        blocks: parseMarkdownBlocks(body),
      } satisfies BlogPost;
    } catch {
      continue;
    }
  }

  return null;
}

  "sent",
  "failed",

  templateKey: z.string().min(3).max(120),

});

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/workspaces.ts ---
export type WorkspaceKey =
  | "school"
  | "organization"
  | "professional"
  | "platform"
  | "family";

function isFamilyRole(role: string | null | undefined) {
  return role === "parent" || role === "guardian";
}

export function resolveWorkspaceKeyForRole(
  role: string | null | undefined,
): WorkspaceKey {
  switch (role) {
    case "platform_admin":
      return "platform";
    case "professional":
      return "professional";
    case "organization_admin":
    case "school_admin":
      return "organization";
    case "teacher":
      return "school";
    case "parent":
    case "guardian":
      return "family";
    default:
      return "school";
  }
}

export function buildWorkspaceHref(locale: string, key: WorkspaceKey) {
  return `/${locale}/workspace/${key}`;
}

export function canAccessWorkspace(
  role: string | null | undefined,
  key: WorkspaceKey,
) {
  if (!role) {
    return false;
  }

  switch (key) {
    case "platform":
      return role === "platform_admin";
    case "professional":
      return role === "professional";
    case "organization":
      return role === "organization_admin" || role === "school_admin";
    case "school":
      return role === "teacher";
    case "family":
      return isFamilyRole(role);
    default:
      return false;
  }
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/api/http.ts ---
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
import type { ZodSchema } from "zod";

export async function parseJsonBody<T>(
  request: Request,
  schema: ZodSchema<T>,
): Promise<
  { success: true; data: T } | { success: false; response: NextResponse }
> {
  let body: unknown;

  try {
    body = await request.json();
  } catch {
    return {
      success: false,
      response: NextResponse.json(
        {
          ok: false,
          error: "invalid_json",
          message: "The request body must be valid JSON.",
        },
        { status: 400 },
      ),
    };
  }

  const parsed = schema.safeParse(body);

  if (!parsed.success) {
    return {
      success: false,
      response: NextResponse.json(
        {
          ok: false,
          error: "validation_error",
          message: "The request body is invalid.",
          issues: parsed.error.flatten(),
        },
        { status: 400 },
      ),
    };
  }

  return { success: true, data: parsed.data };
}

export function conflictResponse(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    {
      ok: false,
      error: "conflict",
      message,
    },
    { status: 409 },
  );
}

export function badRequestResponse(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    {
      ok: false,
      error: "bad_request",
      message,
    },
    { status: 400 },
  );
}

export function unauthorizedResponse(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    {
      ok: false,
      error: "unauthorized",
      message,
    },
    { status: 401 },
  );
}

export function forbiddenResponse(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    {
      ok: false,
      error: "forbidden",
      message,
    },
    { status: 403 },
  );
}

export function runtimeAuthErrorResponse(error: Error & { code: string }) {
  if (error.code === "AUTH_CONTEXT_REQUIRED") {
    return unauthorizedResponse(error.message);
  }
  return forbiddenResponse(error.message);
}

export function runtimeAuthErrorStatus(
  error: Error & { code: string },
): 401 | 403 {
  return error.code === "AUTH_CONTEXT_REQUIRED" ? 401 : 403;
}

export function internalErrorResponse(message: string) {
  return NextResponse.json(
    {
      ok: false,
      error: "internal_error",
      message,
    },
    { status: 500 },
  );
}

export function isDatabaseError(
  error: unknown,
): error is { code: string; detail?: string; message: string } {
  return Boolean(
    error &&
    typeof error === "object" &&
    "code" in error &&
    typeof (error as { code?: unknown }).code === "string",
  );
}

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/seo/public-metadata.ts ---
import type { Metadata } from "next";
import { env } from "@/src/lib/config/env";
import { defaultLocale, locales, type Locale } from "@/src/lib/i18n/config";

type PublicOrigin = "site" | "app";

function resolveConfiguredOrigin(input: string, fallback: string) {
  try {
    return new URL(input).origin;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function resolveSiteOrigin() {
  return resolveConfiguredOrigin(
    env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL,
    "https://syncrond.cl",
  );
}

function resolveAppOrigin() {
  return resolveConfiguredOrigin(
    env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL,
    "https://tea.syncrond.cl",
  );
}

function resolveOrigin(origin: PublicOrigin) {
  return origin === "app" ? resolveAppOrigin() : resolveSiteOrigin();
}

function normalizePath(pathname: string) {
  if (!pathname.startsWith("/")) {
    return `/${pathname}`;
  }

  return pathname;
}

export function buildAppPath(pathname: string) {
  return normalizePath(pathname);
}

export function buildPublicUrl(
  pathname: string,
  origin: PublicOrigin = "site",
) {
  return `${resolveOrigin(origin)}${normalizePath(pathname)}`;
}

export function buildLocaleAlternates(
  pathnameByLocale: Record<Locale, string>,
  origin: PublicOrigin = "site",
) {
  return Object.fromEntries(
    locales.map((locale) => [
      locale,
      buildPublicUrl(pathnameByLocale[locale], origin),
    ]),
  );
}

type PublicMetadataInput = {
  locale: Locale;
  pathname: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  keywords?: string[];
  noIndex?: boolean;
  origin?: PublicOrigin;
};

function localizePathname(pathname: string, locale: Locale) {
  const normalized = normalizePath(pathname);
  const segments = normalized.split("/").filter(Boolean);

  if (segments.length === 0) {
    return `/${locale}`;
  }

  if (locales.includes(segments[0] as Locale)) {
    segments[0] = locale;
    return `/${segments.join("/")}`;
  }

  return `/${locale}${normalized === "/" ? "" : normalized}`;
}

export function buildPublicMetadata(input: PublicMetadataInput): Metadata {
  const origin = input.origin ?? "site";
  const canonical = buildPublicUrl(input.pathname, origin);
  const alternates = buildLocaleAlternates(
    Object.fromEntries(
      locales.map((locale) => [
        locale,
        localizePathname(input.pathname, locale),
      ]),
    ) as Record<Locale, string>,
    origin,
  );

  return {
    metadataBase: new URL(resolveOrigin(origin)),
    title: input.title,
    description: input.description,
    keywords: input.keywords,
    alternates: {
      canonical,
      languages: {
        ...alternates,
        "x-default": buildPublicUrl(`/${defaultLocale}`, origin),
      },
    },
    openGraph: {
      type: "website",
      url: canonical,
      siteName: "SyncroND",
      title: input.title,
      description: input.description,
      locale: input.locale,
    },
    twitter: {
      card: "summary_large_image",
      title: input.title,
      description: input.description,
    },
    robots: input.noIndex
      ? {
          index: false,
          follow: false,
          googleBot: {
            index: false,
            follow: false,
          },
        }
      : undefined,
  };
}

import { z } from "zod";

// Local-only fallback defaults. Production and Raspberry deploys must inject
// explicit runtime values through the environment and compose files.
const LOCAL_DB_HOST = "127.0.0.1";
const LOCAL_DB_PORT = 5434;
const LOCAL_DATABASE_URL = `postgresql://tea_connect:tea_connect@${LOCAL_DB_HOST}:${LOCAL_DB_PORT}/tea_connect`;

const emptyStringToUndefined = <T extends z.ZodTypeAny>(schema: T) =>
  z.preprocess((value) => {
    if (typeof value === "string" && value.trim() === "") {
      return undefined;
    }

    return value;
  }, schema);

const optionalString = () =>
  emptyStringToUndefined(z.string().min(1).optional());
const optionalUrl = () => emptyStringToUndefined(z.string().url().optional());
const optionalPositiveInt = () =>
  emptyStringToUndefined(z.coerce.number().int().positive().optional());

const envSchema = z.object({
  NODE_ENV: z
    .enum(["development", "test", "production"])
    .default("development"),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_NAME: z.string().min(1).default("TEA Connect"),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL: z.string().url().default("https://syncrond.cl"),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL: z.string().url().default("http://localhost:3334"),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL: optionalUrl(),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_RELEASE_VERSION: optionalString(),
  DATABASE_URL: z.string().min(1).default(LOCAL_DATABASE_URL),
  DATABASE_HOST: z.string().min(1).default(LOCAL_DB_HOST),
  DATABASE_PORT: z.coerce.number().int().positive().default(LOCAL_DB_PORT),
  DATABASE_NAME: z.string().min(1).default("tea_connect"),
  DATABASE_USER: z.string().min(1).default("tea_connect"),
  DATABASE_PASSWORD: z.string().min(1).default("tea_connect"),
  REDIS_URL: optionalString(),
  MINIO_ENDPOINT: optionalString(),
  MINIO_PORT: optionalPositiveInt(),
  MINIO_CONSOLE_PORT: optionalPositiveInt(),
  MINIO_ACCESS_KEY: optionalString(),
  MINIO_SECRET_KEY: optionalString(),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY: optionalString(),
  CLERK_SECRET_KEY: optionalString(),
  CLERK_WEBHOOK_SECRET: optionalString(),
  FORCE_LOGOUT_SECRET: optionalString(),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_ENABLE_SENTRY: z.enum(["true", "false"]).default("false"),
  NEXT_PUBLIC_SENTRY_DSN: optionalString(),
  SENTRY_DSN: optionalString(),
  SENTRY_ENVIRONMENT: optionalString(),
  SENTRY_TRACES_SAMPLE_RATE: emptyStringToUndefined(
    z.coerce.number().min(0).max(1).optional(),
  ),
  SENTRY_REPLAYS_SESSION_SAMPLE_RATE: emptyStringToUndefined(
    z.coerce.number().min(0).max(1).optional(),
  ),
  SENTRY_REPLAYS_ON_ERROR_SAMPLE_RATE: emptyStringToUndefined(
    z.coerce.number().min(0).max(1).optional(),
  ),
  GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID: optionalString(),
  GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET: optionalString(),
  FLOW_ENVIRONMENT: z.enum(["sandbox", "production"]).default("sandbox"),
  FLOW_API_KEY: optionalString(),
  FLOW_SECRET_KEY: optionalString(),
  OPENAI_API_KEY: optionalString(),
  GOOGLE_GENERATIVE_AI_API_KEY: optionalString(),
  ANTHROPIC_API_KEY: optionalString(),
  REPLICATE_API_TOKEN: optionalString(),
  RESEND_API_KEY: optionalString(),
  SMTP_HOST: optionalString(),
  SMTP_PORT: optionalPositiveInt(),
  SMTP_USER: optionalString(),
  SMTP_PASSWORD: optionalString(),
  SMTP_FROM: optionalString(),
  SMTP_FROM_NAME: optionalString(),
  TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID: optionalString(),
  TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN: optionalString(),

  EXTERNAL_ALERTS_WEBHOOK_URL: optionalString(),
  UPTIME_CHECKS_PROVIDER: optionalString(),
  RELEASE_EVIDENCE_DIR: optionalString(),
  INTEROP_HTTP_DELIVERY_MODE: z.enum(["dry_run", "live"]).default("dry_run"),

  BILLING_PROVIDER_LEDGER_MODE: z.enum(["dry_run", "live"]).default("dry_run"),

import { z } from "zod";

export const workspaceActionSourceContextSchema = z.enum([
  "workspace.professional",
  "workspace.school",
  "workspace.platform",
  "workspace.family",
  "admin.console",
  "api",
]);

export type WorkspaceActionSourceContext = z.infer<
  typeof workspaceActionSourceContextSchema
>;

export const workspaceActionMetricKeySchema = z.enum([
  "clinical_note_draft",
  "coordination_follow_up",
  "evidence_report",
]);

export type WorkspaceActionMetricKey = z.infer<
  typeof workspaceActionMetricKeySchema
>;

export function describeWorkspaceActionSource(
  sourceContext: WorkspaceActionSourceContext,
) {
  switch (sourceContext) {
    case "workspace.professional":
      return "Workspace Professional";
    case "workspace.school":
      return "Workspace School";
    case "workspace.platform":
      return "Workspace Platform";
    case "workspace.family":
      return "Workspace Family";
    case "admin.console":
      return "Consola interna";
    case "api":
      return "API directa";
    default:
      return sourceContext;
  }
}

export function describeWorkspaceActionMetric(
  actionKey: WorkspaceActionMetricKey,
) {
  switch (actionKey) {
    case "clinical_note_draft":
      return "Notas draft";
    case "coordination_follow_up":
      return "Follow-ups";
    case "evidence_report":
      return "Reportes de evidencia";
    default:
      return actionKey;
  }
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/observability/logger.ts ---
type LogLevel = "debug" | "info" | "warn" | "error";

type LogFields = Record<string, unknown>;

const SENSITIVE_KEY_PATTERN =
  /(email|full_?name|first_?name|last_?name|phone|token|secret|password|authorization|signature|prompt|transcript|payload|body|content|diagnosis|rut)/i;
const EMAIL_PATTERN = /\b[A-Z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,}\b/gi;
const RUT_PATTERN = /\b\d{1,2}\.?\d{3}\.?\d{3}-[\dkK]\b/g;

function cleanFields(fields: LogFields) {
  return Object.fromEntries(
    Object.entries(fields).filter(([, value]) => value !== undefined),
  );
}

function redactString(value: string) {
  return value
    .replaceAll(EMAIL_PATTERN, "[redacted:email]")
    .replaceAll(RUT_PATTERN, "[redacted:rut]");
}

function sanitizeError(error: Error & { code?: string; status?: number }) {
  return {
    name: error.name,
    message: redactString(error.message),
    code: error.code,
    status: error.status,
  };
}

function sanitizeValue(value: unknown, key?: string): unknown {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) {
    return value;
  }

  if (value instanceof Error) {
    return sanitizeError(value as Error & { code?: string; status?: number });
  }

  if (typeof value === "string") {
    if (key && SENSITIVE_KEY_PATTERN.test(key)) {
      return "[redacted:sensitive-field]";
    }

    return redactString(value);
  }

  if (typeof value === "number" || typeof value === "boolean") {
    return value;
  }

  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((item) => sanitizeValue(item, key));
  }

  if (typeof value === "object") {
    return Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(value).map(([entryKey, entryValue]) => [
        entryKey,
        sanitizeValue(entryValue, entryKey),
      ]),
    );
  }

  return String(value);
}

export function logEvent(level: LogLevel, event: string, fields: LogFields) {
  const sanitizedFields = sanitizeValue(cleanFields(fields)) as Record<
    string,
    unknown
  >;
  const payload = {
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    level,
    event,
    ...sanitizedFields,
  };

  const line = JSON.stringify(payload);

  switch (level) {
    case "debug":
    case "info":
      console.log(line);
      break;
    case "warn":
      console.warn(line);
      break;
    case "error":
      console.error(line);
      break;
  }
}

function normalizeOptionalString(value: string | undefined) {
  const normalized = value?.trim();
  return normalized ? normalized : undefined;
}

function normalizeSampleRate(value: number | undefined, fallback: number) {
  if (typeof value !== "number" || Number.isNaN(value)) {
    return fallback;
  }

  return Math.min(1, Math.max(0, value));
}

  return normalizeOptionalString(
    process.env.SENTRY_DSN ?? process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SENTRY_DSN,
  );
}

}

    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_ENABLE_SENTRY === "true" && Boolean(getSentryDsn())
  );
}

    normalizeOptionalString(process.env.SENTRY_ENVIRONMENT) ??
    normalizeOptionalString(process.env.NODE_ENV) ??
    "development"
  );
}

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/observability/metrics.ts ---
type LabelValue = string | number | boolean;

type MetricKind = "counter" | "gauge";

type MetricSample = {
  kind: MetricKind;
  name: string;
  help: string;
  labels: Record<string, LabelValue>;
  value: number;
};

type HttpMetricInput = {
  method: string;
  route: string;
  status: number;
  latencyMs: number;
  domain?: string | null;
  surface?: string | null;
};

type MetricsStore = {
  samples: Map<string, MetricSample>;
  setGauge: (
    name: string,
    help: string,
    value: number,
    labels?: Record<string, LabelValue>,
  ) => void;
  increment: (
    name: string,
    help: string,
    labels?: Record<string, LabelValue>,
    amount?: number,
  ) => void;
};

declare global {
  // eslint-disable-next-line no-var
  var __teaMetricsStore: MetricsStore | undefined;
}

function normalizeLabels(labels: Record<string, LabelValue>) {
  return Object.keys(labels)
    .sort()
    .map((key) => `${key}=${String(labels[key])}`)
    .join(",");
}

function createStore(): MetricsStore {
  const samples = new Map<string, MetricSample>();

  return {
    samples,
    setGauge(name, help, value, labels = {}) {
      samples.set(`${name}|${normalizeLabels(labels)}`, {
        kind: "gauge",
        name,
        help,
        labels,
        value,
      });
    },
    increment(name, help, labels = {}, amount = 1) {
      const key = `${name}|${normalizeLabels(labels)}`;
      const existing = samples.get(key);

      samples.set(key, {
        kind: "counter",
        name,
        help,
        labels,
        value: (existing?.value ?? 0) + amount,
      });
    },
  };
}

function getStore() {
  if (!globalThis.__teaMetricsStore) {
    globalThis.__teaMetricsStore = createStore();
  }

  return globalThis.__teaMetricsStore;
}

function escapeLabel(value: LabelValue) {
  return String(value).replace(/\\/g, "\\\\").replace(/"/g, '\\"');
}

function formatLabels(labels: Record<string, LabelValue>) {
  const entries = Object.entries(labels);
  if (!entries.length) {
    return "";
  }

  return `{${entries
    .sort(([a], [b]) => a.localeCompare(b))
    .map(([key, value]) => `${key}="${escapeLabel(value)}"`)
    .join(",")}}`;
}

export function recordHttpRequestMetric(input: HttpMetricInput) {
  const store = getStore();
  const labels = {
    method: input.method.toUpperCase(),
    route: input.route,
    status: String(input.status),
    status_class: `${Math.floor(input.status / 100)}xx`,
    domain: input.domain ?? "tea-connect",
    surface: input.surface ?? "unknown",
  };

  store.increment(
    "http_requests_total",
    "Total HTTP requests observed by the runtime.",
    labels,
  );
  store.increment(
    "http_request_duration_ms_sum",
    "Total accumulated HTTP request duration in milliseconds.",
    labels,
    input.latencyMs,
  );
  store.increment(
    "http_request_duration_ms_count",
    "Total number of HTTP request duration samples.",
    labels,
  );

  if (input.status >= 500) {
    store.increment(
      "http_5xx_total",
      "Total HTTP 5xx responses observed by the runtime.",
      labels,
    );
  }

  if (input.status === 403) {
    store.increment(
      "auth_forbidden_total",
      "Total forbidden responses observed by the runtime.",
      labels,
    );
  }
}

export function setMetricGauge(
  name: string,
  help: string,
  value: number,
  labels?: Record<string, LabelValue>,
) {
  getStore().setGauge(name, help, value, labels);
}

export function getHttpMetricsSummary(): {
  totalRequests: number;
  total5xx: number;
  total4xx: number;
  avgLatencyMs: number | null;
} {
  const { samples } = getStore();
  let totalRequests = 0;
  let total5xx = 0;
  let total4xx = 0;
  let durationSum = 0;
  let durationCount = 0;

  for (const sample of samples.values()) {
    if (sample.name === "http_requests_total") {
      totalRequests += sample.value;
      const statusClass = String(sample.labels["status_class"] ?? "");
      if (statusClass === "4xx") total4xx += sample.value;
    } else if (sample.name === "http_5xx_total") {
      total5xx += sample.value;
    } else if (sample.name === "http_request_duration_ms_sum") {
      durationSum += sample.value;
    } else if (sample.name === "http_request_duration_ms_count") {
      durationCount += sample.value;
    }
  }

  return {
    totalRequests,
    total5xx,
    total4xx,
    avgLatencyMs:
      durationCount > 0 ? Math.round(durationSum / durationCount) : null,
  };
}

export function renderPrometheusMetrics() {
  const { samples } = getStore();

  return Array.from(samples.values())
    .sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
    .map(
      (sample) =>
        `# HELP ${sample.name} ${sample.help}\n# TYPE ${sample.name} ${sample.kind}\n${sample.name}${formatLabels(sample.labels)} ${sample.value}`,
    )
    .join("\n");
}

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/secret-refs.ts ---
export type SecretRefStatus = "ready" | "missing" | "inline" | "not_required";

export interface SecretRefResolution {
  ref: string | null;
  status: SecretRefStatus;
  source: "none" | "env" | "inline";
  envKey: string | null;
  value: string | null;
}

function normalizeRef(ref: string | null | undefined) {
  if (!ref) {
    return null;
  }

  const trimmed = ref.trim();
  return trimmed.length > 0 ? trimmed : null;
}

function secretPathToEnvKey(ref: string) {
  const normalized = ref
    .replace(/^secrets\//, "")
    .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]+/g, "_")
    .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, "")
    .toUpperCase();

  return normalized.length > 0 ? `TEA_SECRET_${normalized}` : null;
}

function getEnvValue(envKey: string | null) {
  if (!envKey) {
    return null;
  }

  const value = process.env[envKey];
  if (typeof value !== "string") {
    return null;
  }

  const trimmed = value.trim();
  return trimmed.length > 0 ? trimmed : null;
}

export function resolveSecretRef(
  ref: string | null | undefined,
): SecretRefResolution {
  const normalized = normalizeRef(ref);

  if (!normalized) {
    return {
      ref: null,
      status: "not_required",
      source: "none",
      envKey: null,
      value: null,
    };
  }

  if (normalized.startsWith("env:")) {
    const envKey = normalizeRef(normalized.slice(4));
    const value = getEnvValue(envKey);

    return {
      ref: normalized,
      status: value ? "ready" : "missing",
      source: "env",
      envKey,
      value,
    };
  }

  if (normalized.startsWith("secrets/")) {
    const envKey = secretPathToEnvKey(normalized);
    const value = getEnvValue(envKey);

    return {
      ref: normalized,
      status: value ? "ready" : "missing",
      source: "env",
      envKey,
      value,
    };
  }

  if (/^[A-Z0-9_]+$/.test(normalized)) {
    const value = getEnvValue(normalized);

    return {
      ref: normalized,
      status: value ? "ready" : "missing",
      source: "env",
      envKey: normalized,
      value,
    };
  }

  return {
    ref: normalized,
    status: "inline",
    source: "inline",
    envKey: null,
    value: normalized,
  };
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/simple-pdf.ts ---
function escapePdfText(text: string) {
  return text
    .replace(/\\/g, "\\\\")
    .replace(/\(/g, "\\(")
    .replace(/\)/g, "\\)");
}

function normalizeText(input: string) {
  return input
    .replace(/\r\n/g, "\n")
    .replace(/\t/g, "  ")
    .replace(/[^\x20-\x7E\xA0-\xFF]/g, " ");
}

function wrapLine(line: string, maxChars: number) {
  const normalized = normalizeText(line);

  if (normalized.length <= maxChars) {
    return [normalized];
  }

  const words = normalized.split(/\s+/);
  const chunks: string[] = [];
  let current = "";

  for (const word of words) {
    if (!current) {
      current = word;
      continue;
    }

    if ((current + " " + word).length <= maxChars) {
      current += " " + word;
      continue;
    }

    chunks.push(current);
    current = word;
  }

  if (current) {
    chunks.push(current);
  }

  return chunks;
}

function buildTextLines(
  metadata: Array<[string, string | null | undefined]>,
  body: string,
) {
  const lines: string[] = [];

  for (const [label, value] of metadata) {
    lines.push(`${label}: ${value && value.trim() ? value : "—"}`);
  }

  lines.push("");

  for (const sourceLine of body.replace(/\r\n/g, "\n").split("\n")) {
    if (!sourceLine.trim()) {
      lines.push("");
      continue;
    }

    lines.push(...wrapLine(sourceLine, 92));
  }

  return lines;
}

function paginate(
  lines: string[],
  firstPageCapacity = 44,
  nextPageCapacity = 48,
) {
  const pages: string[][] = [];
  let cursor = 0;

  while (cursor < lines.length) {
    const capacity = pages.length === 0 ? firstPageCapacity : nextPageCapacity;
    pages.push(lines.slice(cursor, cursor + capacity));
    cursor += capacity;
  }

  return pages.length > 0 ? pages : [[]];
}

function createPdfObjectBuffer(content: string) {
  return Buffer.from(content, "latin1");
}

export function createSimplePdfDocument(args: {
  title: string;
  metadata: Array<[string, string | null | undefined]>;
  body: string;
}) {
  const title = normalizeText(args.title || "Document");
  const lines = buildTextLines(args.metadata, args.body);
  const pages = paginate(lines);

  const objects: Buffer[] = [];
  const pageObjectIds: number[] = [];
  const contentObjectIds: number[] = [];
  const fontObjectId = 3;

  for (let index = 0; index < pages.length; index += 1) {
    pageObjectIds.push(4 + index * 2);
    contentObjectIds.push(5 + index * 2);
  }

  objects[1] = createPdfObjectBuffer("<< /Type /Catalog /Pages 2 0 R >>");
  objects[2] = createPdfObjectBuffer(
    `<< /Type /Pages /Kids [${pageObjectIds.map((id) => `${id} 0 R`).join(" ")}] /Count ${pageObjectIds.length} >>`,
  );
  objects[3] = createPdfObjectBuffer(
    "<< /Type /Font /Subtype /Type1 /BaseFont /Helvetica >>",
  );

  pages.forEach((pageLines, index) => {
    const commands: string[] = [
      "BT",
      "/F1 18 Tf",
      "50 770 Td",
      `(${escapePdfText(title)}) Tj`,
      "/F1 11 Tf",
      "0 -22 Td",
      "14 TL",
      `(${escapePdfText(`Page ${index + 1} of ${pages.length}`)}) Tj`,
      "T*",
    ];

    for (const line of pageLines) {
      commands.push(`(${escapePdfText(line)}) Tj`);
      commands.push("T*");
    }

    commands.push("ET");

    const stream = commands.join("\n");
    const streamBuffer = createPdfObjectBuffer(stream);

    const pageObjectId = pageObjectIds[index];
    const contentObjectId = contentObjectIds[index];

    objects[pageObjectId] = createPdfObjectBuffer(
      `<< /Type /Page /Parent 2 0 R /MediaBox [0 0 612 792] /Resources << /Font << /F1 ${fontObjectId} 0 R >> >> /Contents ${contentObjectId} 0 R >>`,
    );
    objects[contentObjectId] = Buffer.concat([
      createPdfObjectBuffer(`<< /Length ${streamBuffer.length} >>\nstream\n`),
      streamBuffer,
      createPdfObjectBuffer("\nendstream"),
    ]);
  });

  const buffers: Buffer[] = [createPdfObjectBuffer("%PDF-1.4\n")];
  const offsets: number[] = [0];

  for (let id = 1; id < objects.length; id += 1) {
    const objectBody = objects[id];
    if (!objectBody) {
      continue;
    }

    offsets[id] = Buffer.concat(buffers).length;
    buffers.push(createPdfObjectBuffer(`${id} 0 obj\n`));
    buffers.push(objectBody);
    buffers.push(createPdfObjectBuffer("\nendobj\n"));
  }

  const xrefOffset = Buffer.concat(buffers).length;
  const objectCount = objects.length;

  let xref = `xref\n0 ${objectCount}\n0000000000 65535 f \n`;

  for (let id = 1; id < objectCount; id += 1) {
    const offset = offsets[id] ?? 0;
    xref += `${String(offset).padStart(10, "0")} 00000 n \n`;
  }

  buffers.push(createPdfObjectBuffer(xref));
  buffers.push(
    createPdfObjectBuffer(
      `trailer\n<< /Size ${objectCount} /Root 1 0 R >>\nstartxref\n${xrefOffset}\n%%EOF`,
    ),
  );

  return Buffer.concat(buffers);
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/request-origin.ts ---
import "server-only";
import { env } from "@/src/lib/config/env";

function firstHeaderValue(value: string | null) {
  return value?.split(",")[0]?.trim() || null;
}

function isPrivateHostname(hostname: string) {
  const normalized = hostname.trim().toLowerCase();

  if (
    normalized === "localhost" ||
    normalized === "0.0.0.0" ||
    normalized === "::1" ||
    normalized.endsWith(".local")
  ) {
    return true;
  }

  if (normalized.startsWith("127.")) {
    return true;
  }

  if (normalized.startsWith("10.") || normalized.startsWith("192.168.")) {
    return true;
  }

  const private172Match = normalized.match(/^172\.(\d{1,3})\./);
  if (private172Match) {
    const segment = Number(private172Match[1]);
    if (segment >= 16 && segment <= 31) {
      return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function normalizeOrigin(origin: string | null) {
  if (!origin) {
    return null;
  }

  try {
    return new URL(origin).origin;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

function normalizeReferrerOrigin(referrer: string | null) {
  if (!referrer) {
    return null;
  }

  try {
    return new URL(referrer).origin;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

function buildOrigin(protocol: string, host: string) {
  return normalizeOrigin(`${protocol}://${host}`);
}

function isPublicOrigin(origin: string | null) {
  if (!origin) {
    return false;
  }

  try {
    return !isPrivateHostname(new URL(origin).hostname);
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

export function resolveExternalRequestOrigin(request: Request) {
  const requestUrl = new URL(request.url);
  const requestProtocol = requestUrl.protocol.replace(":", "");
  const forwardedProto =
    firstHeaderValue(request.headers.get("x-forwarded-proto")) ||
    requestProtocol;
  const forwardedHost = firstHeaderValue(
    request.headers.get("x-forwarded-host"),
  );
  const originHeader = normalizeOrigin(request.headers.get("origin"));
  const referrerHeader = normalizeReferrerOrigin(
    request.headers.get("referer"),
  );
  const hostHeader = firstHeaderValue(request.headers.get("host"));
  const configuredAppOrigin = normalizeOrigin(env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL);
  const directRequestOrigin =
    (hostHeader ? buildOrigin(requestProtocol, hostHeader) : null) ??
    requestUrl.origin;

  const candidates = [
    forwardedHost ? buildOrigin(forwardedProto, forwardedHost) : null,
    originHeader,
    referrerHeader,
    hostHeader ? buildOrigin(forwardedProto, hostHeader) : null,
    requestUrl.origin,
  ];

  for (const candidate of candidates) {
    if (isPublicOrigin(candidate)) {
      return candidate!;
    }
  }

  if (configuredAppOrigin) {
    if (
      isPrivateHostname(requestUrl.hostname) &&
      isPrivateHostname(new URL(directRequestOrigin).hostname)
    ) {
      return directRequestOrigin;
    }

    return configuredAppOrigin;
  }

  return directRequestOrigin;
}

export function buildExternalRequestUrl(request: Request, pathname: string) {
  return new URL(pathname, resolveExternalRequestOrigin(request));
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/request-context.ts ---
const REQUEST_ID_HEADER = "x-request-id";
const PRIVATE_RESPONSE_HEADERS = [
  "x-clerk-auth-reason",
  "x-clerk-auth-status",
  "x-clerk-auth-message",
];

function generateRequestId() {
  if (
    typeof crypto !== "undefined" &&
    typeof crypto.randomUUID === "function"
  ) {
    return crypto.randomUUID();
  }

  return `req_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10)}`;
}

export function resolveRequestId(headers?: Headers | null) {
  const requestId = headers?.get(REQUEST_ID_HEADER)?.trim();
  return requestId || generateRequestId();
}

export function ensureRequestId(headers: Headers) {
  const requestId = resolveRequestId(headers);
  headers.set(REQUEST_ID_HEADER, requestId);
  return requestId;
}

export function applyRequestIdHeader(
  response: Response,
  requestId?: string | null,
) {
  response.headers.set(REQUEST_ID_HEADER, requestId || generateRequestId());
  for (const header of PRIVATE_RESPONSE_HEADERS) {
    response.headers.delete(header);
  }
  return response;
}

export function createRequestContext(headers?: Headers | null) {
  const requestId = resolveRequestId(headers);
  const accessPurpose = headers?.get("x-tea-access-purpose")?.trim() || null;

  return {
    requestId,
    accessPurpose,
    responseHeaders: {
      [REQUEST_ID_HEADER]: requestId,
    },
  };
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/request-actor.ts ---
import "server-only";
import { auth } from "@clerk/nextjs/server";
import { headers } from "next/headers";
import { redirect } from "next/navigation";

import { INTERNAL_AUTH_HEADER } from "@/src/lib/server/auth-headers";
import {
  type SessionActor,
  getSessionActorByEmail,
  getSessionActorByExternalAuthId,
  resolveSessionActorFromHeaders,
} from "@/src/server/auth/session";
import { isClerkConfigured } from "@/src/lib/server/clerk-runtime";

export async function getRequestActorProfileId() {
  const requestHeaders = await headers();
  const explicitProfileId =
    requestHeaders.get(INTERNAL_AUTH_HEADER)?.trim() === "1"
      ? requestHeaders.get("x-tea-actor-profile-id")?.trim()
      : null;

  if (explicitProfileId) {
    return explicitProfileId;
  }

  const actor = await resolveSessionActorFromHeaders(requestHeaders);
  return actor?.profileId ?? null;
}

export async function getCurrentSessionActor(): Promise<SessionActor | null> {
  const requestHeaders = await headers();
  const existingActor = await resolveSessionActorFromHeaders(requestHeaders);
  const isPublicSurface = requestHeaders.get("x-tea-surface") === "public";

  if (existingActor) {
    return existingActor;
  }

  if (isPublicSurface) {
    return null;
  }

  if (!isClerkConfigured()) {
    return null;
  }

  const authState = await auth();

  if (!authState.userId) {
    return null;
  }

  const actorByExternalId = await getSessionActorByExternalAuthId(
    authState.userId,
  );

  if (actorByExternalId?.status === "active") {
    return actorByExternalId;
  }

  const claimBag = authState.sessionClaims as
    | Record<string, unknown>
    | null
    | undefined;
  const emailClaim =
    typeof claimBag?.email === "string"
      ? claimBag.email
      : typeof claimBag?.email_address === "string"
        ? claimBag.email_address
        : null;

  if (!emailClaim) {
    return null;
  }

  const actorByEmail = await getSessionActorByEmail(emailClaim);
  return actorByEmail?.status === "active" ? actorByEmail : null;
}

export async function requireRequestActorProfileId(
  locale: string,
  nextPath: string,
) {
  const actorProfileId = await getRequestActorProfileId();

  if (!actorProfileId) {
    redirect(`/${locale}/login?next=${encodeURIComponent(nextPath)}`);
  }

  return actorProfileId;
}

import "server-only";
import { isRuntimeAuthError } from "@/src/server/runtime-auth/service";

export async function loadAuthorizedSnapshot<T>(loader: () => Promise<T>) {
  try {
    return await loader();
  } catch (error) {
    if (isRuntimeAuthError(error)) {
      return null;
    }

    throw error;
  }
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/request-surface.ts ---
import type { NextRequest } from "next/server";
import { isLocale } from "@/src/lib/i18n/config";

const PUBLIC_LOCALE_SEGMENTS = new Set([
  "tea-connect",
  "tea-rocalian",
  "colegios",
  "blog",
  "login",
  "book",
]);

const PUBLIC_API_PATHS = new Set([
  "/api/health",
  "/api/v1/health",
  "/api/v1/health/deep",
  "/api/v1/auth/session",
  "/api/v1/auth/logout",
  "/api/v1/booking/public-slots",
  "/api/v1/booking/reservations",
]);

const PUBLIC_STATIC_PATHS = new Set(["/robots.txt", "/sitemap.xml"]);

export function normalizeHost(value: string | null) {
  return value?.split(":")[0].trim().toLowerCase() ?? "";
}

export function isPublicPathname(pathname: string) {
  const normalizedPathname =
    pathname.endsWith("/") && pathname.length > 1
      ? pathname.slice(0, -1)
      : pathname;

  if (PUBLIC_API_PATHS.has(normalizedPathname)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (PUBLIC_STATIC_PATHS.has(normalizedPathname)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (
    pathname.startsWith("/api") ||
    pathname.startsWith("/_next") ||
    pathname === "/favicon.ico" ||
    /\.[^/]+$/.test(pathname)
  ) {
    return false;
  }

  const segments = pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean);

  if (segments.length === 0) {
    return true;
  }

  const [firstSegment, secondSegment] = segments;

  if (!isLocale(firstSegment)) {
    return false;
  }

  if (!secondSegment) {
    return true;
  }

  return PUBLIC_LOCALE_SEGMENTS.has(secondSegment);
}

export function isPublicSiteRequest(request: Pick<NextRequest, "nextUrl">) {
  return isPublicPathname(request.nextUrl.pathname);
}

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/lib/server/workspace-access.ts ---
import "server-only";

import { redirect } from "next/navigation";
import {
  getCurrentSessionActor,
  requireRequestActorProfileId,
} from "@/src/lib/server/request-actor";
import {
  buildWorkspaceHref,
  canAccessWorkspace,
  resolveWorkspaceKeyForRole,
  type WorkspaceKey,
} from "@/src/lib/workspaces";

export async function requireWorkspaceActor(
  locale: string,
  nextPath: string,
  expectedWorkspace?: WorkspaceKey,
) {
  const actorProfileId = await requireRequestActorProfileId(locale, nextPath);
  const actor = await getCurrentSessionActor();

  if (!actor) {
    redirect(`/${locale}/login?next=${encodeURIComponent(nextPath)}`);
  }

  const recommendedWorkspace = resolveWorkspaceKeyForRole(actor.role);

  if (expectedWorkspace && !canAccessWorkspace(actor.role, expectedWorkspace)) {
    redirect(buildWorkspaceHref(locale, recommendedWorkspace));
  }

  return { actorProfileId, actor, recommendedWorkspace };
}

--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/proxy.ts ---
import { clerkMiddleware } from "@clerk/nextjs/server";
import {
  NextResponse,
  type NextFetchEvent,
  type NextRequest,
} from "next/server";
import { defaultLocale, isLocale, type Locale } from "@/src/lib/i18n/config";
import {
  ACTOR_PROFILE_COOKIE,
  INTERNAL_AUTH_HEADER,
  PROXY_AUTH_HEADER,
} from "@/src/lib/server/auth-headers";
import {
  applyRequestIdHeader,
  ensureRequestId,
} from "@/src/lib/server/request-context";
import { logEvent } from "@/src/lib/observability/logger";
import { recordHttpRequestMetric } from "@/src/lib/observability/metrics";
import {
  isPublicSiteRequest,
  normalizeHost,
} from "@/src/lib/server/request-surface";

const TEA_PRODUCT_HOSTS = new Set([
  "tea.syncrond.cl",
  "syncrond.cl",
  "localhost",
  "127.0.0.1",
  "::1",
]);
const clerkConfigured = Boolean(
  process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY && process.env.CLERK_SECRET_KEY,
);

function hasActorSignal(request: NextRequest) {
  return Boolean(request.cookies.get(ACTOR_PROFILE_COOKIE)?.value);
}

function isTrustedInternalOverride(request: NextRequest, host: string) {
  const internalHeader = request.headers.get(INTERNAL_AUTH_HEADER)?.trim();
  return (
    internalHeader === "1" &&
    (host === "localhost" || host === "127.0.0.1" || host === "::1")
  );
}

import { locales } from "@/src/lib/i18n/config";

function getPreferredLocale(request: NextRequest): string {
  const acceptLanguage = request.headers.get("accept-language");
  if (!acceptLanguage) return defaultLocale;

  const preferredLocales = acceptLanguage
    .split(",")
    .map((lang) => {
      const [locale] = lang.split(";");
      return locale.split("-")[0].trim().toLowerCase();
    })
    .filter((preferred) => isLocale(preferred));

  return (preferredLocales[0] as Locale) || defaultLocale;
}

async function handleRequest(request: NextRequest, userId: string | null) {
  const startedAt = Date.now();
  const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;
  const rawHost =
    request.headers.get("x-forwarded-host") ?? request.headers.get("host");
  const host = normalizeHost(rawHost);

  const forwardedHeaders = new Headers(request.headers);
  const requestId = ensureRequestId(forwardedHeaders);
  const publicSurface = isPublicSiteRequest(request);
  const trustedInternalOverride = isTrustedInternalOverride(request, host);

  for (const headerName of [
    "x-tea-actor-profile-id",
    "x-clerk-user-id",
    "x-tea-external-auth-id",
    "x-auth-user-id",
    "x-auth-email",
    INTERNAL_AUTH_HEADER,
    PROXY_AUTH_HEADER,
  ]) {
    forwardedHeaders.delete(headerName);
  }

  forwardedHeaders.set("x-tea-surface", publicSurface ? "public" : "app");
  forwardedHeaders.set("x-tea-pathname", pathname);

  if (userId) {
    forwardedHeaders.set("x-clerk-user-id", userId);
    forwardedHeaders.set(PROXY_AUTH_HEADER, "1");
  }

  if (trustedInternalOverride) {
    forwardedHeaders.set(INTERNAL_AUTH_HEADER, "1");
    const internalActorProfileId = request.headers
      .get("x-tea-actor-profile-id")
      ?.trim();
    const internalExternalAuthId = request.headers
      .get("x-tea-external-auth-id")
      ?.trim();

    if (internalActorProfileId) {
      forwardedHeaders.set("x-tea-actor-profile-id", internalActorProfileId);
    }

    if (internalExternalAuthId) {
      forwardedHeaders.set("x-tea-external-auth-id", internalExternalAuthId);
    }
  }

  function finalize(response: NextResponse) {
    const latencyMs = Date.now() - startedAt;
    const surface = publicSurface ? "public" : "app";

    recordHttpRequestMetric({
      method: request.method,
      route: pathname,
      status: response.status,
      latencyMs,
      domain: "proxy",
      surface,
    });
    logEvent("info", "middleware.request", {
      request_id: requestId,
      cf_ray: request.headers.get("cf-ray"),
      route: pathname,
      domain: "proxy",
      surface,
      actor_profile_id:
        request.cookies.get(ACTOR_PROFILE_COOKIE)?.value ??
        (trustedInternalOverride
          ? request.headers.get("x-tea-actor-profile-id")
          : null) ??
        null,
      latency_ms: latencyMs,
      result: response.status,
      auth_state: userId ? "authenticated" : "anonymous",
    });

    return applyRequestIdHeader(response, requestId);
  }

  if (
    pathname.startsWith("/api") ||
    pathname.startsWith("/trpc") ||
    pathname.startsWith("/_next") ||
    pathname === "/favicon.ico" ||
    /\.[^/]+$/.test(pathname)
  ) {
    return finalize(
      NextResponse.next({
        request: { headers: forwardedHeaders },
      }),
    );
  }

  const firstSegment = pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean)[0];

  if (firstSegment && isLocale(firstSegment)) {
    const secondSegment = pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean)[1];
    const isProtectedSegment =
      secondSegment === "admin" || secondSegment === "workspace";
    if (isProtectedSegment && !hasActorSignal(request) && !userId) {
      const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
      url.pathname = `/${firstSegment}/login`;
      url.searchParams.set("next", `${pathname}${request.nextUrl.search}`);
      logEvent("info", "middleware.auth_redirect", {
        request_id: requestId,
        route: pathname,
        domain: "proxy",
        surface: "app",
        reason: `unauthenticated_${secondSegment}_access`,
      });
      return finalize(NextResponse.redirect(url));
    }

    return finalize(
      NextResponse.next({
        request: { headers: forwardedHeaders },
      }),
    );
  }

  if (TEA_PRODUCT_HOSTS.has(host) && pathname === "/") {
    const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
    url.pathname = `/${getPreferredLocale(request)}`;
    logEvent("info", "middleware.redirect", {
      request_id: requestId,
      route: pathname,
      domain: "proxy",
      surface: "public",
      reason: "landing_locale_redirect",
      target: url.pathname,
    });
    return finalize(NextResponse.redirect(url));
  }

  const url = request.nextUrl.clone();
  url.pathname = `/${getPreferredLocale(request)}${pathname}`;
  logEvent("info", "middleware.redirect", {
    request_id: requestId,
    route: pathname,
    domain: "proxy",
    surface: "public",
    reason: "locale_fallback",
    target: url.pathname,
  });

  return finalize(NextResponse.redirect(url));
}

const noOpMiddleware = async (request: NextRequest) =>
  handleRequest(request, null);

const authMiddleware = clerkMiddleware(async (auth, request) => {
  const authState = await auth();
  return handleRequest(request, authState.userId ?? null);
});

export default async function proxy(
  request: NextRequest,
  event: NextFetchEvent,
) {
  try {
    const isHandshake = request.nextUrl.searchParams.has("__clerk_handshake");
    if (isHandshake) {
      logEvent("info", "middleware.clerk_handshake", {
        request_id: request.headers.get("x-request-id"),
        route: request.nextUrl.pathname,
        domain: "proxy",
      });
    }

    if (!clerkConfigured || (isPublicSiteRequest(request) && !isHandshake)) {
      return noOpMiddleware(request);
    }

    return await authMiddleware(request, event);
  } catch (error) {
    logEvent("error", "middleware.failure", {
      request_id: request.headers.get("x-request-id"),
      cf_ray: request.headers.get("cf-ray"),
      route: request.nextUrl.pathname,
      domain: "proxy",
      error_code: error instanceof Error ? error.name : "middleware_failure",
      error_message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
    });
    // Intentamos servir de forma anónima para evitar 500 absoluto si Clerk falla
    return noOpMiddleware(request);
  }
}

export const config = {
  matcher: [
    "/((?!_next|[^?]*\\.(?:html?|css|js(?!on)|jpe?g|webp|png|gif|svg|ttf|woff2?|ico|csv|docx?|xlsx?|zip|webmanifest)).*)",
    "/(api|trpc)(.*)",
  ],
};

export async function listOrganizations(): Promise<OrganizationSummary[]> {
  const prisma = getPrisma();

  const rows = await prisma.organizations.findMany({
    orderBy: { created_at: "desc" },
    select: {
      id: true,
      slug: true,
      legal_name: true,
      display_name: true,
      status: true,
      logo_url: true,
      created_at: true,
      _count: { select: { organization_memberships: true } },
    },
  });

  return rows.map((row) => ({
    id: row.id,
    slug: row.slug,
    legalName: row.legal_name,
    displayName: row.display_name,
    status: row.status,
    logoUrl: row.logo_url,
    memberCount: row._count.organization_memberships,
    createdAt: row.created_at.toISOString(),
  }));
}

      legal_name: true,

): Promise<OrganizationSummary> {

        display_name: input.displayName,
      }),
      ...(input.status !== undefined && {
        status: input.status as OrganizationStatus,
      }),
      ...(input.logoUrl !== undefined && { logo_url: input.logoUrl }),
      updated_at: new Date(),
    },
    select: {
      id: true,
      slug: true,
      legal_name: true,
      display_name: true,
      status: true,
      logo_url: true,
      created_at: true,
      _count: { select: { organization_memberships: true } },
    },
  });

  return {
    id: updated.id,
    slug: updated.slug,
    legalName: updated.legal_name,
    displayName: updated.display_name,
    status: updated.status,
    logoUrl: updated.logo_url,
    memberCount: updated._count.organization_memberships,
    createdAt: updated.created_at.toISOString(),
  };
}
