export async function listStudentTimeline(): Promise<StudentTimelineItem[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<StudentTimelineItem>(
    `
      select *
      from (
        select
          'student-' || scp.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          scp.organization_id as "organizationId",
          owner_org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'student-core'::text as domain,
          'student.created'::text as "eventType",
          'Student core created'::text as title,
          coalesce(scp.baseline_summary, 'Canonical student profile created.') as summary,
          null::text as "actorName",
          scp.created_at as "occurredAt"
        from student_core_profiles scp
        inner join organizations owner_org on owner_org.id = scp.organization_id

        union all

        select
          'enrollment-' || se.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          se.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'student-core'::text as domain,
          'student.enrollment.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          case se.enrollment_type
            when 'clinical' then 'Clinical enrollment recorded'
            else 'School enrollment recorded'
          end as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', coalesce(se.program_name, ''), coalesce(se.grade_level, ''), se.enrollment_status)) as summary,
          null::text as "actorName",
          coalesce(se.start_date::timestamptz, se.created_at) as "occurredAt"
        from student_enrollments se
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = se.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = se.organization_id

        union all

        select
          'family-' || fr.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          scp.organization_id as "organizationId",
          owner_org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'student-core'::text as domain,
          'student.family_relationship.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Family relationship linked'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', p.full_name, fr.relationship_type, case when fr.is_primary_guardian then 'primary guardian' else null end)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          fr.created_at as "occurredAt"
        from family_relationships fr
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = fr.student_id
        inner join organizations owner_org on owner_org.id = scp.organization_id
        inner join profiles p on p.id = fr.profile_id

        union all

        select
          'care-team-' || ctm.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          coalesce(ctm.organization_id, scp.organization_id) as "organizationId",
          coalesce(org.display_name, owner_org.display_name) as "organizationName",
          'student-core'::text as domain,
          'student.care_team.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Care team member linked'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', p.full_name, ctm.team_role, ctm.visibility_scope)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          ctm.created_at as "occurredAt"
        from care_team_members ctm
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ctm.student_id
        inner join organizations owner_org on owner_org.id = scp.organization_id
        left join organizations org on org.id = ctm.organization_id
        inner join profiles p on p.id = ctm.profile_id

        union all

        select
          'support-' || sn.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          scp.organization_id as "organizationId",
          owner_org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'student-core'::text as domain,
          'student.support_need.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Support need recorded'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', sn.category, sn.priority, sn.status, sn.description)) as summary,
          null::text as "actorName",
          sn.created_at as "occurredAt"
        from support_needs sn
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = sn.student_id
        inner join organizations owner_org on owner_org.id = scp.organization_id

        union all

        select
          'paec-' || pr.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          pr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'school-compliance'::text as domain,
          'school_compliance.paec.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'PAEC updated'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', 'status=' || pr.status, 'version=' || pr.version::text, coalesce(pr.support_summary, ''))) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          coalesce(pr.signed_at, pr.updated_at, pr.created_at) as "occurredAt"
        from paec_records pr
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = pr.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = pr.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = pr.owner_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'dec-' || dl.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          dl.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'school-compliance'::text as domain,
          'school_compliance.dec_log.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'DEC log entry recorded'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', dl.severity, dl.trigger_summary, coalesce(dl.response_summary, ''))) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          dl.occurred_at as "occurredAt"
        from dec_log_entries dl
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = dl.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = dl.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = dl.recorded_by_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'incident-' || ir.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          ir.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'school-compliance'::text as domain,
          'school_compliance.incident.reported'::text as "eventType",
          'Incident reported'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', ir.incident_type, ir.severity, ir.status, ir.summary)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          ir.occurred_at as "occurredAt"
        from incident_reports ir
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ir.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = ir.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = ir.reported_by_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'crisis-' || ce.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          ce.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'school-compliance'::text as domain,
          'school_compliance.crisis.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Crisis event recorded'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', ce.escalation_level, ce.status, ce.trigger_summary)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          ce.occurred_at as "occurredAt"
        from crisis_events ce
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ce.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = ce.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = ce.triggered_by_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'observation-' || co.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          co.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'care-coordination'::text as domain,
          'care_coordination.observation.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Shared observation recorded'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', co.source_context, co.observation_type, co.content)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          co.observed_at as "occurredAt"
        from coordination_observations co
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = co.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = co.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = co.author_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'followup-' || cf.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          cf.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'care-coordination'::text as domain,
          'care_coordination.follow_up.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Follow-up tracked'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', cf.status, cf.title, coalesce(cf.details, ''))) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          coalesce(cf.completed_at, cf.due_at, cf.created_at) as "occurredAt"
        from coordination_follow_ups cf
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cf.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = cf.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = cf.owner_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'session-' || ts.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          ts.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'clinical-core'::text as domain,
          'clinical_core.session.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Therapy session registered'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', ts.session_type, ts.modality, ts.status, coalesce(ts.summary, ''))) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          ts.started_at as "occurredAt"
        from therapy_sessions ts
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ts.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = ts.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = ts.professional_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'note-' || cn.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          cn.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'clinical-core'::text as domain,
          'clinical_core.note.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Clinical note updated'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', cn.note_type, cn.status, cn.title)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          coalesce(cn.signed_at, cn.updated_at, cn.created_at) as "occurredAt"
        from clinical_notes cn
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cn.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = cn.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = cn.author_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'report-' || cr.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          cr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'clinical-core'::text as domain,
          'clinical_core.report.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Clinical report updated'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', cr.report_type, cr.status, cr.title)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          coalesce(cr.exported_at, cr.signed_at, cr.generated_at, cr.updated_at, cr.created_at) as "occurredAt"
        from clinical_reports cr
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cr.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = cr.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = cr.author_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'appointment-' || ap.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          ap.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'scheduling'::text as domain,
          'scheduling.appointment.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Appointment scheduled'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', ap.appointment_type, ap.status, ap.channel, ap.title)) as summary,
          p.full_name as "actorName",
          ap.starts_at as "occurredAt"
        from appointments ap
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ap.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = ap.organization_id
        left join profiles p on p.id = ap.professional_profile_id

        union all

        select
          'case-review-' || scr.id::text as id,
          scp.id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          scr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          org.display_name as "organizationName",
          'student-core'::text as domain,
          'student.case_review.recorded'::text as "eventType",
          'Case review recorded'::text as title,
          trim(concat_ws(' • ', scr.review_type, scr.status, scr.title, coalesce(scr.summary, ''))) as summary,
          creator.full_name as "actorName",
          coalesce(scr.closed_at, scr.next_review_at, scr.created_at) as "occurredAt"
        from student_case_reviews scr
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = scr.student_id
        inner join organizations org on org.id = scr.organization_id
        inner join profiles creator on creator.id = scr.created_by_profile_id
      ) timeline
      order by "occurredAt" desc
      limit 80
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listStudentAuditLogs(): Promise<
  StudentAuditLogSummary[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<StudentAuditLogSummary>(
    `
      select
        aal.id,
        scp.id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
        concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        coalesce(aal.organization_id, scp.organization_id) as "organizationId",
        coalesce(org.display_name, owner_org.display_name) as "organizationName",
        actor.full_name as "actorName",
        target.full_name as "targetProfileName",
        aal.resource_type as "resourceType",
        aal.resource_id as "resourceId",
        aal.action,
        aal.purpose,
        aal.outcome,
        host(aal.ip_address) as "ipAddress",
        aal.created_at as "createdAt"
      from access_audit_logs aal
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = aal.student_id
      inner join organizations owner_org on owner_org.id = scp.organization_id
      left join organizations org on org.id = aal.organization_id
      left join profiles actor on actor.id = aal.actor_profile_id
      left join profiles target on target.id = aal.target_profile_id
      order by aal.created_at desc
      limit 80
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

async function listCareTeamProfiles(
  visibleStudentIds: string[],
  organizationScope: string[] | null,
) {
  const prisma = getPrisma();
  const where: Prisma.profilesWhereInput =
    organizationScope === null
      ? {
          status: ACTIVE_PROFILE_STATUS,
          role: {
            in: CARE_TEAM_PROFILE_ROLES,
          },
        }
      : {
          status: ACTIVE_PROFILE_STATUS,
          role: {
            in: CARE_TEAM_PROFILE_ROLES,
          },
          OR: [
            {
              organization_memberships: {
                some: { organization_id: { in: organizationScope } },
              },
            },
            {
              family_relationships: {
                some: { student_id: { in: visibleStudentIds } },
              },
            },
            {
              care_team_members: {
                some: { student_id: { in: visibleStudentIds } },
              },
            },
          ],
        };

  const rows = await prisma.profiles.findMany({
    where,
    orderBy: { full_name: "asc" },
    select: {
      id: true,
      full_name: true,
      email: true,
      role: true,
      organization_memberships: {
        where:
          organizationScope === null
            ? undefined
            : { organization_id: { in: organizationScope } },
        orderBy: { created_at: "asc" },
        take: 1,
        select: {
          organizations: {
            select: { display_name: true },
          },
        },
      },
    },
  });

  return rows.map((row) => ({
    id: row.id,
    fullName: row.full_name,
    email: row.email,
    role: row.role,
    organizationName:
      row.organization_memberships[0]?.organizations.display_name ?? null,
  }));
}

export async function createStudent(
  input: CreateStudentInput,
): Promise<StudentSummary> {
  return runInPrismaTransaction(async (tx) => {
    const created = await tx.student_core_profiles.create({
      data: {
        canonical_code: input.canonicalCode,
        organization_id: input.organizationId,
        first_name: input.firstName,
        last_name: input.lastName,
        preferred_name: input.preferredName ?? null,
        birth_date: input.birthDate ? new Date(input.birthDate) : null,
        status: input.status as ChildStatus,
        baseline_summary: input.baselineSummary ?? null,
      },
      select: { id: true },
    });

    if (input.primaryGuardianProfileId) {
      await tx.family_relationships.upsert({
        where: {
          student_id_profile_id: {
            student_id: created.id,
            profile_id: input.primaryGuardianProfileId,
          },
        },
        create: {
          student_id: created.id,
          profile_id: input.primaryGuardianProfileId,
          relationship_type: "guardian",
          is_primary_guardian: true,
          legal_guardian: true,
          emergency_contact: true,
        },
        update: {
          relationship_type: "guardian",
          is_primary_guardian: true,
          legal_guardian: true,
          emergency_contact: true,
        },
      });
    }

    if (input.schoolOrganizationId) {
      await tx.student_enrollments.upsert({
        where: {
          student_id_organization_id_enrollment_type: {
            student_id: created.id,
            organization_id: input.schoolOrganizationId,
            enrollment_type: "school",
          },
        },
        create: {
          student_id: created.id,
          organization_id: input.schoolOrganizationId,
          enrollment_type: "school",
          enrollment_status: "active",
          grade_level: input.gradeLevel ?? null,
          start_date: new Date(),
        },
        update: {
          enrollment_status: "active",
          grade_level: input.gradeLevel ?? null,
        },
      });
    }

    return getStudentSummaryById(created.id);
  });
}

export async function createStudentEnrollment(
  input: CreateStudentEnrollmentInput,
): Promise<StudentEnrollmentSummary> {
  return runInPrismaTransaction(async (tx) => {
    const snapshot = await tx.student_enrollments.upsert({
      where: {
        student_id_organization_id_enrollment_type: {
          student_id: input.studentId,
          organization_id: input.organizationId,
          enrollment_type: input.enrollmentType,
        },
      },
      create: {
        student_id: input.studentId,
        organization_id: input.organizationId,
        enrollment_type: input.enrollmentType,
        enrollment_status: input.enrollmentStatus,
        grade_level: input.gradeLevel ?? null,
        program_name: input.programName ?? null,
        start_date: input.startDate ? new Date(input.startDate) : null,
        end_date: input.endDate ? new Date(input.endDate) : null,
      },
      update: {
        enrollment_status: input.enrollmentStatus,
        grade_level: input.gradeLevel ?? null,
        program_name: input.programName ?? null,
        start_date: input.startDate ? new Date(input.startDate) : null,
        end_date: input.endDate ? new Date(input.endDate) : null,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        student_id: true,
        organization_id: true,
        enrollment_type: true,
        enrollment_status: true,
        grade_level: true,
        program_name: true,
        start_date: true,
        end_date: true,
        created_at: true,
        student_core_profiles: {
          select: {
            first_name: true,
            last_name: true,
            canonical_code: true,
          },
        },
        organizations: { select: { display_name: true } },
      },
    });

    return mapEnrollmentSummary(snapshot);
  });
}

export async function createStudentCareTeamMember(
  input: CreateStudentCareTeamMemberInput,
): Promise<StudentCareTeamMemberSummary> {
  return runInPrismaTransaction(async (tx) => {
    const snapshot = await tx.care_team_members.upsert({
      where: {
        student_id_profile_id_team_role: {
          student_id: input.studentId,
          profile_id: input.profileId,
          team_role: input.teamRole,
        },
      },
      create: {
        student_id: input.studentId,
        profile_id: input.profileId,
        organization_id: input.organizationId,
        team_role: input.teamRole,
        visibility_scope: input.visibilityScope,
        active: input.active,
      },
      update: {
        organization_id: input.organizationId,
        visibility_scope: input.visibilityScope,
        active: input.active,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        student_id: true,
        organization_id: true,
        profile_id: true,
        team_role: true,
        visibility_scope: true,
        active: true,
        created_at: true,
        student_core_profiles: {
          select: {
            first_name: true,
            last_name: true,
            canonical_code: true,
            organization_id: true,
            organizations: { select: { display_name: true } },
          },
        },
        organizations: { select: { display_name: true } },
        profiles: { select: { full_name: true, role: true } },
      },
    });

    return mapCareTeamMemberSummary(snapshot);
  });
}

export async function createStudentCaseReview(
  input: CreateStudentCaseReviewInput,
): Promise<StudentCaseReviewSummary> {
  return runInPrismaTransaction(async (tx) => {
    const snapshot = await tx.student_case_reviews.create({
      data: {
        student_id: input.studentId,
        organization_id: input.organizationId,
        created_by_profile_id: input.createdByProfileId ?? null,
        review_type: input.reviewType,
        status: input.status,
        title: input.title,
        summary: input.summary ?? "",
        decisions: input.decisions,
        next_review_at: input.nextReviewAt
          ? new Date(input.nextReviewAt)
          : null,
        closed_at: input.closedAt ? new Date(input.closedAt) : null,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        student_id: true,
        organization_id: true,
        review_type: true,
        status: true,
        title: true,
        summary: true,
        decisions: true,
        next_review_at: true,
        closed_at: true,
        created_at: true,
        student_core_profiles: {
          select: {
            first_name: true,
            last_name: true,
            canonical_code: true,
          },
        },
        organizations: { select: { display_name: true } },
        profiles: { select: { full_name: true } },
      },
    });

    return mapCaseReviewSummary(snapshot);
  });
}

export async function getStudentCoreSnapshot(options?: {
  actorProfileId?: string | null;
}): Promise<StudentCoreSnapshot> {
  const database = await checkDatabaseHealth();

  if (database.status === "down") {
    return {
      database,
      stats: {
        students: 0,
        schoolEnrollments: 0,
        familyLinks: 0,
        careTeamLinks: 0,
      },
      students: [],
      enrollments: [],
      careTeamMembers: [],
      supportNeeds: [],
      caseReviews: [],
      timeline: [],
      auditLogs: [],
      organizations: [],
      guardianProfiles: [],
      careTeamProfiles: [],
    };
  }

  const authorization = await authorizeInternalReadPermission({
    actorProfileId: options?.actorProfileId,
    permissionCodes: ["student.read"],
  });

  const [
    students,
    enrollments,
    careTeamMembers,
    supportNeeds,
    caseReviews,
    timeline,
    auditLogs,
    organizationsResult,
  ] = await Promise.all([
    listStudents(),
    listStudentEnrollments(),
    listStudentCareTeamMembers(),
    listStudentSupportNeeds(),
    listStudentCaseReviews(),
    listStudentTimeline(),
    listStudentAuditLogs(),
    getPrisma().organizations.findMany({
      orderBy: { display_name: "asc" },
      select: { id: true, display_name: true },
    }),
  ]);

  const scopedStudents = applyOrganizationScope(
    students,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const visibleStudentIds = scopedStudents.map((student) => student.id);

  const scopedEnrollments = applyOrganizationScope(
    enrollments,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  ).filter((item) => visibleStudentIds.includes(item.studentId));

  const scopedCareTeamMembers = applyOrganizationScope(
    careTeamMembers,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  ).filter((item) => visibleStudentIds.includes(item.studentId));

  const scopedSupportNeeds = applyOrganizationScope(
    supportNeeds,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  ).filter((item) => visibleStudentIds.includes(item.studentId));

  const scopedCaseReviews = applyOrganizationScope(
    caseReviews,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  ).filter((item) => visibleStudentIds.includes(item.studentId));

  const scopedTimeline = applyOrganizationScope(
    timeline,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  ).filter((item) => visibleStudentIds.includes(item.studentId));

  const scopedAuditLogs = applyOrganizationScope(
    auditLogs,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  ).filter((item) => visibleStudentIds.includes(item.studentId));

  const scopedOrganizations = applyOrganizationScope(
    organizationsResult.map((organization) => ({
      id: organization.id,
      displayName: organization.display_name,
    })),
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.id,
  );

  const scopedGuardianProfiles =
    visibleStudentIds.length === 0
      ? []
      : (
          await getPrisma().family_relationships.findMany({
            where: {
              student_id: { in: visibleStudentIds },
            },
            distinct: ["profile_id"],
            orderBy: { profiles: { full_name: "asc" } },
            select: {
              profile_id: true,
              profiles: {
                select: {
                  full_name: true,
                  email: true,
                },
              },
            },
          })
        ).map<GuardianOption>((row) => ({
          id: row.profile_id,
          fullName: row.profiles.full_name,
          email: row.profiles.email,
        }));

  const scopedCareTeamProfiles =
    visibleStudentIds.length === 0 && authorization.organizationScope !== null
      ? []
      : await listCareTeamProfiles(
          visibleStudentIds,
          authorization.organizationScope,
        );

  const scopedCounts: StudentCoreCounts = {
    students: scopedStudents.length,
    schoolEnrollments: scopedEnrollments.length,
    familyLinks:
      visibleStudentIds.length === 0
        ? 0
        : await getPrisma().family_relationships.count({
            where: { student_id: { in: visibleStudentIds } },
          }),
    careTeamLinks: scopedCareTeamMembers.filter((item) => item.active).length,
  };

  return {
    database,
    stats: scopedCounts,
    students: scopedStudents,
    enrollments: scopedEnrollments,
    careTeamMembers: scopedCareTeamMembers,
    supportNeeds: scopedSupportNeeds,
    caseReviews: scopedCaseReviews,
    timeline: scopedTimeline,
    auditLogs: scopedAuditLogs,
    organizations: scopedOrganizations,
    guardianProfiles: scopedGuardianProfiles,
    careTeamProfiles: scopedCareTeamProfiles,
  };
}

  isFlowConfigured,
  getFlow,
  postFlow,
  type FlowPaymentStatusResponse,

import type {
  BookingCommerceMetricsSummary,
  BookingServiceSummary,
  BookingPublicProfileSummary,

async function appendReservationEvent(
  client: {
    query: (
      text: string,
      params?: unknown[],
    ) => Promise<{ rows: Record<string, unknown>[] }>;
  },
  input: {
    reservationId: string;
    organizationId: string;
    eventType: string;
    payload: Record<string, unknown>;
  },
) {
  await client.query(
    `
      insert into booking_reservation_events (
        id, reservation_id, sequence, organization_id, event_type, payload
      )
      values (
        $1,
        $2,
        (
          select coalesce(max(sequence), 0) + 1
          from booking_reservation_events
          where reservation_id = $2
        ),
        $3,
        $4,
        $5
      )
    `,
    [
      crypto.randomUUID(),
      input.reservationId,
      input.organizationId,
      input.eventType,
      JSON.stringify(input.payload),
    ],
  );
}

      returning id, organization_id as "organizationId", code, title, description,
                status, modality, duration_minutes as "durationMinutes",
                created_at as "createdAt", updated_at as "updatedAt"

export async function getBookingCommerceMetrics(
  organizationId?: string | null,
): Promise<BookingCommerceMetricsSummary> {
  const scopedOrganizationId = organizationId?.trim() || null;
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<BookingCommerceMetricsSummary>(
    `
      with booking_scope as (
        select $1::uuid as organization_id
      )
      select
        (select organization_id from booking_scope) as "organizationId",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_public_profiles
          where status = 'published'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "activePublicProfiles",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_services
          where status = 'active'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "activeServices",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_reservations
          where created_at >= timezone('utc', now()) - interval '30 days'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "reservationsLast30Days",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_reservations
          where status = 'pending_confirmation'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "pendingReservations",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_reservations
          where status = 'confirmed'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "confirmedReservations",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_checkout_sessions
          where status = 'paid'
            and created_at >= timezone('utc', now()) - interval '30 days'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "paidCheckoutsLast30Days",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_checkout_sessions
          where status in ('created', 'pending')
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "pendingCheckouts",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_session_packs
          where status = 'active'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "activePacks",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_wallets
          where status = 'active'
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "activeWallets",
        (
          select count(*)::int
          from booking_reminder_deliveries
          where status = 'pending'
            and scheduled_for <= timezone('utc', now())
            and (
              (select organization_id from booking_scope) is null
              or organization_id = (select organization_id from booking_scope)
            )
        ) as "pendingReminders"
    `,
    [scopedOrganizationId],
  );

  const raw = rows[0];
  if (!raw) {
    return {
      organizationId: scopedOrganizationId,
      activePublicProfiles: 0,
      activeServices: 0,
      reservationsLast30Days: 0,
      pendingReservations: 0,
      confirmedReservations: 0,
      paidCheckoutsLast30Days: 0,
      pendingCheckouts: 0,
      activePacks: 0,
      activeWallets: 0,
      confirmationRatePct: 0,
      paymentRatePct: 0,
      pendingReminders: 0,
    };
  }

  const confirmationRatePct =
    raw.reservationsLast30Days > 0
      ? Math.round(
          (raw.confirmedReservations / raw.reservationsLast30Days) * 100,
        )
      : 0;

  const paymentRatePct =
    raw.confirmedReservations > 0
      ? Math.round(
          (raw.paidCheckoutsLast30Days / raw.confirmedReservations) * 100,
        )
      : 0;

  return { ...raw, confirmationRatePct, paymentRatePct };
}

export async function getPublicAvailableSlots(
  organizationId: string,
  serviceId: string,
): Promise<any[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<any>(
    `
      select 
        av.id,
        av.starts_at as "startsAt",
        av.ends_at as "endsAt",
        av.modality,
        av.location_label as "locationLabel",
        p.full_name as "professionalName"
      from availability_slots av
      inner join profiles p on p.id = av.professional_profile_id
      inner join booking_service_professionals bsp on bsp.profile_id = p.id
      where av.organization_id = $1
        and bsp.service_id = $2
        and av.status = 'open'
        and bsp.status = 'active'
        and av.starts_at > timezone('utc', now())
        -- Filter out slots with active reservations (unless expired > 30m)
        and not exists (
          select 1 from booking_reservations br
          where br.organization_id = av.organization_id
            and br.starts_at = av.starts_at
            and br.status in ('confirmed', 'pending_confirmation')
            and (
              br.status = 'confirmed' 
              or br.created_at > timezone('utc', now()) - interval '30 minutes'
            )
        )
      order by av.starts_at asc
      limit 50
    `,
    [organizationId, serviceId],
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function initiateBookingReservation(
  organizationId: string,
  input: CreateBookingReservationInput,
): Promise<BookingReservationSummary> {
  const reservationId = crypto.randomUUID();

  // Generating a short, random public reference (ex: TX-A1B2C)
  const shortHash = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8).toUpperCase();
  const publicReference = `TX-${shortHash}`;

  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const { rows } = await client.query(
      `
        insert into booking_reservations (
          id, organization_id, public_reference, service_id,
          customer_name, customer_email, starts_at, status
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, 'pending_confirmation')
        returning
          id, organization_id as "organizationId", public_reference as "publicReference",
          appointment_id as "appointmentId", student_id as "studentId", service_id as "serviceId",
          customer_name as "customerName", customer_email as "customerEmail",
          status, starts_at as "startsAt", created_at as "createdAt", updated_at as "updatedAt"
      `,
      [
        reservationId,
        organizationId,
        publicReference,
        input.serviceId,
        input.customerName,
        input.customerEmail,
        input.startsAt,
      ],
    );

    const reservation = rows[0];

    await appendReservationEvent(client, {
      reservationId,
      organizationId,
      eventType: "reservation_initiated",
      payload: {
        serviceId: input.serviceId,
        customerEmail: input.customerEmail,
        startsAt: input.startsAt,
      },
    });

    return reservation as BookingReservationSummary;
  });
}

export async function listBookingReservations(
  organizationId: string,
): Promise<BookingReservationSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<BookingReservationSummary>(
    `
      select
        id,
        organization_id as "organizationId",
        public_reference as "publicReference",
        appointment_id as "appointmentId",
        student_id as "studentId",
        service_id as "serviceId",
        customer_name as "customerName",
        customer_email as "customerEmail",
        status,
        starts_at as "startsAt",
        created_at as "createdAt",
        updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from booking_reservations
      where organization_id = $1
      order by starts_at asc, created_at desc
    `,

  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listBookingReservationsByStudentIds(
  studentIds: string[],
): Promise<BookingReservationSummary[]> {
  if (studentIds.length === 0) return [];

  const placeholders = studentIds.map((_, i) => `$${i + 1}`).join(", ");
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<BookingReservationSummary>(
    `
      select
        id,
        organization_id as "organizationId",
        public_reference as "publicReference",
        appointment_id as "appointmentId",
        student_id as "studentId",
        service_id as "serviceId",
        customer_name as "customerName",
        customer_email as "customerEmail",
        status,
        starts_at as "startsAt",
        created_at as "createdAt",
        updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from booking_reservations
      where student_id in (${placeholders})
        and status in ('pending_confirmation', 'confirmed')
        and starts_at >= now()
      order by starts_at asc
      limit 10
    `,
    studentIds,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function updateBookingReservation(
  organizationId: string,
  input: UpdateBookingReservationInput,
): Promise<BookingReservationSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const { rows: existingRows } =
      await client.query<BookingReservationSummary>(
        `
        select
          id,
          organization_id as "organizationId",
          public_reference as "publicReference",
          appointment_id as "appointmentId",
          student_id as "studentId",
          service_id as "serviceId",
          customer_name as "customerName",
          customer_email as "customerEmail",
          status,
          starts_at as "startsAt",
          created_at as "createdAt",
          updated_at as "updatedAt"
        from booking_reservations
        where id = $1 and organization_id = $2
        limit 1
        for update
      `,
        [input.reservationId, organizationId],
      );

    const existing = existingRows[0];
    if (!existing) {
      throw new Error("Reservation not found");
    }

    const nextStartsAt = input.startsAt ?? existing.startsAt;
    const { rows } = await client.query<BookingReservationSummary>(
      `
        update booking_reservations
        set
          status = $3,
          starts_at = $4,
          updated_at = timezone('utc', now())
        where id = $1 and organization_id = $2
        returning
          id,
          organization_id as "organizationId",
          public_reference as "publicReference",
          appointment_id as "appointmentId",
          student_id as "studentId",
          service_id as "serviceId",
          customer_name as "customerName",
          customer_email as "customerEmail",
          status,
          starts_at as "startsAt",
          created_at as "createdAt",
          updated_at as "updatedAt"
      `,
      [input.reservationId, organizationId, input.status, nextStartsAt],
    );

    const eventType =
      input.status === "cancelled"
        ? "reservation_cancelled"
        : input.status === "rescheduled"
          ? "reservation_rescheduled"
          : input.status === "confirmed"
            ? "reservation_confirmed_manually"
            : "reservation_updated";

    await appendReservationEvent(client, {
      reservationId: input.reservationId,
      organizationId,
      eventType,
      payload: {
        previousStatus: existing.status,
        nextStatus: input.status,
        previousStartsAt: existing.startsAt,
        nextStartsAt,
        note: input.note ?? null,
        source: "booking_reservations_api",
      },
    });

    return rows[0];
  });
}

export async function getOrCreateWallet(
  organizationId: string,
  customerEmail: string,
): Promise<BookingWalletSummary> {
  const { rows: existing } = await dbQuery<BookingWalletSummary>(
    `SELECT id, organization_id as "organizationId", customer_email as "customerEmail", student_id as "studentId", 
              balance_sessions as "balanceSessions", balance_credits as "balanceCredits", status
       FROM booking_wallets 
       WHERE organization_id = $1 AND customer_email = $2`,
    [organizationId, customerEmail],
  );

  if (existing.length > 0) return existing[0];

  const id = crypto.randomUUID();
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<any>(
    `INSERT INTO booking_wallets (id, organization_id, customer_email, balance_sessions, balance_credits, status)
       VALUES ($1, $2, $3, 0, 0, 'active')
       RETURNING id, organization_id as "organizationId", customer_email as "customerEmail", student_id as "studentId", 
                 balance_sessions as "balanceSessions", balance_credits as "balanceCredits", status`,
    [id, organizationId, customerEmail],
  );
  return rows[0];
}

export async function initiateCheckout(
  organizationId: string,
  reservationId: string | null,
  provider: string = "flow",
  options: {
    amount?: number;
    subscriptionPlanCode?: string;
    intent?: string;
    subject?: string;
  } = {},
): Promise<{ checkoutUrl: string; checkoutId: string }> {
  return await runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    let amount = options.amount;
    let subject = options.subject;
    let customerEmail = "";

    if (reservationId) {
      const res = await client.query(
        `SELECT b.id, b.organization_id, s.price, b.customer_email, s.display_name as service_name
           FROM booking_reservations b
           JOIN booking_services s ON s.id = b.service_id
           WHERE b.id = $1 AND b.organization_id = $2`,
        [reservationId, organizationId],
      );

      if (res.rows.length === 0) throw new Error("Reservation not found");
      const reservation = res.rows[0];
      amount = amount ?? Number(reservation.price || 0);
      subject = subject ?? `Reserva: ${reservation.service_name}`;
      customerEmail = reservation.customer_email;
    }

    if (amount === undefined) {
      throw new Error(
        "Amount is required for checkout if no reservation is provided",
      );
    }

    let providerToken = `sim-${crypto.randomUUID()}`;
    let checkoutUrl = `/checkout/${crypto.randomUUID()}`;

    // 310: Real Flow Integration
    if (provider === "flow" && isFlowConfigured()) {
      try {
        const response = await postFlow<{ url: string; token: string }>(
          "/payment/create",
          {
            apiKey: env.FLOW_API_KEY!,
            commerceOrder: reservationId
              ? `book-${reservationId.split("-")[0]}`
              : `sub-${organizationId.split("-")[0]}-${crypto.randomUUID().split("-")[0]}`,
            subject: subject ?? "Pago TEA Connect",
            currency: "CLP",
            amount: Math.round(amount),
            email: customerEmail,
            urlConfirmation: new URL(
              "/api/v1/booking/checkouts/callback",
              env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL,
            ).toString(),
            urlReturn: new URL(
              `/api/v1/booking/checkouts/callback?orgId=${organizationId}`,
              env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL,
            ).toString(),
          },
        );

        if (response.token && response.url) {
          providerToken = response.token;
          const separator = response.url.includes("?") ? "&" : "?";
          checkoutUrl = `${response.url}${separator}token=${providerToken}`;
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logEvent("warn", "booking.flow.create_session_failed", {
          organizationId,
          reservationId,
          provider,
          error,
          fallbackMode: "simulation",
        });
      }
    } else if (provider === "flow") {
      // Simulation mode for flow
      checkoutUrl = `https://workshop.flow.cl/checkout/${providerToken}`;
    }

    const checkoutId = crypto.randomUUID();
    const metadata = {
      subscriptionPlanCode: options.subscriptionPlanCode,
      intent: options.intent,
      manualAmount: options.amount !== undefined,
    };

    await client.query(
      `INSERT INTO booking_checkout_sessions (id, organization_id, reservation_id, provider_checkout_id, provider_name, amount, status, metadata)
         VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, 'pending', $7::jsonb)`,
      [
        checkoutId,
        organizationId,
        reservationId,
        providerToken,
        provider,
        amount,
        JSON.stringify(metadata),
      ],
    );

    return { checkoutUrl, checkoutId };
  });
}

export async function reconcileFlowPayment(
  organizationId: string,
  providerCheckoutId: string,
): Promise<{ paid: boolean; reservationId: string | null }> {
  return await runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    // 1. Idempotencia y bloqueo pesimista:
    // Buscamos la sesión y la bloqueamos (FOR UPDATE) hasta que termine la transacción
    const res = await client.query(
      `SELECT id, reservation_id, organization_id, amount, status, metadata
         FROM booking_checkout_sessions
         WHERE provider_checkout_id = $1 AND organization_id = $2
         FOR UPDATE`,
      [providerCheckoutId, organizationId],
    );

    if (res.rows.length === 0) return { paid: false, reservationId: null };
    const session = res.rows[0];

    // Si ya está pagada, resolvemos de inmediato sin re-procesar (Idempotencia)
    if (session.status === "paid") {
      return { paid: true, reservationId: session.reservation_id ?? null };
    }

    // 310: Billing sandbox only: before declaring Flow live, reconcile against the real
    // provider status instead of promoting the checkout optimistically.
    if (isFlowConfigured() && !providerCheckoutId.startsWith("sim-")) {
      try {
        const flowStatus = await getFlow<FlowPaymentStatusResponse>(
          "/payment/getStatus",
          {
            apiKey: env.FLOW_API_KEY!,
            token: providerCheckoutId,
          },
        );

        // Status 2 is 'paid' in Flow
        if (Number(flowStatus.status) !== 2) {
          logEvent("info", "billing.flow.status_pending", {
            organizationId,
            providerStatus: Number(flowStatus.status),
          });
          return { paid: false, reservationId: null };
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logEvent("warn", "billing.flow.status_verification_failed", {
          organizationId,
          error,
        });
        return { paid: false, reservationId: null };
      }
    }

    // 2. Actualizar la sesión de checkout
    await client.query(
      `UPDATE booking_checkout_sessions SET status = 'paid', updated_at = NOW() WHERE id = $1`,
      [session.id],
    );

    if (session.reservation_id) {
      // 3. Confirmar la reserva comercial
      await client.query(
        `UPDATE booking_reservations SET status = 'confirmed', updated_at = NOW() WHERE id = $1`,
        [session.reservation_id],
      );

      // 4. Registro inmutable de auditoría
      await appendReservationEvent(client, {
        reservationId: session.reservation_id,
        organizationId,
        eventType: "reservation_confirmed",
        payload: {
          reason: "payment_received",
          checkoutId: session.id,
          source: "flow_webhook",
        },
      });
    }

    // 5. Soporte para intenciones especiales (Suscripciones Familiares)
    const metadata = session.metadata as any;
    if (metadata?.intent === "activate_family_premium") {
      logEvent("info", "billing.premium.activating", {
        organizationId,
        checkoutId: session.id,
      });

      // A. Habilitar módulo de feature toggle
      await upsertOrganizationFeatureToggle({
        organizationId,
        moduleKey: "family_premium",
        enabled: true,
        metadata: { activatedByCheckout: session.id },
      });

      // B. Crear/Actualizar registro de suscripción en el ledger
      const now = new Date();
      const nextMonth = new Date();
      nextMonth.setDate(now.getDate() + 30);

      await createPlatformSubscription({
        organizationId,
        planCode: metadata.subscriptionPlanCode || "premium_family_standard",
        status: "active",
        billingCycle: "monthly",
        seatsIncluded: 1, // Plan familiar base
        seatsUsed: 1,
        currentPeriodStart: now.toISOString(),
        currentPeriodEnd: nextMonth.toISOString(),
        metadata: {
          lastCheckoutId: session.id,
          source: "family_checkout_v1",
        },
      });

      logEvent("info", "billing.premium.activated", {
        organizationId,
        checkoutId: session.id,
      });
    }

    return { paid: true, reservationId: session.reservation_id ?? null };
  });
}

export async function onboardReservation(
  organizationId: string,
  reservationId: string,
): Promise<string> {
  return await runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    // 1. Get reservation details
    const res = await client.query(
      `SELECT b.*, s.title as service_title, s.duration_minutes
       FROM booking_reservations b
       JOIN booking_services s ON s.id = b.service_id
       WHERE b.id = $1 AND b.organization_id = $2`,
      [reservationId, organizationId],
    );

    if (res.rows.length === 0) throw new Error("Reservation not found");
    const reservation = res.rows[0];

    // 2. Resolve or create Student Core Profile
    let studentId = reservation.student_id;
    if (!studentId) {
      const names = reservation.customer_name.split(" ");
      const firstName = names[0];
      const lastName = names.slice(1).join(" ") || "Invitado";

      const { rows: existingStudent } = await client.query(
        `SELECT id FROM student_core_profiles 
         WHERE organization_id = $1 AND first_name = $2 AND last_name = $3`,
        [organizationId, firstName, lastName],
      );

      if (existingStudent.length > 0) {
        studentId = existingStudent[0].id;
      } else {
        studentId = crypto.randomUUID();
        await client.query(
          `INSERT INTO student_core_profiles (id, organization_id, first_name, last_name, canonical_code)
           VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)`,
          [
            studentId,
            organizationId,
            firstName,
            lastName,
            `BOOK-${reservation.public_reference}`,
          ],
        );
      }
    }

    // 3. Resolve Professional
    const profRes = await client.query(
      `SELECT profile_id FROM booking_service_professionals 
       WHERE service_id = $1 AND status = 'active' LIMIT 1`,
      [reservation.service_id],
    );
    if (profRes.rows.length === 0)
      throw new Error("No active professional for this service");
    const professionalProfileId = profRes.rows[0].profile_id;

    // 4. Create Appointment
    const appointmentId = crypto.randomUUID();
    const startsAt = new Date(reservation.starts_at);
    const endsAt = new Date(
      startsAt.getTime() + reservation.duration_minutes * 60000,
    );

    await client.query(
      `INSERT INTO appointments (id, organization_id, student_id, professional_profile_id, title, starts_at, ends_at, status)
       VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, 'scheduled')`,
      [
        appointmentId,
        organizationId,
        studentId,
        professionalProfileId,
        reservation.service_title,
        startsAt,
        endsAt,
        "scheduled",
      ],
    );

    // 5. Update Reservation
    await client.query(
      `UPDATE booking_reservations SET student_id = $1, appointment_id = $2, status = 'confirmed' WHERE id = $3`,
      [studentId, appointmentId, reservationId],
    );

    // 6. Bridge Event
    await appendReservationEvent(client, {
      reservationId,
      organizationId,
      eventType: "reservation_onboarded",
      payload: { studentId, appointmentId },
    });

    return appointmentId;
  });
}

export async function scheduleReminders(
  organizationId: string,
  reservationId: string,
): Promise<void> {
  await runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const res = await client.query(
      `SELECT starts_at FROM booking_reservations WHERE id = $1`,
      [reservationId],
    );
    if (res.rows.length === 0) return;
    const startsAt = new Date(res.rows[0].starts_at);

    // 1. Confirmation (Immediate)
    await client.query(
      `INSERT INTO booking_reminder_deliveries (id, organization_id, reservation_id, reminder_type, scheduled_for, status)
       VALUES ($1, $2, $3, 'confirmation', NOW(), 'pending')`,
      [crypto.randomUUID(), organizationId, reservationId],
    );

    // 2. 24h Before
    const reminder24h = new Date(startsAt.getTime() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    if (reminder24h > new Date()) {
      await client.query(
        `INSERT INTO booking_reminder_deliveries (id, organization_id, reservation_id, reminder_type, scheduled_for, status)
             VALUES ($1, $2, $3, '24h_before', $4, 'pending')`,
        [crypto.randomUUID(), organizationId, reservationId, reminder24h],
      );
    }
  });
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Booking notification dispatch
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

interface ReminderRow {
  id: string;
  organization_id: string;
  reservation_id: string;
  reminder_type: string;
  customer_name: string;
  customer_email: string;
  service_title: string;
  starts_at: string;
}

/**
 * Reads pending booking_reminder_deliveries that are due and dispatches them.
 * Provider: local_dispatcher — logs the notification payload and marks as sent.
 * When an external email provider is configured (Twilio SendGrid, Resend, etc.)
 * this function is the single integration point to swap.
 *
 * Returns the count of processed reminders.
 */
export async function dispatchPendingBookingReminders(
  organizationId?: string | null,
): Promise<number> {
  const scopedOrgId = organizationId?.trim() || null;

  const { rows } = await dbQuery<ReminderRow>(
    `
      SELECT
        brd.id,
        brd.organization_id,
        brd.reservation_id,
        brd.reminder_type,
        br.customer_name,
        br.customer_email,
        bs.title  AS service_title,
        br.starts_at
      FROM booking_reminder_deliveries brd
      JOIN booking_reservations br ON br.id = brd.reservation_id
      JOIN booking_services     bs ON bs.id = br.service_id
      WHERE brd.status = 'pending'
        AND brd.scheduled_for <= now()
        AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR brd.organization_id = $1::uuid)
      ORDER BY brd.scheduled_for ASC
      LIMIT 50
    `,
    [scopedOrgId],
  );

  if (rows.length === 0) return 0;

  let dispatched = 0;

  for (const row of rows) {
    try {
      // Local dispatch — structured log acts as the delivery record.
      // Replace this block with real provider call (Resend, SendGrid, etc.)
      logEvent("info", "booking.reminder.dispatched", {
        reminder_id: row.id,
        organization_id: row.organization_id,
        reservation_id: row.reservation_id,
        reminder_type: row.reminder_type,
        recipient_label: row.customer_name,
        service_title: row.service_title,
        starts_at: row.starts_at,
        provider: "local_dispatcher",
      });

      await dbQuery(
        `UPDATE booking_reminder_deliveries
         SET status = 'sent', sent_at = now(), updated_at = now(),
             provider_id = 'local_' || id
         WHERE id = $1`,
        [row.id],
      );

      dispatched += 1;
    } catch (err) {
      logEvent("error", "booking.reminder.dispatch.error", {
        reminder_id: row.id,
        organization_id: row.organization_id,
        error_message: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
      });

      await dbQuery(
        `UPDATE booking_reminder_deliveries
         SET status = 'failed', updated_at = now()
         WHERE id = $1`,
        [row.id],
      ).catch(() => {});
    }
  }

  return dispatched;
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Booking funnel conversion metrics (P2-12)
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface BookingFunnelMetrics {
  organizationId: string | null;
  activeServices: number;
  availableSlots: number;
  reservationsCreatedLast30d: number;
  reservationsConfirmed: number;
  checkoutsInitiated: number;
  checkoutsPaid: number;
  /** reservation → confirmed rate, 0-1 */
  confirmationRate: number;
  /** confirmed → paid rate, 0-1 */
  paymentConversionRate: number;
}

export async function getBookingFunnelMetrics(
  organizationId?: string | null,
): Promise<BookingFunnelMetrics> {
  const scopedOrgId = organizationId?.trim() || null;

  const { rows } = await dbQuery<{
    active_services: number;
    available_slots: number;
    reservations_created: number;
    reservations_confirmed: number;
    checkouts_initiated: number;
    checkouts_paid: number;
  }>(
    `
      SELECT
        (
          SELECT count(*)::int FROM booking_services
          WHERE status = 'active'
            AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR organization_id = $1::uuid)
        ) AS active_services,
        (
          SELECT count(*)::int FROM booking_availability_slots
          WHERE starts_at > now()
            AND is_available = true
            AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR organization_id = $1::uuid)
        ) AS available_slots,
        (
          SELECT count(*)::int FROM booking_reservations
          WHERE created_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
            AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR organization_id = $1::uuid)
        ) AS reservations_created,
        (
          SELECT count(*)::int FROM booking_reservations
          WHERE status IN ('confirmed', 'onboarded')
            AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR organization_id = $1::uuid)
        ) AS reservations_confirmed,
        (
          SELECT count(*)::int FROM booking_checkout_sessions
          WHERE status != 'cancelled'
            AND created_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
            AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR organization_id = $1::uuid)
        ) AS checkouts_initiated,
        (
          SELECT count(*)::int FROM booking_checkout_sessions
          WHERE status = 'paid'
            AND created_at >= now() - interval '30 days'
            AND ($1::uuid IS NULL OR organization_id = $1::uuid)
        ) AS checkouts_paid
    `,
    [scopedOrgId],
  );

  const row = rows[0] ?? {
    active_services: 0,
    available_slots: 0,
    reservations_created: 0,
    reservations_confirmed: 0,
    checkouts_initiated: 0,
    checkouts_paid: 0,
  };

  const confirmationRate =
    row.reservations_created > 0
      ? row.reservations_confirmed / row.reservations_created
      : 0;

  const paymentConversionRate =
    row.checkouts_initiated > 0
      ? row.checkouts_paid / row.checkouts_initiated
      : 0;

  return {
    organizationId: scopedOrgId,
    activeServices: row.active_services,
    availableSlots: row.available_slots,
    reservationsCreatedLast30d: row.reservations_created,
    reservationsConfirmed: row.reservations_confirmed,
    checkoutsInitiated: row.checkouts_initiated,
    checkoutsPaid: row.checkouts_paid,
    confirmationRate: Math.round(confirmationRate * 1000) / 1000,
    paymentConversionRate: Math.round(paymentConversionRate * 1000) / 1000,
  };
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/server/ops/deep-health.ts ---
import net from "node:net";
import { URL } from "node:url";
import { env } from "@/src/lib/config/env";
import { checkDatabaseHealth } from "@/src/server/db/health";

type DependencyStatus = "up" | "down" | "unconfigured";

type DependencyHealth = {
  status: DependencyStatus;
  target: string | null;
  latencyMs: number | null;
  error: string | null;
};

const REDIS_FALLBACK_URL = "redis://redis:6379";
const MINIO_FALLBACK_HEALTH_URL = "http://minio:9000/minio/health/live";

function durationMs(startedAt: number) {
  return Math.max(Date.now() - startedAt, 0);
}

async function checkTcpTarget(target: string): Promise<DependencyHealth> {
  const startedAt = Date.now();

  try {
    const parsed = new URL(target);
    const hostname = parsed.hostname;
    const port = Number(parsed.port || 0);

    if (!hostname || !port) {
      return {
        status: "down",
        target,
        latencyMs: durationMs(startedAt),
        error: "invalid tcp target",
      };
    }

    await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
      const socket = net.createConnection({ host: hostname, port });
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
        socket.destroy();
        reject(new Error("timeout"));
      }, 5000);

      socket.on("connect", () => {
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        socket.end();
        resolve();
      });

      socket.on("error", (error) => {
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        reject(error);
      });
    });

    return {
      status: "up",
      target,
      latencyMs: durationMs(startedAt),
      error: null,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      status: "down",
      target,
      latencyMs: durationMs(startedAt),
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "tcp connectivity failed",
    };
  }
}

async function checkHttpTarget(target: string): Promise<DependencyHealth> {
  const startedAt = Date.now();

  try {
    const response = await fetch(target, {
      method: "GET",
      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000),
      cache: "no-store",
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      return {
        status: "down",
        target,
        latencyMs: durationMs(startedAt),
        error: `http ${response.status}`,
      };
    }

    return {
      status: "up",
      target,
      latencyMs: durationMs(startedAt),
      error: null,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      status: "down",
      target,
      latencyMs: durationMs(startedAt),
      error:
        error instanceof Error ? error.message : "http health check failed",
    };
  }
}

function resolveRedisTarget() {
  return env.REDIS_URL || REDIS_FALLBACK_URL;
}

function resolveMinioHealthTarget() {
  if (env.MINIO_ENDPOINT) {
    const normalizedHost = env.MINIO_ENDPOINT.replace(/^https?:\/\//, "");
    const protocol = env.MINIO_ENDPOINT.startsWith("https://")
      ? "https://"
      : "http://";
    const port = env.MINIO_PORT ?? 9010;
    return `${protocol}${normalizedHost}:${port}/minio/health/live`;
  }

  return MINIO_FALLBACK_HEALTH_URL;
}

function computeClerkReadiness() {
  if (
    env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY &&
    env.CLERK_SECRET_KEY &&
    env.CLERK_WEBHOOK_SECRET
  ) {
    return "configured";
  }

  if (
    env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY ||
    env.CLERK_SECRET_KEY ||
    env.CLERK_WEBHOOK_SECRET
  ) {
    return "partial";
  }

  return "missing";
}

export async function getDeepHealthSnapshot() {
  const database = await checkDatabaseHealth();
  const redis = await checkTcpTarget(resolveRedisTarget());
  const objectStorage = await checkHttpTarget(resolveMinioHealthTarget());
  const billingProviderMode =
    env.FLOW_API_KEY && env.FLOW_SECRET_KEY
      ? `flow:${env.FLOW_ENVIRONMENT}`
      : env.BILLING_PROVIDER_LEDGER_MODE;

  const ok =
    database.status === "up" &&
    redis.status === "up" &&
    objectStorage.status === "up";

  return {
    ok,
    runtime: {
      mode: env.NODE_ENV,
      appUrl: env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL,
    },
    services: {
      database,
      redis,
      objectStorage,
    },
    integrations: {
      clerk: computeClerkReadiness(),
      interoperabilityDeliveryMode: env.INTEROP_HTTP_DELIVERY_MODE,
      billingProviderMode,
    },
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
}
