import { dbQuery, runInTransaction } from "@/src/server/db/client";
import { checkDatabaseHealth } from "@/src/server/db/health";
import {
  applyOrganizationScope,
  authorizeInternalReadPermission,
} from "@/src/server/runtime-auth/service";
import type {
  ComplianceCaseSummary,
  ComplianceDashboardSummary,
  CreateCrisisEventInput,
  CreateDecLogInput,
  CreateEvidenceComplianceReportInput,
  CreateIncidentReportInput,
  CreatePaecInput,
  UpdatePaecInput,
  CrisisEventSummary,
  DecLogSummary,
  EvidenceComplianceReportDetail,
  EvidenceComplianceReportSummary,
  IncidentReportSummary,
  PaecSummary,
  SchoolComplianceSnapshot,
} from "@/src/lib/school-compliance/contracts";

type Queryable = {
  query: <T = unknown>(
    text: string,
    params?: unknown[],
  ) => Promise<{ rows: T[] }>;
};

type OrganizationReference = { id: string; displayName: string };
type ActorReference = { id: string; displayName: string };
type StudentReference = { id: string; displayName: string };

type EvidenceSourceItem = {
  resourceType: string;
  resourceId: string;
  title: string;
  summary: string;
  occurredAt: string | null;
  status: string | null;
};

type EvidenceBuildContext = {
  organization: { id: string; displayName: string };
  student: { id: string; canonicalCode: string; fullName: string };
  paecRecords: PaecSummary[];
  decLogs: DecLogSummary[];
  incidents: IncidentReportSummary[];
  crisisEvents: CrisisEventSummary[];
  meetingMinutes: EvidenceSourceItem[];
  signatures: EvidenceSourceItem[];
  createdByProfileName: string | null;
};

type EvidencePayloadSection = {
  title: string;
  items: EvidenceSourceItem[];
};

type EvidencePayload = {
  version: number;
  reportType: CreateEvidenceComplianceReportInput["reportType"];
  organization: { id: string; displayName: string };
  student: { id: string; canonicalCode: string; fullName: string };
  generatedAt: string;
  preparedBy: string | null;
  sections: EvidencePayloadSection[];
  export: {
    fileBase: string;
    html: string;
    markdown: string;
  };
};

type SchoolComplianceAccessPurpose =
  | "operational_console"
  | "compliance_review"
  | "family_review"
  | "general";

type SchoolComplianceSubjectRecord = {
  organizationId: string;
  studentId: string | null;
};

type ActorSchoolComplianceAccess = {
  platformAdmin: boolean;
  organizationRoleCodes: Map<string, Set<string>>;
  guardianStudentIds: Set<string>;
  schoolStudentIds: Set<string>;
};

const REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT =
  "[redacted: elevated compliance access required]";
const FULL_SCHOOL_COMPLIANCE_PURPOSES = new Set<SchoolComplianceAccessPurpose>([
  "operational_console",
  "compliance_review",
]);

async function emitOutboxEvent(
  client: Queryable,
  aggregateType: string,
  aggregateId: string,
  eventName: string,
  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
) {
  await client.query(
    `
      insert into outbox_events (
        aggregate_type,
        aggregate_id,
        event_name,
        event_version,
        payload,
        status
      )
      values ($1, $2, $3, 1, $4::jsonb, 'pending')
    `,
    [aggregateType, aggregateId, eventName, JSON.stringify(payload)],
  );
}

function escapeHtml(value: string) {
  return value
    .replaceAll("&", "&amp;")
    .replaceAll("<", "&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">", "&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"', "&quot;")
    .replaceAll("'", "&#39;");
}

function formatDateTime(value: string | null) {
  if (!value) return "not available";
  return new Date(value).toISOString();
}

function resolveSchoolComplianceAccessPurpose(
  input?: string | null,
): SchoolComplianceAccessPurpose {
  switch (input) {
    case "operational_console":
    case "compliance_review":
    case "family_review":
      return input;
    default:
      return "general";
  }
}

function truncateNarrative(text: string, maxLength = 220) {
  return text.length <= maxLength
    ? text
    : `${text.slice(0, maxLength).trimEnd()}…`;
}

function limitedComplianceNarrative(
  text: string,
  label: string,
  maxLength = 180,
) {
  return `[limited ${label}] ${truncateNarrative(text, maxLength)}`;
}

async function buildActorSchoolComplianceAccess(
  actorProfileId: string,
  organizationIds: string[],
  studentIds: string[],
): Promise<ActorSchoolComplianceAccess> {
  const organizationRoleCodes = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
  const guardianStudentIds = new Set<string>();
  const schoolStudentIds = new Set<string>();

  const [
    { rows: platformRows },
    { rows: roleRows },
    { rows: familyRows },
    { rows: careTeamRows },
  ] = await Promise.all([
    dbQuery<{ hasPlatformAdmin: boolean }>(
      `
          select exists (
            select 1
            from profile_role_assignments pra
            inner join roles r on r.id = pra.role_id and r.active = true
            where pra.profile_id = $1
              and pra.active = true
              and pra.organization_id is null
              and r.code = 'platform.super_admin'
          ) as "hasPlatformAdmin"
        `,
      [actorProfileId],
    ),
    organizationIds.length > 0
      ? dbQuery<{ organizationId: string; roleCode: string }>(
          `
              select
                pra.organization_id as "organizationId",
                r.code as "roleCode"
              from profile_role_assignments pra
              inner join roles r on r.id = pra.role_id and r.active = true
              where pra.profile_id = $1
                and pra.active = true
                and pra.organization_id = any($2::uuid[])
            `,
          [actorProfileId, organizationIds],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({
          rows: [] as Array<{ organizationId: string; roleCode: string }>,
        }),
    studentIds.length > 0
      ? dbQuery<{ studentId: string }>(
          `
              select fr.student_id as "studentId"
              from family_relationships fr
              where fr.profile_id = $1
                and fr.student_id = any($2::uuid[])
            `,
          [actorProfileId, studentIds],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({ rows: [] as Array<{ studentId: string }> }),
    studentIds.length > 0
      ? dbQuery<{ studentId: string; teamRole: string }>(
          `
              select
                ctm.student_id as "studentId",
                ctm.team_role as "teamRole"
              from care_team_members ctm
              where ctm.profile_id = $1
                and ctm.active = true
                and ctm.student_id = any($2::uuid[])
            `,
          [actorProfileId, studentIds],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({
          rows: [] as Array<{ studentId: string; teamRole: string }>,
        }),
  ]);

  for (const row of roleRows) {
    const roleCodes =
      organizationRoleCodes.get(row.organizationId) ?? new Set<string>();
    roleCodes.add(row.roleCode);
    organizationRoleCodes.set(row.organizationId, roleCodes);
  }

  for (const row of familyRows) {
    guardianStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
  }

  for (const row of careTeamRows) {
    if (row.teamRole === "guardian") {
      guardianStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
    }
    if (
      row.teamRole === "teacher" ||
      row.teamRole === "school_admin" ||
      row.teamRole === "care_coordinator"
    ) {
      schoolStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
    }
  }

  return {
    platformAdmin: Boolean(platformRows[0]?.hasPlatformAdmin),
    organizationRoleCodes,
    guardianStudentIds,
    schoolStudentIds,
  };
}

function hasSchoolComplianceRole(
  access: ActorSchoolComplianceAccess,
  organizationId: string,
) {
  const roleCodes = access.organizationRoleCodes.get(organizationId);

  return Boolean(
    roleCodes &&
    (roleCodes.has("org.owner") ||
      roleCodes.has("org.admin") ||
      roleCodes.has("school.teacher")),
  );
}

function canReadFullSchoolComplianceContent(
  access: ActorSchoolComplianceAccess,
  item: SchoolComplianceSubjectRecord,
  purpose: SchoolComplianceAccessPurpose,
) {
  if (!FULL_SCHOOL_COMPLIANCE_PURPOSES.has(purpose)) {
    return false;
  }

  return (
    access.platformAdmin ||
    hasSchoolComplianceRole(access, item.organizationId) ||
    (item.studentId !== null && access.schoolStudentIds.has(item.studentId))
  );
}

function buildEvidenceExportArtifacts(args: {
  title: string;
  reportType: string;
  organizationName: string;
  studentName: string;
  studentCode: string;
  generatedAt: string | null;
  preparedBy: string | null;
  sections: EvidencePayloadSection[];
  fileBase: string;
}) {
  const markdown = [
    `# ${args.title}`,
    "",
    `- Organization: ${args.organizationName}`,
    `- Student: ${args.studentName} (${args.studentCode})`,
    `- Report type: ${args.reportType}`,
    `- Generated at: ${args.generatedAt ?? "—"}`,
    `- Prepared by: ${args.preparedBy ?? "system"}`,
    "",
    ...args.sections.flatMap((section) => [
      `## ${section.title}`,
      ...renderSourceItemsMarkdown(section.items),
      "",
    ]),
  ].join("\n");

  const html = `<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <title>${escapeHtml(args.title)}</title>
    <style>
      body { font-family: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif; padding: 24px; color: #1f2937; }
      h1, h2 { color: #7c3f12; }
      .meta { margin-bottom: 18px; }
      .section { margin-top: 24px; }
      li { margin-bottom: 12px; }
      p { margin: 6px 0 0; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>${escapeHtml(args.title)}</h1>
    <div class="meta">
      <div><strong>Organization:</strong> ${escapeHtml(args.organizationName)}</div>
      <div><strong>Student:</strong> ${escapeHtml(args.studentName)} (${escapeHtml(args.studentCode)})</div>
      <div><strong>Report type:</strong> ${escapeHtml(args.reportType)}</div>
      <div><strong>Generated at:</strong> ${escapeHtml(args.generatedAt ?? "—")}</div>
      <div><strong>Prepared by:</strong> ${escapeHtml(args.preparedBy ?? "system")}</div>
    </div>
    ${args.sections
      .map(
        (section) =>
          `<section class="section"><h2>${escapeHtml(section.title)}</h2><ul>${renderSourceItemsHtml(section.items)}</ul></section>`,
      )
      .join("")}
  </body>
</html>`;

  return {
    fileBase: args.fileBase,
    html,
    markdown,
  };
}

function normalizeEvidencePayload(
  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
): EvidencePayload | null {
  const sections = Array.isArray(payload.sections)
    ? payload.sections.flatMap((section) => {
        if (!section || typeof section !== "object") return [];
        const record = section as Record<string, unknown>;
        if (typeof record.title !== "string" || !Array.isArray(record.items))
          return [];

        const items = record.items.flatMap((item) => {
          if (!item || typeof item !== "object") return [];
          const source = item as Record<string, unknown>;
          if (
            typeof source.resourceType !== "string" ||
            typeof source.title !== "string"
          )
            return [];

          return [
            {
              resourceType: source.resourceType,
              resourceId:
                typeof source.resourceId === "string"
                  ? source.resourceId
                  : `${source.resourceType}-redacted`,
              title: source.title,
              summary: typeof source.summary === "string" ? source.summary : "",
              occurredAt:
                typeof source.occurredAt === "string"
                  ? source.occurredAt
                  : null,
              status: typeof source.status === "string" ? source.status : null,
            } satisfies EvidenceSourceItem,
          ];
        });

        return [{ title: record.title, items }];
      })
    : null;

  const organization =
    payload.organization && typeof payload.organization === "object"
      ? (payload.organization as Record<string, unknown>)
      : null;
  const student =
    payload.student && typeof payload.student === "object"
      ? (payload.student as Record<string, unknown>)
      : null;
  const exportPayload =
    payload.export && typeof payload.export === "object"
      ? (payload.export as Record<string, unknown>)
      : null;

  if (!sections || !organization || !student || !exportPayload) {
    return null;
  }

  if (
    typeof payload.version !== "number" ||
    typeof payload.reportType !== "string" ||
    typeof organization.id !== "string" ||
    typeof organization.displayName !== "string" ||
    typeof student.id !== "string" ||
    typeof student.canonicalCode !== "string" ||
    typeof student.fullName !== "string" ||
    typeof payload.generatedAt !== "string" ||
    typeof exportPayload.fileBase !== "string" ||
    typeof exportPayload.html !== "string" ||
    typeof exportPayload.markdown !== "string"
  ) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    version: payload.version,
    reportType:
      payload.reportType as CreateEvidenceComplianceReportInput["reportType"],
    organization: {
      id: organization.id,
      displayName: organization.displayName,
    },
    student: {
      id: student.id,
      canonicalCode: student.canonicalCode,
      fullName: student.fullName,
    },
    generatedAt: payload.generatedAt,
    preparedBy:
      typeof payload.preparedBy === "string" ? payload.preparedBy : null,
    sections,
    export: {
      fileBase: exportPayload.fileBase,
      html: exportPayload.html,
      markdown: exportPayload.markdown,
    },
  };
}

function sanitizeEvidenceSourceItem(
  item: EvidenceSourceItem,
  purpose: SchoolComplianceAccessPurpose,
): EvidenceSourceItem {
  if (purpose === "family_review") {
    return {
      ...item,
      resourceId: `${item.resourceType}-family-view`,
      summary: item.summary
        ? limitedComplianceNarrative(item.summary, "evidence summary", 160)
        : "",
    };
  }

  return {
    ...item,
    resourceId: `${item.resourceType}-restricted`,
    summary: REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,
  };
}

async function withSchoolComplianceAccess<
  T extends SchoolComplianceSubjectRecord,
  TResult,
>(
  items: T[],
  actorProfileId: string | null | undefined,
  accessPurpose: string | null | undefined,
  mapper: (
    item: T,
    context: {
      canReadFullContent: boolean;
      purpose: SchoolComplianceAccessPurpose;
    },
  ) => TResult,
) {
  const purpose = resolveSchoolComplianceAccessPurpose(accessPurpose);

  if (!actorProfileId || items.length === 0) {
    return items.map((item) =>
      mapper(item, { canReadFullContent: true, purpose }),
    );
  }

  const access = await buildActorSchoolComplianceAccess(
    actorProfileId,
    [...new Set(items.map((item) => item.organizationId))],
    [
      ...new Set(
        items
          .map((item) => item.studentId)
          .filter((item): item is string => Boolean(item)),
      ),
    ],
  );

  return items.map((item) =>
    mapper(item, {
      canReadFullContent: canReadFullSchoolComplianceContent(
        access,
        item,
        purpose,
      ),
      purpose,
    }),
  );
}

export async function applySchoolComplianceAccessToPaecRecords(
  items: PaecSummary[],
  actorProfileId?: string | null,
  accessPurpose?: string | null,
) {
  return withSchoolComplianceAccess(
    items,
    actorProfileId,
    accessPurpose,
    (item, context) =>
      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            supportSummary:
              item.supportSummary === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? limitedComplianceNarrative(
                      item.supportSummary,
                      "PAEC summary",
                      180,
                    )
                  : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,
            primaryObjective:
              item.primaryObjective === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? limitedComplianceNarrative(
                      item.primaryObjective,
                      "PAEC objective",
                      120,
                    )
                  : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,
            familyCoordinationSummary:
              item.familyCoordinationSummary === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? limitedComplianceNarrative(
                      item.familyCoordinationSummary,
                      "family coordination summary",
                      140,
                    )
                  : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,
            accommodations: [],
            successIndicators: [],
          },
  );
}

      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            triggerSummary:
              context.purpose === "family_review"
                ? limitedComplianceNarrative(
                    item.triggerSummary,
                    "trigger summary",
                    140,
                  )
                : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,
            responseSummary:
              item.responseSummary === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? limitedComplianceNarrative(
                      item.responseSummary,
                      "response summary",
                      140,
                    )
                  : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,
          },
  );
}

      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            location:
              item.location === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? limitedComplianceNarrative(item.location, "location", 60)
                  : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,

              context.purpose === "family_review"
                ? limitedComplianceNarrative(

                    160,

                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"

export async function applySchoolComplianceAccessToCrisisEvents(
  items: CrisisEventSummary[],

                ? limitedComplianceNarrative(

                    "crisis trigger",

                  )
                : REDACTED_COMPLIANCE_TEXT,

              item.deescalationSummary === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? limitedComplianceNarrative(

async function applySchoolComplianceAccessToEvidenceReport(
  item: EvidenceComplianceReportDetail,
  actorProfileId?: string | null,
  accessPurpose?: string | null,
): Promise<EvidenceComplianceReportDetail> {
  const purpose = resolveSchoolComplianceAccessPurpose(accessPurpose);

  if (!actorProfileId) {
    return item;
  }

  const access = await buildActorSchoolComplianceAccess(
    actorProfileId,
    [item.organizationId],
    item.studentId ? [item.studentId] : [],
  );
  const canReadFullContent = canReadFullSchoolComplianceContent(
    access,
    { organizationId: item.organizationId, studentId: item.studentId },
    purpose,
  );

  if (canReadFullContent) {
    return item;
  }

  const payload = normalizeEvidencePayload(item.payload);
  if (!payload) {
    return {
      ...item,
      sourceRefs: [],
      payload: {
        redacted: true,
        purpose,
        reason: "elevated_compliance_access_required",
      },
    };
  }

  const redactedSections = payload.sections.map((section) => ({
    title: section.title,
    items: section.items.map((entry) =>
      sanitizeEvidenceSourceItem(entry, purpose),
    ),
  }));
  const exportArtifacts = buildEvidenceExportArtifacts({
    title: item.title,
    reportType: item.reportType,
    organizationName: item.organizationName,
    studentName: item.studentName ?? payload.student.fullName,
    studentCode: item.studentCode ?? payload.student.canonicalCode,
    generatedAt: item.generatedAt,
    preparedBy: item.createdByProfileName,
    sections: redactedSections,
    fileBase: `${payload.export.fileBase}-${purpose}`,
  });

  return {
    ...item,
    sourceRefs: redactedSections.flatMap((section) =>
      section.items.map((entry) => ({
        resourceType: entry.resourceType,
        title: entry.title,
        occurredAt: entry.occurredAt,
        status: entry.status,
        summary: entry.summary,
      })),
    ),
    payload: {
      ...payload,
      preparedBy: item.createdByProfileName,
      sections: redactedSections,
      export: exportArtifacts,
      redacted: true,
      purpose,
      reason:
        purpose === "family_review"
          ? "family_safe_view"
          : "elevated_compliance_access_required",
    },
  };
}

function renderSourceItemsMarkdown(items: EvidenceSourceItem[]) {
  if (items.length === 0) {
    return ["- No structured records available for this section."];
  }

  return items.map((item) => {
    const parts = [item.title];
    if (item.status) parts.push(`status=${item.status}`);
    if (item.occurredAt) parts.push(`at=${formatDateTime(item.occurredAt)}`);
    if (item.summary) parts.push(item.summary);
    return `- ${parts.join(" | ")}`;
  });
}

function renderSourceItemsHtml(items: EvidenceSourceItem[]) {
  if (items.length === 0) {
    return "<li>No structured records available for this section.</li>";
  }

  return items
    .map((item) => {
      const meta = [
        item.status ? `status=${item.status}` : null,
        item.occurredAt ? `at=${formatDateTime(item.occurredAt)}` : null,
      ]
        .filter(Boolean)
        .join(" | ");
      return `<li><strong>${escapeHtml(item.title)}</strong>${meta ? `<div>${escapeHtml(meta)}</div>` : ""}<p>${escapeHtml(item.summary || "")}</p></li>`;
    })
    .join("");
}

function buildEvidencePackage(
  input: CreateEvidenceComplianceReportInput,
  context: EvidenceBuildContext,
) {
  const paecItems: EvidenceSourceItem[] = context.paecRecords.map((record) => ({
    resourceType: "paec_record",
    resourceId: record.id,
    title: `${record.studentCode} PAEC`,
    summary: record.supportSummary ?? "No support summary available.",
    occurredAt: record.signedAt ?? record.createdAt,
    status: record.status,
  }));
  const decItems: EvidenceSourceItem[] = context.decLogs.map((record) => ({
    resourceType: "dec_log_entry",
    resourceId: record.id,
    title: `${record.studentCode} DEC`,
    summary: `${record.triggerSummary}${record.responseSummary ? ` | ${record.responseSummary}` : ""}`,
    occurredAt: record.occurredAt,
    status: record.followUpRequired ? "follow_up_required" : "logged",
  }));
  const incidentItems: EvidenceSourceItem[] = context.incidents.map(
    (record) => ({
      resourceType: "incident_report",
      resourceId: record.id,
      title: `${record.studentCode} incident`,
      summary: `${record.incidentType} | ${record.summary}${record.actionsTaken ? ` | ${record.actionsTaken}` : ""}`,
      occurredAt: record.occurredAt,
      status: record.status,
    }),
  );
  const crisisItems: EvidenceSourceItem[] = context.crisisEvents.map(
    (record) => ({
      resourceType: "crisis_event",
      resourceId: record.id,
      title: `${record.studentCode} crisis`,
      summary: `${record.triggerSummary}${record.deescalationSummary ? ` | ${record.deescalationSummary}` : ""}`,
      occurredAt: record.occurredAt,
      status: record.status,
    }),
  );

  const sectionMap = {
    paec_signed_record: [
      { title: "PAEC signed record", items: paecItems },
      { title: "Related signatures", items: context.signatures },
      { title: "Meeting minutes", items: context.meetingMinutes },
    ],
    dec_exportable_logbook: [
      { title: "DEC logbook", items: decItems },
      { title: "Linked incidents", items: incidentItems },
      { title: "Linked crisis events", items: crisisItems },
    ],
    intervention_history: [
      { title: "PAEC history", items: paecItems },
      { title: "DEC logbook", items: decItems },
      { title: "Incidents", items: incidentItems },
      { title: "Crisis events", items: crisisItems },
      { title: "Meeting minutes", items: context.meetingMinutes },
    ],
    mineduc_supervision_report: [
      { title: "PAEC status", items: paecItems },
      { title: "DEC evidence", items: decItems },
      { title: "Incidents", items: incidentItems },
      { title: "Crisis events", items: crisisItems },
      { title: "Meeting minutes", items: context.meetingMinutes },
      { title: "Signatures", items: context.signatures },
    ],
  } as const;

  const selectedSections = sectionMap[input.reportType];
  const allSourceRefs = selectedSections.flatMap((section) => section.items);
  const materializedSections: EvidencePayloadSection[] = selectedSections.map(
    (section) => ({
      title: section.title,
      items: [...section.items],
    }),
  );
  const generatedAt = new Date().toISOString();
  const title =
    input.title?.trim() ||
    `${input.reportType.replaceAll("_", " ")} · ${context.student.canonicalCode}`;
  const fileBase = `${input.reportType}-${context.student.canonicalCode}-${generatedAt.slice(0, 10)}`;
  const exportArtifacts = buildEvidenceExportArtifacts({
    title,
    reportType: input.reportType,
    organizationName: context.organization.displayName,
    studentName: context.student.fullName,
    studentCode: context.student.canonicalCode,
    generatedAt,
    preparedBy: context.createdByProfileName,
    sections: materializedSections,
    fileBase,
  });

  return {
    title,
    sourceRefs: allSourceRefs,
    payload: {
      version: 1,
      reportType: input.reportType,
      organization: context.organization,
      student: context.student,
      generatedAt,
      preparedBy: context.createdByProfileName,
      sections: materializedSections,
      export: exportArtifacts,
    },
  };
}

async function getEvidenceBuildContext(
  client: Queryable,
  input: CreateEvidenceComplianceReportInput,
) {
  const organization = (
    await client.query<{ id: string; displayName: string }>(
      `
        select id, display_name as "displayName"
        from organizations
        where id = $1
        limit 1
      `,
      [input.organizationId],
    )
  ).rows[0];

  const student = (
    await client.query<{ id: string; canonicalCode: string; fullName: string }>(
      `
        select
          id,
          canonical_code as "canonicalCode",
          concat_ws(' ', first_name, last_name) as "fullName"
        from student_core_profiles
        where id = $1
          and organization_id = $2
        limit 1
      `,
      [input.studentId, input.organizationId],
    )
  ).rows[0];

  if (!organization || !student) {
    throw new Error(
      "Organization or student not found for evidence packaging.",
    );
  }

  const createdByProfileName = input.createdByProfileId
    ? ((
        await client.query<{ fullName: string }>(
          `
            select full_name as "fullName"
            from profiles
            where id = $1
            limit 1
          `,
          [input.createdByProfileId],
        )
      ).rows[0]?.fullName ?? null)
    : null;

  const [
    paecRecords,
    decLogs,
    incidents,
    crisisEvents,
    meetingMinutes,
    signatures,
  ] = await Promise.all([
    client.query<PaecSummary>(
      `
        select
          pr.id,
          pr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          pr.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          owner.full_name as "ownerProfileName",
          pr.status,
          pr.support_summary as "supportSummary",
          pr.primary_objective as "primaryObjective",
          pr.accommodations,
          pr.family_coordination_summary as "familyCoordinationSummary",
          pr.review_cadence as "reviewCadence",
          pr.success_indicators as "successIndicators",
          pr.review_due_at as "reviewDueAt",
          pr.signed_at as "signedAt",
          pr.created_at as "createdAt"
        from paec_records pr
        inner join organizations o on o.id = pr.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = pr.student_id
        left join profiles owner on owner.id = pr.owner_profile_id
        where pr.organization_id = $1 and pr.student_id = $2
        order by pr.created_at desc
      `,
      [input.organizationId, input.studentId],
    ),
    client.query<DecLogSummary>(
      `
        select
          dl.id,
          dl.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          dl.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          recorder.full_name as "recordedByProfileName",
          dl.severity,
          dl.trigger_summary as "triggerSummary",
          dl.response_summary as "responseSummary",
          dl.follow_up_required as "followUpRequired",
          dl.occurred_at as "occurredAt"
        from dec_log_entries dl
        inner join organizations o on o.id = dl.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = dl.student_id
        left join profiles recorder on recorder.id = dl.recorded_by_profile_id
        where dl.organization_id = $1 and dl.student_id = $2
        order by dl.occurred_at desc
      `,
      [input.organizationId, input.studentId],
    ),
    client.query<IncidentReportSummary>(
      `
        select
          ir.id,
          ir.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          ir.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          reporter.full_name as "reportedByProfileName",
          ir.incident_type as "incidentType",
          ir.severity,
          ir.status,
          ir.location,
          ir.summary,
          ir.actions_taken as "actionsTaken",
          ir.occurred_at as "occurredAt"
        from incident_reports ir
        inner join organizations o on o.id = ir.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ir.student_id
        left join profiles reporter on reporter.id = ir.reported_by_profile_id
        where ir.organization_id = $1 and ir.student_id = $2
        order by ir.occurred_at desc
      `,
      [input.organizationId, input.studentId],
    ),
    client.query<CrisisEventSummary>(
      `
        select
          ce.id,
          ce.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          ce.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          actor.full_name as "triggeredByProfileName",
          ce.escalation_level as "escalationLevel",
          ce.status,
          ce.trigger_summary as "triggerSummary",
          ce.deescalation_summary as "deescalationSummary",
          ce.occurred_at as "occurredAt",
          ce.resolved_at as "resolvedAt"
        from crisis_events ce
        inner join organizations o on o.id = ce.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ce.student_id
        left join profiles actor on actor.id = ce.triggered_by_profile_id
        where ce.organization_id = $1 and ce.student_id = $2
        order by ce.occurred_at desc
      `,
      [input.organizationId, input.studentId],
    ),
    client.query<EvidenceSourceItem>(
      `
        select
          'meeting_minute' as "resourceType",
          mm.id::text as "resourceId",
          mm.title,
          mm.summary,
          mm.meeting_at as "occurredAt",
          mm.status
        from meeting_minutes mm
        where mm.organization_id = $1 and mm.student_id = $2
        order by mm.meeting_at desc
      `,
      [input.organizationId, input.studentId],
    ),
    client.query<EvidenceSourceItem>(
      `
        select
          'signature' as "resourceType",
          s.id::text as "resourceId",
          s.related_resource_type as title,
          concat_ws(' | ', signer.full_name, s.related_resource_type, s.related_resource_id::text) as summary,
          s.signed_at as "occurredAt",
          s.signature_status as status
        from signatures s
        left join profiles signer on signer.id = s.signer_profile_id
        where s.organization_id = $1 and s.student_id = $2
        order by s.created_at desc
      `,
      [input.organizationId, input.studentId],
    ),
  ]);

  return {
    organization,
    student,
    paecRecords: paecRecords.rows,
    decLogs: decLogs.rows,
    incidents: incidents.rows,
    crisisEvents: crisisEvents.rows,
    meetingMinutes: meetingMinutes.rows,
    signatures: signatures.rows,
    createdByProfileName,
  } satisfies EvidenceBuildContext;
}

export async function listPaecRecords(): Promise<PaecSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<PaecSummary>(
    `
      select
        pr.id,
        pr.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        pr.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        owner.full_name as "ownerProfileName",
        pr.status,
        pr.support_summary as "supportSummary",
        pr.primary_objective as "primaryObjective",
        pr.accommodations,
        pr.family_coordination_summary as "familyCoordinationSummary",
        pr.review_cadence as "reviewCadence",
        pr.success_indicators as "successIndicators",
        pr.review_due_at as "reviewDueAt",
        pr.signed_at as "signedAt",
        pr.created_at as "createdAt"
      from paec_records pr
      inner join organizations o on o.id = pr.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = pr.student_id
      left join profiles owner on owner.id = pr.owner_profile_id
      order by pr.created_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listComplianceDashboard(): Promise<
  ComplianceDashboardSummary[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<ComplianceDashboardSummary>(
    `
      select
        o.id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from paec_records pr where pr.organization_id = o.id and pr.status in ('active','signed')), 0) as "activePaec",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from paec_records pr where pr.organization_id = o.id and (pr.status = 'signed' or pr.signed_at is not null)), 0) as "signedPaec",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from incident_reports ir where ir.organization_id = o.id and ir.status in ('open','reviewing')), 0) as "openIncidents",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from crisis_events ce where ce.organization_id = o.id and ce.status in ('active','stabilized')), 0) as "activeCrisis",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from dec_log_entries dl where dl.organization_id = o.id and dl.follow_up_required = true), 0) as "followUpRequired",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from evidence_compliance_reports ecr where ecr.organization_id = o.id and ecr.status in ('generated','signed','exported')), 0) as "generatedReports"
      from organizations o
      order by o.display_name asc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listComplianceCaseSummaries(): Promise<
  ComplianceCaseSummary[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<ComplianceCaseSummary>(
    `
      select
        scp.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        scp.id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from paec_records pr where pr.student_id = scp.id and pr.status in ('active','signed')), 0) as "activePaec",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from incident_reports ir where ir.student_id = scp.id and ir.status in ('open','reviewing')), 0) as "openIncidents",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from crisis_events ce where ce.student_id = scp.id and ce.status in ('active','stabilized')), 0) as "activeCrisis",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from dec_log_entries dl where dl.student_id = scp.id and dl.follow_up_required = true), 0) as "followUpRequired",
        coalesce((select count(*)::int from evidence_compliance_reports ecr where ecr.student_id = scp.id and ecr.status in ('generated','signed','exported')), 0) as "reportCount",
        greatest(
          coalesce((select max(pr.created_at) from paec_records pr where pr.student_id = scp.id), '-infinity'::timestamptz),
          coalesce((select max(dl.occurred_at) from dec_log_entries dl where dl.student_id = scp.id), '-infinity'::timestamptz),
          coalesce((select max(ir.occurred_at) from incident_reports ir where ir.student_id = scp.id), '-infinity'::timestamptz),
          coalesce((select max(ce.occurred_at) from crisis_events ce where ce.student_id = scp.id), '-infinity'::timestamptz),
          coalesce((select max(mm.meeting_at) from meeting_minutes mm where mm.student_id = scp.id), '-infinity'::timestamptz)
        ) as "lastComplianceEventAt"
      from student_core_profiles scp
      inner join organizations o on o.id = scp.organization_id
      order by "activeCrisis" desc, "openIncidents" desc, "followUpRequired" desc, "lastComplianceEventAt" desc nulls last, scp.canonical_code asc
      limit 24
    `,
  );

  return rows.map((row) => ({
    ...row,
    lastComplianceEventAt:
      row.lastComplianceEventAt === "-infinity"
        ? null
        : row.lastComplianceEventAt,
  }));
}

export async function listEvidenceComplianceReports(): Promise<
  EvidenceComplianceReportSummary[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<EvidenceComplianceReportSummary>(
    `
      select
        ecr.id,
        ecr.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        ecr.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        creator.full_name as "createdByProfileName",
        ecr.report_type as "reportType",
        ecr.status,
        ecr.title,
        ecr.generated_at as "generatedAt",
        ecr.exported_at as "exportedAt",
        ecr.created_at as "createdAt",
        jsonb_array_length(coalesce(ecr.source_refs, '[]'::jsonb))::int as "sourceCount",
        ecr.payload -> 'export' ->> 'fileBase' as "fileName"
      from evidence_compliance_reports ecr
      inner join organizations o on o.id = ecr.organization_id
      left join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ecr.student_id
      left join profiles creator on creator.id = ecr.created_by_profile_id
      order by ecr.created_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function getEvidenceComplianceReportById(
  reportId: string,
  options?: {
    actorProfileId?: string | null;
    accessPurpose?: string | null;
  },
): Promise<EvidenceComplianceReportDetail | null> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<EvidenceComplianceReportDetail>(
    `
      select
        ecr.id,
        ecr.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        ecr.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        creator.full_name as "createdByProfileName",
        ecr.report_type as "reportType",
        ecr.status,
        ecr.title,
        ecr.generated_at as "generatedAt",
        ecr.exported_at as "exportedAt",
        ecr.created_at as "createdAt",
        jsonb_array_length(coalesce(ecr.source_refs, '[]'::jsonb))::int as "sourceCount",
        ecr.payload -> 'export' ->> 'fileBase' as "fileName",
        ecr.payload as payload,
        coalesce(ecr.source_refs, '[]'::jsonb) as "sourceRefs"
      from evidence_compliance_reports ecr
      inner join organizations o on o.id = ecr.organization_id
      left join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ecr.student_id
      left join profiles creator on creator.id = ecr.created_by_profile_id
      where ecr.id = $1
      limit 1
    `,
    [reportId],
  );

  const detail = rows[0] ?? null;
  if (!detail) {
    return null;
  }

  return applySchoolComplianceAccessToEvidenceReport(
    detail,
    options?.actorProfileId,
    options?.accessPurpose,
  );
}

export async function createPaecRecord(
  input: CreatePaecInput,
): Promise<PaecSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const { rows } = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into paec_records (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          owner_profile_id,
          status,
          support_summary,
          primary_objective,
          accommodations,
          family_coordination_summary,
          review_cadence,
          success_indicators,
          review_due_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7::jsonb, $8, $9, $10::jsonb, $11)
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.ownerProfileId ?? null,
        input.status,
        input.supportSummary,
        input.primaryObjective,
        JSON.stringify(input.accommodations),
        input.familyCoordinationSummary,
        input.reviewCadence,
        JSON.stringify(input.successIndicators),
        input.reviewDueAt ?? null,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "paec_record",
      rows[0].id,
      "school_compliance.paec_created",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        status: input.status,
        reviewCadence: input.reviewCadence,
      },
    );

    const created = await client.query<PaecSummary>(
      `
        select
          pr.id,
          pr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          pr.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          owner.full_name as "ownerProfileName",
          pr.status,
          pr.support_summary as "supportSummary",
          pr.primary_objective as "primaryObjective",
          pr.accommodations,
          pr.family_coordination_summary as "familyCoordinationSummary",
          pr.review_cadence as "reviewCadence",
          pr.success_indicators as "successIndicators",
          pr.review_due_at as "reviewDueAt",
          pr.signed_at as "signedAt",
          pr.created_at as "createdAt"
        from paec_records pr
        inner join organizations o on o.id = pr.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = pr.student_id
        left join profiles owner on owner.id = pr.owner_profile_id
        where pr.id = $1
      `,
      [rows[0].id],
    );

    return created.rows[0];
  });
}

export async function updatePaecRecord(
  paecId: string,
  input: UpdatePaecInput,
): Promise<PaecSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const setClauses: string[] = [];
    const values: unknown[] = [];
    let idx = 1;

    if (input.status !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`status = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.status);
    }
    if (input.supportSummary !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`support_summary = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.supportSummary);
    }
    if (input.primaryObjective !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`primary_objective = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.primaryObjective);
    }
    if (input.accommodations !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`accommodations = $${idx++}::jsonb`);
      values.push(JSON.stringify(input.accommodations));
    }
    if (input.familyCoordinationSummary !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`family_coordination_summary = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.familyCoordinationSummary);
    }
    if (input.reviewCadence !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`review_cadence = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.reviewCadence);
    }
    if (input.successIndicators !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`success_indicators = $${idx++}::jsonb`);
      values.push(JSON.stringify(input.successIndicators));
    }
    if (input.reviewDueAt !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`review_due_at = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.reviewDueAt);
    }
    if (input.signedAt !== undefined) {
      setClauses.push(`signed_at = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(input.signedAt);
    }

    if (setClauses.length === 0) {
      throw new Error("No fields provided for update.");
    }

    values.push(paecId);
    const { rowCount } = await client.query(
      `update paec_records set ${setClauses.join(", ")} where id = $${idx}`,
      values,
    );

    if (!rowCount || rowCount === 0) {
      throw new Error(`PAEC record ${paecId} not found.`);
    }

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "paec_record",
      paecId,
      "school_compliance.paec_updated",
      {
        paecId,
        updatedFields: Object.keys(input).filter(
          (k) => input[k as keyof UpdatePaecInput] !== undefined,
        ),
      },
    );

    const updated = await client.query<PaecSummary>(
      `
        select
          pr.id,
          pr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          pr.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          owner.full_name as "ownerProfileName",
          pr.status,
          pr.support_summary as "supportSummary",
          pr.primary_objective as "primaryObjective",
          pr.accommodations,
          pr.family_coordination_summary as "familyCoordinationSummary",
          pr.review_cadence as "reviewCadence",
          pr.success_indicators as "successIndicators",
          pr.review_due_at as "reviewDueAt",
          pr.signed_at as "signedAt",
          pr.created_at as "createdAt"
        from paec_records pr
        inner join organizations o on o.id = pr.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = pr.student_id
        left join profiles owner on owner.id = pr.owner_profile_id
        where pr.id = $1
      `,
      [paecId],
    );

    return updated.rows[0];
  });
}

export async function createCrisisEvent(
  input: CreateCrisisEventInput,
): Promise<CrisisEventSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const { rows } = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into crisis_events (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          triggered_by_profile_id,
          escalation_level,
          status,
          trigger_summary,
          deescalation_summary,
          occurred_at,
          resolved_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9)
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.triggeredByProfileId ?? null,
        input.escalationLevel,
        input.status,
        input.triggerSummary,
        input.deescalationSummary ?? null,
        input.occurredAt,
        input.resolvedAt ?? null,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "crisis_event",
      rows[0].id,
      "school_compliance.crisis_triggered",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        escalationLevel: input.escalationLevel,
        status: input.status,
      },
    );

    const created = await client.query<CrisisEventSummary>(
      `
        select
          ce.id,
          ce.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          ce.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          actor.full_name as "triggeredByProfileName",
          ce.escalation_level as "escalationLevel",
          ce.status,
          ce.trigger_summary as "triggerSummary",
          ce.deescalation_summary as "deescalationSummary",
          ce.occurred_at as "occurredAt",
          ce.resolved_at as "resolvedAt"
        from crisis_events ce
        inner join organizations o on o.id = ce.organization_id
        inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ce.student_id
        left join profiles actor on actor.id = ce.triggered_by_profile_id
        where ce.id = $1
      `,
      [rows[0].id],
    );

    return created.rows[0];
  });
}

export async function createEvidenceComplianceReport(
  input: CreateEvidenceComplianceReportInput,
): Promise<EvidenceComplianceReportSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const context = await getEvidenceBuildContext(client, input);
    const packaged = buildEvidencePackage(input, context);

    const { rows } = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into evidence_compliance_reports (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          created_by_profile_id,
          report_type,
          status,
          title,
          payload,
          source_refs,
          generated_at,
          exported_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, 'generated', $5, $6::jsonb, $7::jsonb, now(), null)
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.createdByProfileId ?? null,
        input.reportType,
        packaged.title,
        JSON.stringify(packaged.payload),
        JSON.stringify(packaged.sourceRefs),
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "evidence_compliance_report",
      rows[0].id,
      "school_compliance.evidence_report_generated",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        reportType: input.reportType,
        sourceCount: packaged.sourceRefs.length,
        sourceContext: input.sourceContext ?? null,
      },
    );

    const created = await client.query<EvidenceComplianceReportSummary>(
      `
        select
          ecr.id,
          ecr.organization_id as "organizationId",
          o.display_name as "organizationName",
          ecr.student_id as "studentId",
          scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
          concat_ws(' ', scp.first_name, scp.last_name) as "studentName",
          creator.full_name as "createdByProfileName",
          ecr.report_type as "reportType",
          ecr.status,
          ecr.title,
          ecr.generated_at as "generatedAt",
          ecr.exported_at as "exportedAt",
          ecr.created_at as "createdAt",
          jsonb_array_length(coalesce(ecr.source_refs, '[]'::jsonb))::int as "sourceCount",
          ecr.payload -> 'export' ->> 'fileBase' as "fileName"
        from evidence_compliance_reports ecr
        inner join organizations o on o.id = ecr.organization_id
        left join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ecr.student_id
        left join profiles creator on creator.id = ecr.created_by_profile_id
        where ecr.id = $1
      `,
      [rows[0].id],
    );

    return created.rows[0];
  });
}

export async function getSchoolComplianceSnapshot(options?: {
  actorProfileId?: string | null;
  requestedOrganizationId?: string | null;
}): Promise<SchoolComplianceSnapshot> {
  const database = await checkDatabaseHealth();

  if (database.status === "down") {
    return {
      database,
      stats: {
        paec: 0,
        decLogs: 0,
        incidents: 0,
        crisisEvents: 0,
        meetingMinutes: 0,
        signatures: 0,
      },
      dashboard: [],
      caseSummaries: [],
      evidenceReports: [],
      paecRecords: [],
      decLogs: [],
      incidents: [],
      crisisEvents: [],
      organizations: [],
      students: [],
      staffProfiles: [],
    };
  }

  const authorization = await authorizeInternalReadPermission({
    actorProfileId: options?.actorProfileId,
    permissionCodes: ["compliance.read"],
    requestedOrganizationId: options?.requestedOrganizationId ?? undefined,
  });

  const requestedScope = options?.requestedOrganizationId
    ? [options.requestedOrganizationId]
    : authorization.organizationScope;

  const [
    paecRecords,
    decLogs,
    incidents,
    crisisEvents,
    dashboard,
    caseSummaries,
    evidenceReports,
    counts,
    organizations,
    students,
    staffProfiles,
  ] = await Promise.all([
    listPaecRecords(),
    listDecLogs(),
    listIncidentReports(),
    listCrisisEvents(),
    listComplianceDashboard(),
    listComplianceCaseSummaries(),
    listEvidenceComplianceReports(),
    dbQuery<{
      paec: number;
      decLogs: number;
      incidents: number;
      crisisEvents: number;
      meetingMinutes: number;
      signatures: number;
    }>(
      `
        select
          (select count(*)::int from paec_records) as paec,
          (select count(*)::int from dec_log_entries) as "decLogs",
          (select count(*)::int from incident_reports) as incidents,
          (select count(*)::int from crisis_events) as "crisisEvents",
          (select count(*)::int from meeting_minutes) as "meetingMinutes",
          (select count(*)::int from signatures) as signatures
      `,
    ),
    dbQuery<OrganizationReference>(
      `
        select id, display_name as "displayName"
        from organizations
        order by display_name asc
      `,
    ),
    dbQuery<StudentReference>(
      `
        select
          id,
          concat(canonical_code, ' · ', first_name, ' ', last_name) as "displayName"
        from student_core_profiles
        order by canonical_code asc
      `,
    ),
    dbQuery<ActorReference>(
      `
        select id, full_name as "displayName"
        from profiles
        where role in ('organization_admin', 'teacher', 'professional')
        order by full_name asc
      `,
    ),
  ]);

  const scopedPaecRecords = applyOrganizationScope(
    paecRecords,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedDecLogs = applyOrganizationScope(
    decLogs,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedIncidents = applyOrganizationScope(
    incidents,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedCrisisEvents = applyOrganizationScope(
    crisisEvents,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedDashboard = applyOrganizationScope(
    dashboard,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedCaseSummaries = applyOrganizationScope(
    caseSummaries,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedEvidenceReports = applyOrganizationScope(
    evidenceReports,
    requestedScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedOrganizations = applyOrganizationScope(
    organizations.rows,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.id,
  );
  const scopedStudents =
    requestedScope === null
      ? students.rows
      : (
          await dbQuery<StudentReference>(
            `
              select
                id,
                concat(canonical_code, ' · ', first_name, ' ', last_name) as "displayName"
              from student_core_profiles
              where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
              order by canonical_code asc
            `,
            [requestedScope],
          )
        ).rows;
  const scopedStaffProfiles =
    requestedScope === null
      ? staffProfiles.rows
      : (
          await dbQuery<ActorReference>(
            `
              select distinct p.id, p.full_name as "displayName"
              from organization_memberships om
              inner join profiles p on p.id = om.profile_id
              where om.organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
                and p.role in ('organization_admin', 'teacher', 'professional')
              order by p.full_name asc
            `,
            [requestedScope],
          )
        ).rows;
  const scopedCounts =
    requestedScope === null
      ? counts.rows[0]
      : (
          await dbQuery<{
            paec: number;
            decLogs: number;
            incidents: number;
            crisisEvents: number;
            meetingMinutes: number;
            signatures: number;
          }>(
            `
              select
                (select count(*)::int from paec_records where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])) as paec,
                (select count(*)::int from dec_log_entries where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])) as "decLogs",
                (select count(*)::int from incident_reports where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])) as incidents,
                (select count(*)::int from crisis_events where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])) as "crisisEvents",
                (select count(*)::int from meeting_minutes where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])) as "meetingMinutes",
                (select count(*)::int from signatures where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])) as signatures
            `,
            [requestedScope],
          )
        ).rows[0];

  return {
    database,
    stats: scopedCounts,
    dashboard: scopedDashboard,
    caseSummaries: scopedCaseSummaries,
    evidenceReports: scopedEvidenceReports,
    paecRecords: await applySchoolComplianceAccessToPaecRecords(
      scopedPaecRecords,
      authorization.actorProfileId,
      "operational_console",
    ),
    decLogs: await applySchoolComplianceAccessToDecLogs(
      scopedDecLogs,
      authorization.actorProfileId,
      "operational_console",
    ),
    incidents: await applySchoolComplianceAccessToIncidentReports(
      scopedIncidents,
      authorization.actorProfileId,
      "operational_console",
    ),
    crisisEvents: await applySchoolComplianceAccessToCrisisEvents(
      scopedCrisisEvents,
      authorization.actorProfileId,
      "operational_console",
    ),
    organizations: scopedOrganizations,
    students: scopedStudents,
    staffProfiles: scopedStaffProfiles,
  };
}

import { dbQuery, runInTransaction } from "@/src/server/db/client";
import { checkDatabaseHealth } from "@/src/server/db/health";
import {
  applyOrganizationScope,
  authorizeInternalReadPermission,
} from "@/src/server/runtime-auth/service";
import type {
  CareCoordinationReference,
  CareCoordinationSnapshot,
  CoordinationMessageSummary,
  CoordinationThreadSummary,
  CoordinationVisibility,
  CreateFollowUpInput,
  CreateMessageInput,
  CreateObservationInput,
  CreateThreadInput,
  FollowUpSummary,
  ObservationSummary,
  ParticipantRole,
} from "@/src/lib/care-coordination/contracts";

async function emitOutboxEvent(
  client: { query: (text: string, params?: unknown[]) => Promise<unknown> },
  aggregateType: string,
  aggregateId: string,
  eventName: string,
  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
) {
  await client.query(
    `
      insert into outbox_events (
        aggregate_type,
        aggregate_id,
        event_name,
        event_version,
        payload,
        status
      )
      values ($1, $2, $3, 1, $4::jsonb, 'pending')
    `,
    [aggregateType, aggregateId, eventName, JSON.stringify(payload)],
  );
}

function mapProfileRoleToParticipantRole(
  role: string | null | undefined,
): ParticipantRole {
  switch (role) {
    case "parent":
    case "guardian":
      return "guardian";
    case "teacher":
      return "teacher";
    case "professional":
      return "professional";
    case "organization_admin":
      return "organization_admin";
    default:
      return "care_coordinator";
  }
}

type CoordinationVisibilityRecord = {
  organizationId: string;
  studentId: string;
  visibilityScope: CoordinationVisibility;
};

type ActorCoordinationAccess = {
  platformAdmin: boolean;
  organizationRoleCodes: Map<string, Set<string>>;
  guardianStudentIds: Set<string>;
  schoolStudentIds: Set<string>;
  clinicalStudentIds: Set<string>;
};

function careCoordinationAuthError(message: string, code: string) {
  return Object.assign(new Error(message), { code });
}

async function buildActorCoordinationAccess(
  actorProfileId: string,
  organizationIds: string[],
  studentIds: string[],
): Promise<ActorCoordinationAccess> {
  const organizationRoleCodes = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
  const guardianStudentIds = new Set<string>();
  const schoolStudentIds = new Set<string>();
  const clinicalStudentIds = new Set<string>();

  const [
    { rows: platformRows },
    { rows: roleRows },
    { rows: familyRows },
    { rows: careTeamRows },
  ] = await Promise.all([
    dbQuery<{ hasPlatformAdmin: boolean }>(
      `
          select exists (
            select 1
            from profile_role_assignments pra
            inner join roles r on r.id = pra.role_id and r.active = true
            where pra.profile_id = $1
              and pra.active = true
              and pra.organization_id is null
              and r.code = 'platform.super_admin'
          ) as "hasPlatformAdmin"
        `,
      [actorProfileId],
    ),
    organizationIds.length > 0
      ? dbQuery<{ organizationId: string; roleCode: string }>(
          `
              select
                pra.organization_id as "organizationId",
                r.code as "roleCode"
              from profile_role_assignments pra
              inner join roles r on r.id = pra.role_id and r.active = true
              where pra.profile_id = $1
                and pra.active = true
                and pra.organization_id = any($2::uuid[])
            `,
          [actorProfileId, organizationIds],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({
          rows: [] as Array<{ organizationId: string; roleCode: string }>,
        }),
    studentIds.length > 0
      ? dbQuery<{ studentId: string }>(
          `
              select fr.student_id as "studentId"
              from family_relationships fr
              where fr.profile_id = $1
                and fr.student_id = any($2::uuid[])
            `,
          [actorProfileId, studentIds],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({ rows: [] as Array<{ studentId: string }> }),
    studentIds.length > 0
      ? dbQuery<{ studentId: string; teamRole: string }>(
          `
              select
                ctm.student_id as "studentId",
                ctm.team_role as "teamRole"
              from care_team_members ctm
              where ctm.profile_id = $1
                and ctm.active = true
                and ctm.student_id = any($2::uuid[])
            `,
          [actorProfileId, studentIds],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({
          rows: [] as Array<{ studentId: string; teamRole: string }>,
        }),
  ]);

  for (const row of roleRows) {
    const roleCodes =
      organizationRoleCodes.get(row.organizationId) ?? new Set<string>();
    roleCodes.add(row.roleCode);
    organizationRoleCodes.set(row.organizationId, roleCodes);
  }

  for (const row of familyRows) {
    guardianStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
  }

  for (const row of careTeamRows) {
    if (row.teamRole === "guardian") {
      guardianStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
    }
    if (
      row.teamRole === "teacher" ||
      row.teamRole === "school_admin" ||
      row.teamRole === "care_coordinator"
    ) {
      schoolStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
    }
    if (
      row.teamRole === "professional" ||
      row.teamRole === "care_coordinator"
    ) {
      clinicalStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
    }
  }

  return {
    platformAdmin: Boolean(platformRows[0]?.hasPlatformAdmin),
    organizationRoleCodes,
    guardianStudentIds,
    schoolStudentIds,
    clinicalStudentIds,
  };
}

function hasAnyRoleCode(
  access: ActorCoordinationAccess,
  organizationId: string,
  roleCodes: string[],
) {
  const assigned = access.organizationRoleCodes.get(organizationId);
  return Boolean(
    assigned && roleCodes.some((roleCode) => assigned.has(roleCode)),
  );
}

function canAccessCoordinationRecord(
  access: ActorCoordinationAccess,
  item: CoordinationVisibilityRecord,
) {
  if (access.platformAdmin) {
    return true;
  }

  const isOrgAdmin = hasAnyRoleCode(access, item.organizationId, [
    "org.owner",
    "org.admin",
  ]);

  switch (item.visibilityScope) {
    case "shared":
      return true;
    case "school_team":
      return (
        isOrgAdmin ||
        hasAnyRoleCode(access, item.organizationId, ["school.teacher"]) ||
        access.schoolStudentIds.has(item.studentId)
      );
    case "clinical_team":
      return (
        isOrgAdmin ||
        hasAnyRoleCode(access, item.organizationId, [
          "clinical.professional",
        ]) ||
        access.clinicalStudentIds.has(item.studentId)
      );
    case "guardians_only":
      return access.guardianStudentIds.has(item.studentId);
    default:
      return false;
  }
}

export async function filterCareCoordinationVisibility<
  T extends CoordinationVisibilityRecord,
>(items: T[], actorProfileId?: string | null) {
  if (!actorProfileId || items.length === 0) {
    return items;
  }

  const access = await buildActorCoordinationAccess(
    actorProfileId,
    [...new Set(items.map((item) => item.organizationId))],
    [...new Set(items.map((item) => item.studentId))],
  );

  return items.filter((item) => canAccessCoordinationRecord(access, item));
}

export async function assertCareCoordinationVisibilityAccess(input: {
  actorProfileId: string;
  organizationId: string;
  studentId: string;
  visibilityScope: CoordinationVisibility;
}) {
  const access = await buildActorCoordinationAccess(
    input.actorProfileId,
    [input.organizationId],
    [input.studentId],
  );

  if (!canAccessCoordinationRecord(access, input)) {
    throw careCoordinationAuthError(
      "Actor cannot access the requested care coordination visibility scope.",
      "FORBIDDEN",
    );
  }
}

export async function listObservations(): Promise<ObservationSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<ObservationSummary>(
    `
      select
        co.id,
        co.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        co.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        author.full_name as "authorProfileName",
        co.source_context as "sourceContext",
        co.visibility_scope as "visibilityScope",
        co.observation_type as "observationType",
        co.content,
        co.observed_at as "observedAt"
      from coordination_observations co
      inner join organizations o on o.id = co.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = co.student_id
      left join profiles author on author.id = co.author_profile_id
      order by co.observed_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listThreads(): Promise<CoordinationThreadSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<CoordinationThreadSummary>(
    `
      select
        ct.id,
        ct.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        ct.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        creator.full_name as "createdByProfileName",
        ct.title,
        ct.context_summary as "contextSummary",
        ct.visibility_scope as "visibilityScope",
        ct.status,
        ct.priority,
        coalesce(array_remove(array_agg(distinct participant.full_name), null), '{}') as "participantNames",
        count(distinct cm.id)::int as "messageCount",
        ct.created_at as "createdAt"
      from coordination_threads ct
      inner join organizations o on o.id = ct.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ct.student_id
      left join profiles creator on creator.id = ct.created_by_profile_id
      left join coordination_thread_participants ctp on ctp.thread_id = ct.id and ctp.active = true
      left join profiles participant on participant.id = ctp.profile_id
      left join coordination_messages cm on cm.thread_id = ct.id
      group by ct.id, o.display_name, scp.canonical_code, scp.first_name, scp.last_name, creator.full_name
      order by ct.created_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listMessages(): Promise<CoordinationMessageSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<CoordinationMessageSummary>(
    `
      select
        cm.id,
        ct.organization_id as "organizationId",
        cm.thread_id as "threadId",
        ct.title as "threadTitle",
        cm.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        author.full_name as "authorProfileName",
        cm.message_kind as "messageKind",
        cm.visibility_scope as "visibilityScope",
        cm.body,
        cm.created_at as "createdAt"
      from coordination_messages cm
      inner join coordination_threads ct on ct.id = cm.thread_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cm.student_id
      left join profiles author on author.id = cm.author_profile_id
      order by cm.created_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listFollowUps(): Promise<FollowUpSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<FollowUpSummary>(
    `
      select
        cf.id,
        cf.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        cf.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        ct.title as "threadTitle",
        owner.full_name as "ownerProfileName",
        coalesce(ct.visibility_scope, 'shared') as "visibilityScope",
        cf.status,
        cf.title,
        cf.details,
        cf.due_at as "dueAt",
        cf.completed_at as "completedAt",
        cf.created_at as "createdAt"
      from coordination_follow_ups cf
      inner join organizations o on o.id = cf.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cf.student_id
      left join coordination_threads ct on ct.id = cf.thread_id
      left join profiles owner on owner.id = cf.owner_profile_id
      order by cf.created_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

async function getObservationById(
  client: {
    query: (
      text: string,
      params?: unknown[],
    ) => Promise<{ rows: ObservationSummary[] }>;
  },
  id: string,
) {
  const { rows } = await client.query(
    `
      select
        co.id,
        co.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        co.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",

        author.full_name as "authorProfileName",
        co.source_context as "sourceContext",
        co.visibility_scope as "visibilityScope",

        co.content,
        co.observed_at as "observedAt"
      from coordination_observations co
      inner join organizations o on o.id = co.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = co.student_id
      left join profiles author on author.id = co.author_profile_id

async function getThreadById(
  client: {
    query: (
      text: string,
      params?: unknown[],
    ) => Promise<{ rows: CoordinationThreadSummary[] }>;
  },
  id: string,
) {
  const { rows } = await client.query(
    `
      select
        ct.id,
        ct.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        ct.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        creator.full_name as "createdByProfileName",
        ct.title,
        ct.context_summary as "contextSummary",
        ct.visibility_scope as "visibilityScope",
        ct.status,
        ct.priority,
        coalesce(array_remove(array_agg(distinct participant.full_name), null), '{}') as "participantNames",
        count(distinct cm.id)::int as "messageCount",
        ct.created_at as "createdAt"
      from coordination_threads ct
      inner join organizations o on o.id = ct.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ct.student_id
      left join profiles creator on creator.id = ct.created_by_profile_id
      left join coordination_thread_participants ctp on ctp.thread_id = ct.id and ctp.active = true
      left join profiles participant on participant.id = ctp.profile_id
      left join coordination_messages cm on cm.thread_id = ct.id
      where ct.id = $1
      group by ct.id, o.display_name, scp.canonical_code, scp.first_name, scp.last_name, creator.full_name
    `,
    [id],
  );

  return rows[0];
}

export async function getThreadVisibilityContext(threadId: string) {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<{
    organizationId: string;
    studentId: string;
    visibilityScope: CoordinationVisibility;
  }>(
    `
      select
        organization_id as "organizationId",
        student_id as "studentId",
        visibility_scope as "visibilityScope"
      from coordination_threads
      where id = $1
      limit 1
    `,
    [threadId],
  );

  if (!rows[0]) {
    throw careCoordinationAuthError(
      "Coordination thread does not exist.",
      "THREAD_NOT_FOUND",
    );
  }

  return rows[0];
}
