export async function createObservation(
  input: CreateObservationInput,
): Promise<ObservationSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into coordination_observations (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          author_profile_id,
          source_context,
          visibility_scope,
          observation_type,
          content,
          observed_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8)
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.authorProfileId ?? null,
        input.sourceContext,
        input.visibilityScope,
        input.observationType,
        input.content,
        input.observedAt,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "coordination_observation",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "care_coordination.observation_recorded",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        sourceContext: input.sourceContext,
        visibilityScope: input.visibilityScope,
        observationType: input.observationType,
      },
    );

    return getObservationById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function createThread(
  input: CreateThreadInput,
): Promise<CoordinationThreadSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into coordination_threads (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          created_by_profile_id,
          title,
          context_summary,
          visibility_scope,
          status,
          priority,
          updated_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, now())
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.createdByProfileId ?? null,
        input.title,
        input.contextSummary ?? null,
        input.visibilityScope,
        input.status,
        input.priority,
      ],
    );

    if (input.createdByProfileId) {
      const profileLookup = await client.query<{ role: string }>(
        `select role from profiles where id = $1`,
        [input.createdByProfileId],
      );
      const participantRole = mapProfileRoleToParticipantRole(
        profileLookup.rows[0]?.role,
      );
      await client.query(
        `
          insert into coordination_thread_participants (
            thread_id,
            profile_id,
            participant_role,
            access_level,
            active
          )
          values ($1, $2, $3, 'owner', true)
          on conflict (thread_id, profile_id)
          do update set
            participant_role = excluded.participant_role,
            access_level = excluded.access_level,
            active = true
        `,
        [inserted.rows[0].id, input.createdByProfileId, participantRole],
      );
    }

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "coordination_thread",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "care_coordination.thread_opened",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        visibilityScope: input.visibilityScope,
        priority: input.priority,
        status: input.status,
      },
    );

    return getThreadById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function createMessage(
  input: CreateMessageInput,
): Promise<CoordinationMessageSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into coordination_messages (
          thread_id,
          student_id,
          author_profile_id,
          message_kind,
          visibility_scope,
          body
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6)
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.threadId,
        input.studentId,
        input.authorProfileId ?? null,
        input.messageKind,
        input.visibilityScope,
        input.body,
      ],
    );

    await client.query(
      `update coordination_threads set updated_at = now() where id = $1`,
      [input.threadId],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "coordination_message",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "care_coordination.message_posted",
      {
        threadId: input.threadId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        messageKind: input.messageKind,
        visibilityScope: input.visibilityScope,
      },
    );

    return getMessageById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function createFollowUp(
  input: CreateFollowUpInput,
): Promise<FollowUpSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into coordination_follow_ups (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          thread_id,
          owner_profile_id,
          status,
          title,
          details,
          due_at,
          completed_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9)
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.threadId ?? null,
        input.ownerProfileId ?? null,
        input.status,
        input.title,
        input.details ?? null,
        input.dueAt ?? null,
        input.completedAt ?? null,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "coordination_follow_up",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "care_coordination.follow_up_created",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        threadId: input.threadId ?? null,
        status: input.status,
        sourceContext: input.sourceContext ?? null,
      },
    );

    return getFollowUpById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function updateFollowUp(
  input: import("@/src/lib/care-coordination/contracts").UpdateFollowUpInput,
): Promise<FollowUpSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const completedAt =
      input.status === "completed" ? new Date().toISOString() : null;

    const { rows } = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        update coordination_follow_ups
        set
          status = $1,
          completed_at = coalesce($2::timestamptz, completed_at),
          updated_at = now()
        where id = $3 and organization_id = $4
        returning id
      `,
      [input.status, completedAt, input.followUpId, input.organizationId],
    );

    if (rows.length === 0) {
      throw new Error("Follow-up not found.");
    }

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "coordination_follow_up",
      input.followUpId,
      "care_coordination.follow_up_updated",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        nextStatus: input.status,
        note: input.note ?? null,
        source: "follow_ups_api",
      },
    );

    return getFollowUpById(client, input.followUpId);
  });
}

export async function getCareCoordinationSnapshot(options?: {
  actorProfileId?: string | null;
}): Promise<CareCoordinationSnapshot> {
  const database = await checkDatabaseHealth();

  if (database.status === "down") {
    return {
      database,
      stats: {
        observations: 0,
        threads: 0,
        messages: 0,
        followUps: 0,
        openFollowUps: 0,
      },
      observations: [],
      threads: [],
      messages: [],
      followUps: [],
      organizations: [],
      students: [],
      participantProfiles: [],
      threadReferences: [],
    };
  }

  const authorization = await authorizeInternalReadPermission({
    actorProfileId: options?.actorProfileId,
    permissionCodes: ["coordination.read"],
  });

  const [
    observations,
    threads,
    messages,
    followUps,
    organizations,
    students,
    participantProfiles,
    threadReferences,
  ] = await Promise.all([
    listObservations(),
    listThreads(),
    listMessages(),
    listFollowUps(),
    dbQuery<CareCoordinationReference>(
      `select id, display_name as "displayName" from organizations order by display_name asc`,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<CareCoordinationReference>(
      `
          select id, concat(canonical_code, ' · ', first_name, ' ', last_name) as "displayName"
          from student_core_profiles
          order by canonical_code asc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<CareCoordinationReference>(
      `
          select id, full_name as "displayName"
          from profiles
          where status = 'active'
          order by full_name asc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<CareCoordinationReference>(
      `
          select ct.id, concat(scp.canonical_code, ' · ', ct.title) as "displayName"
          from coordination_threads ct
          inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ct.student_id
          order by ct.created_at desc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
  ]);

  const scopedObservations = applyOrganizationScope(
    observations,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const visibleObservations = await filterCareCoordinationVisibility(
    scopedObservations,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
  );
  const scopedThreads = applyOrganizationScope(
    threads,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const visibleThreads = await filterCareCoordinationVisibility(
    scopedThreads,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
  );
  const scopedMessages = applyOrganizationScope(
    messages,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const visibleMessages = await filterCareCoordinationVisibility(
    scopedMessages,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
  );
  const scopedFollowUps = applyOrganizationScope(
    followUps,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const visibleFollowUps = await filterCareCoordinationVisibility(
    scopedFollowUps,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
  );
  const scopedOrganizations = applyOrganizationScope(
    organizations,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.id,
  );
  const scopedStudents =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? students
      : (
          await dbQuery<CareCoordinationReference>(
            `
              select id, concat(canonical_code, ' · ', first_name, ' ', last_name) as "displayName"
              from student_core_profiles
              where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
              order by canonical_code asc
            `,
            [authorization.organizationScope],
          )
        ).rows;
  const scopedParticipantProfiles =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? participantProfiles
      : (
          await dbQuery<CareCoordinationReference>(
            `
              select distinct p.id, p.full_name as "displayName"
              from organization_memberships om
              inner join profiles p on p.id = om.profile_id
              where om.organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
                and p.status = 'active'
              order by p.full_name asc
            `,
            [authorization.organizationScope],
          )
        ).rows;
  const scopedThreadReferences =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? threadReferences
      : visibleThreads.map((thread) => ({
          id: thread.id,
          displayName: `${thread.studentCode} · ${thread.title}`,
        }));

  return {
    database,
    stats: {
      observations: visibleObservations.length,
      threads: visibleThreads.length,
      messages: visibleMessages.length,
      followUps: visibleFollowUps.length,
      openFollowUps: visibleFollowUps.filter(
        (item) => item.status !== "completed",
      ).length,
    },
    observations: visibleObservations,
    threads: visibleThreads,
    messages: visibleMessages,
    followUps: visibleFollowUps,
    organizations: scopedOrganizations,
    students: scopedStudents,
    participantProfiles: scopedParticipantProfiles,
    threadReferences: scopedThreadReferences,
  };
}

import "server-only";

import { dbQuery, runInTransaction } from "@/src/server/db/client";
import type {
  LocalModuleDefinition,
  OrganizationLocalRoleViewSummary,
  OrganizationModuleToggleSummary,
  UpsertOrganizationLocalRoleViewInput,
  UpsertOrganizationModuleToggleInput,
} from "@/src/lib/access-control/contracts";
import type {
  ActorExperienceProfile,
  CreateMarketingLeadInput,
  MarketingLeadRecord,
  OrganizationExperienceSnapshot,
} from "@/src/lib/experience/contracts";
import { familyFeatureKeySchema } from "@/src/lib/experience/contracts";
import { organizationModuleKeySchema } from "@/src/lib/access-control/contracts";

type OrganizationRef = {
  organizationId: string;
};

type FamilyEntitlementRow = {
  featureKey: string;
};

const allModuleKeys = organizationModuleKeySchema.options;

function deriveLocalRoleView(role: string) {
  switch (role) {
    case "platform_admin":
      return "super_admin" as const;
    case "organization_admin":
      return "director" as const;
    case "professional":
      return "external_therapist" as const;
    case "teacher":
      return "teacher" as const;
    default:
      return "guardian_family" as const;
  }
}

export async function listOrganizationFeatureModules(): Promise<
  LocalModuleDefinition[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<LocalModuleDefinition>(
    `
      select
        key,
        display_name as "displayName",
        audience,
        description
      from organization_feature_modules
      order by audience asc, display_name asc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listOrganizationFeatureToggles(): Promise<
  OrganizationModuleToggleSummary[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<OrganizationModuleToggleSummary>(
    `
      select
        oft.id,
        oft.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        oft.module_key as "moduleKey",
        ofm.display_name as "moduleDisplayName",
        oft.enabled,
        p.full_name as "managedByProfileName",
        oft.updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from organization_feature_toggles oft
      inner join organizations o on o.id = oft.organization_id
      inner join organization_feature_modules ofm on ofm.key = oft.module_key
      left join profiles p on p.id = oft.managed_by_profile_id
      order by o.display_name asc, ofm.display_name asc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function listOrganizationLocalRoleViews(): Promise<
  OrganizationLocalRoleViewSummary[]
> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<OrganizationLocalRoleViewSummary>(
    `
      select
        olrv.id,
        olrv.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        olrv.profile_id as "profileId",
        p.full_name as "profileName",
        olrv.view_key as "viewKey",
        olrv.active,
        olrv.updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from organization_local_role_views olrv
      inner join organizations o on o.id = olrv.organization_id
      inner join profiles p on p.id = olrv.profile_id
      order by o.display_name asc, p.full_name asc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function upsertOrganizationFeatureToggle(
  input: UpsertOrganizationModuleToggleInput,
) {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<OrganizationModuleToggleSummary>(
    `
      insert into organization_feature_toggles (
        organization_id,
        module_key,
        enabled,
        managed_by_profile_id,
        metadata
      )
      values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5::jsonb)
      on conflict (organization_id, module_key)
      do update set
        enabled = excluded.enabled,
        managed_by_profile_id = excluded.managed_by_profile_id,
        metadata = excluded.metadata,
        updated_at = now()
      returning id
    `,
    [
      input.organizationId,
      input.moduleKey,
      input.enabled,
      input.managedByProfileId ?? null,
      JSON.stringify(input.metadata ?? {}),
    ],
  );

  const { rows: joined } = await dbQuery<OrganizationModuleToggleSummary>(
    `
      select
        oft.id,
        oft.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        oft.module_key as "moduleKey",
        ofm.display_name as "moduleDisplayName",
        oft.enabled,
        p.full_name as "managedByProfileName",
        oft.updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from organization_feature_toggles oft
      inner join organizations o on o.id = oft.organization_id
      inner join organization_feature_modules ofm on ofm.key = oft.module_key
      left join profiles p on p.id = oft.managed_by_profile_id
      where oft.id = $1
    `,
    [rows[0].id],
  );

  return joined[0];
}

export async function upsertOrganizationLocalRoleView(
  input: UpsertOrganizationLocalRoleViewInput,
) {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<OrganizationLocalRoleViewSummary>(
    `
      insert into organization_local_role_views (
        organization_id,
        profile_id,
        view_key,
        active,
        metadata
      )
      values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5::jsonb)
      on conflict (organization_id, profile_id)
      do update set
        view_key = excluded.view_key,
        active = excluded.active,
        metadata = excluded.metadata,
        updated_at = now()
      returning id
    `,
    [
      input.organizationId,
      input.profileId,
      input.viewKey,
      input.active,
      JSON.stringify(input.metadata ?? {}),
    ],
  );

  const { rows: joined } = await dbQuery<OrganizationLocalRoleViewSummary>(
    `
      select
        olrv.id,
        olrv.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        olrv.profile_id as "profileId",
        p.full_name as "profileName",
        olrv.view_key as "viewKey",
        olrv.active,
        olrv.updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from organization_local_role_views olrv
      inner join organizations o on o.id = olrv.organization_id
      inner join profiles p on p.id = olrv.profile_id
      where olrv.id = $1
    `,
    [rows[0].id],
  );

  return joined[0];
}

async function getPrimaryOrganizationForProfile(profileId: string) {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<OrganizationRef>(
    `
      select organization_id as "organizationId"
      from organization_memberships
      where profile_id = $1
      order by is_default desc, created_at asc
      limit 1
    `,
    [profileId],
  );

  return rows[0]?.organizationId ?? null;
}

export async function getActorExperienceProfile(input: {
  profileId: string;
  role: string;
}): Promise<ActorExperienceProfile> {
  if (input.role === "platform_admin") {
    return {
      organizationId: null,
      localRoleView: "super_admin",
      enabledModules: [...allModuleKeys],
      disabledModules: [],
      familyPremium: true,
      familyPremiumFeatures: [...familyFeatureKeySchema.options],
    };
  }

  const organizationId = await getPrimaryOrganizationForProfile(
    input.profileId,
  );
  const localRoleViewFallback = deriveLocalRoleView(input.role);

  const [toggleRows, roleRows, entitlementRows] = await Promise.all([
    organizationId
      ? dbQuery<{ moduleKey: string; enabled: boolean }>(
          `
            select module_key as "moduleKey", enabled
            from organization_feature_toggles
            where organization_id = $1
          `,
          [organizationId],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({
          rows: [] as Array<{ moduleKey: string; enabled: boolean }>,
        }),
    organizationId
      ? dbQuery<{ viewKey: string }>(
          `
            select view_key as "viewKey"
            from organization_local_role_views
            where organization_id = $1
              and profile_id = $2
              and active = true
            limit 1
          `,
          [organizationId, input.profileId],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({ rows: [] as Array<{ viewKey: string }> }),
    input.role === "parent" || input.role === "guardian"
      ? dbQuery<FamilyEntitlementRow>(
          `
            select
              feature_key as "featureKey",
              enabled,
              plan_key as "planKey"
            from profile_feature_entitlements
            where profile_id = $1
              and enabled = true
          `,
          [input.profileId],
        )
      : Promise.resolve({ rows: [] as FamilyEntitlementRow[] }),
  ]);

  const toggleMap = new Map(
    toggleRows.rows.map((row) => [row.moduleKey, row.enabled]),
  );
  const enabledModules = allModuleKeys.filter(
    (key) => toggleMap.get(key) !== false,
  );
  const disabledModules = allModuleKeys.filter(
    (key) => toggleMap.get(key) === false,
  );
  const localRoleView =
    (roleRows.rows[0]?.viewKey as ActorExperienceProfile["localRoleView"]) ??
    localRoleViewFallback;
  const premiumFeatures = entitlementRows.rows
    .map((row) => row.featureKey)
    .filter(
      (
        value,
      ): value is ActorExperienceProfile["familyPremiumFeatures"][number] =>
        familyFeatureKeySchema.options.includes(
          value as ActorExperienceProfile["familyPremiumFeatures"][number],
        ),
    );

  return {
    organizationId,
    localRoleView,
    enabledModules,
    disabledModules,
    familyPremium:
      premiumFeatures.includes("family_premium") || premiumFeatures.length > 0,
    familyPremiumFeatures: premiumFeatures,
  };
}

export async function listOrganizationExperienceSnapshots(
  organizationIds: string[],
): Promise<OrganizationExperienceSnapshot[]> {
  if (organizationIds.length === 0) {
    return [];
  }

  const { rows: organizations } = await dbQuery<{
    organizationId: string;
    organizationName: string;
  }>(
    `
      select
        id as "organizationId",
        display_name as "organizationName"
      from organizations
      where id = any($1::uuid[])
      order by display_name asc
    `,
    [organizationIds],
  );

  const { rows: toggles } = await dbQuery<{
    organizationId: string;
    moduleKey: string;
    enabled: boolean;
  }>(
    `
      select
        organization_id as "organizationId",
        module_key as "moduleKey",
        enabled
      from organization_feature_toggles
      where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
    `,
    [organizationIds],
  );

  const { rows: settings } = await dbQuery<{
    organizationId: string;
    settingKey: string;
    settingValue: Record<string, unknown>;
  }>(
    `
      select
        organization_id as "organizationId",
        setting_key as "settingKey",
        setting_value as "settingValue"
      from platform_settings
      where scope = 'organization'
        and organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
    `,
    [organizationIds],
  );

  const toggleRegistry = new Map<
    string,
    Array<{ moduleKey: string; enabled: boolean }>
  >();
  for (const toggle of toggles) {
    const current = toggleRegistry.get(toggle.organizationId) ?? [];
    current.push(toggle);
    toggleRegistry.set(toggle.organizationId, current);
  }

  const settingRegistry = new Map<
    string,
    Array<{ settingKey: string; settingValue: Record<string, unknown> }>
  >();
  for (const setting of settings) {
    const current = settingRegistry.get(setting.organizationId) ?? [];
    current.push(setting);
    settingRegistry.set(setting.organizationId, current);
  }

  return organizations.map((organization) => {
    const organizationToggles =
      toggleRegistry.get(organization.organizationId) ?? [];
    const organizationSettings =
      settingRegistry.get(organization.organizationId) ?? [];

    const enabledModules = organizationToggles
      .filter((item) => item.enabled)
      .map((item) => organizationModuleKeySchema.parse(item.moduleKey));
    const disabledModules = organizationToggles
      .filter((item) => !item.enabled)
      .map((item) => organizationModuleKeySchema.parse(item.moduleKey));

    const defaultLocaleSetting = organizationSettings.find(
      (item) => item.settingKey === "experience.default_locale",
    );
    const digestSetting = organizationSettings.find(
      (item) => item.settingKey === "notifications.daily_digest",
    );
    const complianceSetting = organizationSettings.find(
      (item) => item.settingKey === "compliance.reporting_mode",
    );

    return {
      organizationId: organization.organizationId,
      organizationName: organization.organizationName,
      defaultLocale:
        typeof defaultLocaleSetting?.settingValue?.locale === "string"
          ? defaultLocaleSetting.settingValue.locale
          : null,
      bookingEnabled: enabledModules.includes("billing"),
      familyPremiumEnabled: enabledModules.includes("family_premium"),
      dailyDigestHour:
        typeof digestSetting?.settingValue?.sendHour === "string"
          ? digestSetting.settingValue.sendHour
          : null,
      complianceMode:
        typeof complianceSetting?.settingValue?.mode === "string"
          ? complianceSetting.settingValue.mode
          : null,
      signedEvidenceRequired:
        complianceSetting?.settingValue?.signedEvidenceRequired === true,
      activeModuleKeys: enabledModules,
      disabledModuleKeys: disabledModules,
      settingKeys: organizationSettings.map((item) => item.settingKey),
    };
  });
}

export async function createMarketingLead(
  input: CreateMarketingLeadInput,
): Promise<MarketingLeadRecord> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const { rows } = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into marketing_leads (
          email,
          locale,
          source_path,
          campaign_key,
          tags,
          metadata
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5::jsonb, $6::jsonb)
        on conflict (email, source_path)
        do update set
          locale = excluded.locale,
          campaign_key = coalesce(excluded.campaign_key, marketing_leads.campaign_key),
          tags = excluded.tags,
          metadata = excluded.metadata
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.email,
        input.locale,
        input.sourcePath,
        input.campaignKey ?? null,
        JSON.stringify(input.tags ?? []),
        JSON.stringify(input.metadata ?? {}),
      ],
    );

    const { rows: joined } = await client.query<MarketingLeadRecord>(
      `
        select
          id,
          email,
          locale,
          source_path as "sourcePath",
          campaign_key as "campaignKey",
          created_at as "createdAt"
        from marketing_leads
        where id = $1
      `,
      [rows[0].id],
    );

    return joined[0];
  });
}

import "server-only";

import { Prisma, OutcomeStatus } from "@prisma/client";
import { logEvent } from "@/src/lib/observability/logger";
import { getPrisma } from "@/src/server/db/prisma";

type AccessAuditRecordInput = {
  organizationId?: string | null;
  actorProfileId?: string | null;
  targetProfileId?: string | null;
  childId?: string | null;
  studentId?: string | null;
  resourceType: string;
  resourceId: string;
  action: string;
  purpose?: string | null;
  outcome?: OutcomeStatus;
  ipAddress?: string | null;
  metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
};

type BatchStudentAuditInput = {
  request: Request;
  actorProfileId: string;
  organizationId?: string | null;
  studentIds: string[];
  resourceType: string;
  action: string;
  purpose?: string | null;
  metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
  maxStudents?: number;
};

function resolveClientIpAddress(request: Request) {
  const forwardedFor = request.headers.get("x-forwarded-for");
  if (forwardedFor) {
    const candidate = forwardedFor
      .split(",")
      .map((entry) => entry.trim())
      .find(Boolean);
    if (candidate) {
      return candidate;
    }
  }

  const cloudflareIp = request.headers.get("cf-connecting-ip")?.trim();
  if (cloudflareIp) {
    return cloudflareIp;
  }

  return null;
}

export async function recordAccessAuditLog(input: AccessAuditRecordInput) {
  try {
    await getPrisma().access_audit_logs.create({
      data: {
        organization_id: input.organizationId ?? null,
        actor_profile_id: input.actorProfileId ?? null,
        target_profile_id: input.targetProfileId ?? null,
        child_id: input.childId ?? null,
        student_id: input.studentId ?? null,
        resource_type: input.resourceType,
        resource_id: input.resourceId,
        action: input.action,
        purpose: input.purpose ?? null,
        outcome: input.outcome ?? OutcomeStatus.allowed,
        ip_address: input.ipAddress ?? null,
        metadata: (input.metadata ?? {}) as Prisma.InputJsonValue,
      },
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logEvent("warn", "audit.access_log_write_failed", {
      domain: "audit",
      action: input.action,
      resource_type: input.resourceType,
      resource_id: input.resourceId,
      student_id: input.studentId ?? null,
      organization_id: input.organizationId ?? null,
      actor_profile_id: input.actorProfileId ?? null,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "unknown_audit_error",
    });
  }
}

export async function recordStudentAccessAuditBatch(
  input: BatchStudentAuditInput,
) {
  const uniqueStudentIds = [...new Set(input.studentIds.filter(Boolean))];
  if (uniqueStudentIds.length === 0) {
    return;
  }

  const maxStudents = input.maxStudents ?? 12;
  const scopedStudentIds = uniqueStudentIds.slice(0, maxStudents);
  const ipAddress = resolveClientIpAddress(input.request);

  await Promise.all(
    scopedStudentIds.map((studentId) =>
      recordAccessAuditLog({
        organizationId: input.organizationId ?? null,
        actorProfileId: input.actorProfileId,
        studentId,
        resourceType: input.resourceType,
        resourceId: studentId,
        action: input.action,
        purpose: input.purpose ?? null,
        ipAddress,
        metadata: {
          ...(input.metadata ?? {}),
          studentIdsLogged: scopedStudentIds.length,
          totalStudentIdsObserved: uniqueStudentIds.length,
          truncated: uniqueStudentIds.length > scopedStudentIds.length,
        },
      }),
    ),
  );
}

import { getDbPool } from "@/src/server/db/client";

export async function checkDatabaseHealth() {
  try {
    const pool = getDbPool();
    await pool.query("select 1 as ok");

    return {
      status: "up",
      error: null,
    } as const;
  } catch (error) {
    return {
      status: "down",
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "unknown database error",
    } as const;
  }
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/server/db/client.ts ---
import {
  Pool,
  type PoolClient,
  type QueryResult,
  type QueryResultRow,
} from "pg";
import { headers } from "next/headers";
import { env } from "@/src/lib/config/env";

async function getAccessPurpose(): Promise<string | null> {
  try {
    const h = await headers();
    return h.get("x-tea-access-purpose")?.trim() || null;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

let pool: Pool | null = null;

export function getDbPool(): Pool {
  if (!pool) {
    const sslRequired = env.DATABASE_URL.includes("sslmode=require");
    pool = new Pool({
      connectionString: env.DATABASE_URL,
      max: 10,
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30_000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 8_000,
      ssl: sslRequired ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false,
    });
  }

  return pool;
}

export async function dbQuery<T extends QueryResultRow>(
  text: string,
  params: unknown[] = [],
): Promise<QueryResult<T>> {
  return getDbPool().query<T>(text, params);
}

export async function runInTransaction<T>(
  handler: (client: PoolClient) => Promise<T>,
): Promise<T> {
  const client = await getDbPool().connect();
  const purpose = await getAccessPurpose();

  try {
    await client.query("BEGIN");
    if (purpose) {
      // Set the purpose for the transaction session
      await client.query("SELECT set_config('app.current_purpose', $1, true)", [
        purpose,
      ]);
    }
    const result = await handler(client);
    await client.query("COMMIT");
    return result;
  } catch (error) {
    await client.query("ROLLBACK");
    throw error;
  } finally {
    client.release();
  }
}


--- FILE: /home/coldtemplar/Proyectos2026/tea-connect/src/server/db/prisma.ts ---
import "server-only";

import { headers } from "next/headers";
import { Prisma, PrismaClient } from "@prisma/client";
import { PrismaPg } from "@prisma/adapter-pg";
import { getDbPool } from "./client";

function createPrismaClient(
  options?: ConstructorParameters<typeof PrismaClient>[0],
) {
  const pool = getDbPool();
  const adapter = new PrismaPg(pool);
  return new PrismaClient({ ...options, adapter });
}

declare global {
  // eslint-disable-next-line no-var
  var __tea_prisma__: PrismaClient | undefined;
}

export function getPrisma(): PrismaClient {
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === "production") {
    return createPrismaClient();
  }

  if (!globalThis.__tea_prisma__) {
    globalThis.__tea_prisma__ = createPrismaClient();
  }

  return globalThis.__tea_prisma__;
}

async function getAccessPurpose(): Promise<string | null> {
  try {
    const h = await headers();
    return h.get("x-tea-access-purpose")?.trim() || null;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

async function applyPurposeToTransaction(
  tx: Prisma.TransactionClient,
  purpose: string,
) {
  await tx.$executeRaw(
    Prisma.sql`SELECT set_config('app.current_purpose', ${purpose}, true)`,
  );
}

export async function runInPrismaTransaction<T>(
  handler: (tx: Prisma.TransactionClient) => Promise<T>,
): Promise<T> {
  const prisma = getPrisma();
  const purpose = await getAccessPurpose();

  return prisma.$transaction(async (tx) => {
    if (purpose) {
      await applyPurposeToTransaction(tx, purpose);
    }
    return handler(tx);
  });
}

type ClinicalSubjectRecord = {
  organizationId: string;
  studentId: string;
};

type ClinicalAccessPurpose =
  | "operational_console"
  | "clinical_care"
  | "compliance_review"
  | "family_review"
  | "general";

type ActorClinicalAccess = {
  platformAdmin: boolean;
  organizationRoleCodes: Map<string, Set<string>>;
  clinicalStudentIds: Set<string>;
};

const REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT = "[redacted: elevated clinical access required]";
const FULL_CONTENT_PURPOSES = new Set<ClinicalAccessPurpose>([
  "operational_console",
  "clinical_care",
]);

function formatReferenceDateTime(value: string | Date | null | undefined) {
  if (!value) {
    return "No date";
  }

  const parsed = value instanceof Date ? value : new Date(value);

  if (Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime())) {
    return String(value).slice(0, 16).replace("T", " ");
  }

  return parsed.toISOString().slice(0, 16).replace("T", " ");
}

function resolveClinicalAccessPurpose(
  input?: string | null,
): ClinicalAccessPurpose {
  switch (input) {
    case "clinical_care":
    case "operational_console":
    case "compliance_review":
    case "family_review":
      return input;
    default:
      return "general";
  }
}

function truncateNarrative(text: string, maxLength = 220) {
  return text.length <= maxLength
    ? text
    : `${text.slice(0, maxLength).trimEnd()}…`;
}

function limitedClinicalNarrative(
  text: string,
  label: string,
  maxLength = 220,
) {
  return `[limited ${label}] ${truncateNarrative(text, maxLength)}`;
}

function redactStructuredClinicalPayload(
  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
  purpose: ClinicalAccessPurpose,
) {
  const safeKeys =
    purpose === "family_review"
      ? new Set([
          "recommendations",
          "homeRecommendations",
          "schoolRecommendations",
          "followUpWindow",
        ])
      : purpose === "compliance_review"
        ? new Set([
            "recommendations",
            "schoolAccommodations",
            "followUpWindow",
            "riskLevel",
          ])
        : new Set<string>();

  const result: Record<string, unknown> = {
    redacted: true,
    purpose,
    reason: "limited_structured_payload",
  };

  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(payload)) {
    if (!safeKeys.has(key)) continue;

    if (typeof value === "string") {
      result[key] = limitedClinicalNarrative(value, key, 180);
    } else if (Array.isArray(value)) {
      result[key] = value
        .filter((entry) => typeof entry === "string")
        .map((entry) => limitedClinicalNarrative(entry, key, 120))
        .slice(0, 6);
    } else if (value && typeof value === "object") {
      result[key] = "[redacted structured object]";
    } else {
      result[key] = value;
    }
  }

  return result;
}

async function buildActorClinicalAccess(
  actorProfileId: string,
  organizationIds: string[],
  studentIds: string[],
): Promise<ActorClinicalAccess> {
  const organizationRoleCodes = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
  const clinicalStudentIds = new Set<string>();

  const [{ rows: platformRows }, { rows: roleRows }, { rows: careTeamRows }] =
    await Promise.all([
      dbQuery<{ hasPlatformAdmin: boolean }>(
        `
        select exists (
          select 1
          from profile_role_assignments pra
          inner join roles r on r.id = pra.role_id and r.active = true
          where pra.profile_id = $1
            and pra.active = true
            and pra.organization_id is null
            and r.code = 'platform.super_admin'
        ) as "hasPlatformAdmin"
      `,
        [actorProfileId],
      ),
      organizationIds.length > 0
        ? dbQuery<{ organizationId: string; roleCode: string }>(
            `
            select
              pra.organization_id as "organizationId",
              r.code as "roleCode"
            from profile_role_assignments pra
            inner join roles r on r.id = pra.role_id and r.active = true
            where pra.profile_id = $1
              and pra.active = true
              and pra.organization_id = any($2::uuid[])
          `,
            [actorProfileId, organizationIds],
          )
        : Promise.resolve({
            rows: [] as Array<{ organizationId: string; roleCode: string }>,
          }),
      studentIds.length > 0
        ? dbQuery<{ studentId: string; teamRole: string }>(
            `
            select
              ctm.student_id as "studentId",
              ctm.team_role as "teamRole"
            from care_team_members ctm
            where ctm.profile_id = $1
              and ctm.active = true
              and ctm.student_id = any($2::uuid[])
          `,
            [actorProfileId, studentIds],
          )
        : Promise.resolve({
            rows: [] as Array<{ studentId: string; teamRole: string }>,
          }),
    ]);

  for (const row of roleRows) {
    const roleCodes =
      organizationRoleCodes.get(row.organizationId) ?? new Set<string>();
    roleCodes.add(row.roleCode);
    organizationRoleCodes.set(row.organizationId, roleCodes);
  }

  for (const row of careTeamRows) {
    if (
      row.teamRole === "professional" ||
      row.teamRole === "care_coordinator"
    ) {
      clinicalStudentIds.add(row.studentId);
    }
  }

  return {
    platformAdmin: Boolean(platformRows[0]?.hasPlatformAdmin),
    organizationRoleCodes,
    clinicalStudentIds,
  };
}

function hasClinicalRole(access: ActorClinicalAccess, organizationId: string) {
  const roleCodes = access.organizationRoleCodes.get(organizationId);

  return Boolean(
    roleCodes &&
    (roleCodes.has("org.owner") ||
      roleCodes.has("org.admin") ||
      roleCodes.has("clinical.professional")),
  );
}

function canReadFullClinicalContent(
  access: ActorClinicalAccess,
  item: ClinicalSubjectRecord,
  purpose: ClinicalAccessPurpose,
) {
  if (!FULL_CONTENT_PURPOSES.has(purpose)) {
    return false;
  }

  return (
    access.platformAdmin ||
    hasClinicalRole(access, item.organizationId) ||
    access.clinicalStudentIds.has(item.studentId)
  );
}

async function withClinicalAccess<T extends ClinicalSubjectRecord, TResult>(
  items: T[],
  actorProfileId: string | null | undefined,
  accessPurpose: string | null | undefined,
  mapper: (
    item: T,
    context: {
      canReadFullContent: boolean;
      purpose: ClinicalAccessPurpose;
    },
  ) => TResult,
) {
  const purpose = resolveClinicalAccessPurpose(accessPurpose);

  if (!actorProfileId || items.length === 0) {
    return items.map((item) =>
      mapper(item, { canReadFullContent: true, purpose }),
    );
  }

  const access = await buildActorClinicalAccess(
    actorProfileId,
    [...new Set(items.map((item) => item.organizationId))],
    [...new Set(items.map((item) => item.studentId))],
  );
  return items.map((item) =>
    mapper(item, {
      canReadFullContent: canReadFullClinicalContent(access, item, purpose),
      purpose,
    }),
  );
}

export function getRedactedClinicalText() {
  return REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT;
}

export async function applyClinicalAccessToTherapySessions(
  items: TherapySessionSummary[],
  actorProfileId?: string | null,
  accessPurpose?: string | null,
) {
  return withClinicalAccess(
    items,
    actorProfileId,
    accessPurpose,
    (item, context) =>
      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            summary:
              item.summary &&
              (context.purpose === "family_review" ||
                context.purpose === "compliance_review")
                ? limitedClinicalNarrative(item.summary, "session summary", 140)
                : item.summary
                  ? REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT
                  : null,
          },
  );
}

export async function applyClinicalAccessToNotes(
  items: ClinicalNoteSummary[],
  actorProfileId?: string | null,
  accessPurpose?: string | null,
) {
  return withClinicalAccess(
    items,
    actorProfileId,
    accessPurpose,
    (item, context) =>
      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            content:
              context.purpose === "compliance_review" &&
              item.noteType === "coordination"
                ? limitedClinicalNarrative(item.content, "coordination note")
                : context.purpose === "family_review" &&
                    (item.noteType === "progress" ||
                      item.noteType === "coordination")
                  ? limitedClinicalNarrative(item.content, "case note", 180)
                  : REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
          },
  );
}

export async function applyClinicalAccessToSoapNotes(
  items: SoapNoteSummary[],
  actorProfileId?: string | null,
  accessPurpose?: string | null,
) {
  return withClinicalAccess(
    items,
    actorProfileId,
    accessPurpose,
    (item, context) =>
      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            subjective:
              context.purpose === "family_review"
                ? limitedClinicalNarrative(
                    item.subjective,
                    "subjective note",
                    120,
                  )
                : REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
            objective:
              context.purpose === "compliance_review"
                ? limitedClinicalNarrative(
                    item.objective,
                    "objective note",
                    120,
                  )
                : REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
            assessment: REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
            plan:
              context.purpose === "family_review" ||
              context.purpose === "compliance_review"
                ? limitedClinicalNarrative(item.plan, "care plan", 140)
                : REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
          },
  );
}

export async function applyClinicalAccessToReports(
  items: ClinicalReportSummary[],
  actorProfileId?: string | null,
  accessPurpose?: string | null,
) {
  return withClinicalAccess(
    items,
    actorProfileId,
    accessPurpose,
    (item, context) =>
      context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            executiveSummary:
              item.executiveSummary === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "compliance_review" &&
                    item.reportType === "school_summary"
                  ? limitedClinicalNarrative(
                      item.executiveSummary,
                      "school summary",
                    )
                  : context.purpose === "family_review" &&
                      (item.reportType === "progress_report" ||
                        item.reportType === "school_summary")
                    ? limitedClinicalNarrative(
                        item.executiveSummary,
                        "clinical summary",
                        180,
                      )
                    : REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
          },
  );
}

async function getTherapySessionById(
  client: {
    query: (
      text: string,
      params?: unknown[],
    ) => Promise<{ rows: TherapySessionSummary[] }>;
  },
  id: string,
) {
  const { rows } = await client.query(
    `
      select
        ts.id,
        ts.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        ts.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        professional.full_name as "professionalProfileName",
        ts.session_type as "sessionType",
        ts.modality,
        ts.status,
        ts.summary,
        ts.started_at as "startedAt",
        ts.ended_at as "endedAt"
      from therapy_sessions ts
      inner join organizations o on o.id = ts.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ts.student_id
      left join profiles professional on professional.id = ts.professional_profile_id
      where ts.id = $1
    `,
    [id],
  );

  return rows[0];
}

async function getClinicalNoteById(
  client: {
    query: (
      text: string,
      params?: unknown[],
    ) => Promise<{ rows: ClinicalNoteSummary[] }>;
  },
  id: string,
) {
  const { rows } = await client.query(
    `
      select
        cn.id,
        cn.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        cn.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        author.full_name as "authorProfileName",
        case
          when ts.id is null then null
          else concat(ts.session_type, ' · ', to_char(ts.started_at, 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI'))
        end as "therapySessionLabel",
        cn.note_type as "noteType",
        cn.status,
        cn.title,
        cn.content,
        (sn.id is not null) as "hasSoap",
        cn.signed_at as "signedAt",
        cn.created_at as "createdAt"
      from clinical_notes cn
      inner join organizations o on o.id = cn.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cn.student_id
      left join profiles author on author.id = cn.author_profile_id
      left join therapy_sessions ts on ts.id = cn.therapy_session_id
      left join soap_notes sn on sn.clinical_note_id = cn.id
      where cn.id = $1
    `,
    [id],
  );

  return rows[0];
}

async function getSoapNoteById(
  client: {
    query: (
      text: string,
      params?: unknown[],
    ) => Promise<{ rows: SoapNoteSummary[] }>;
  },
  id: string,
) {

      select
        sn.id,
        cn.organization_id as "organizationId",
        sn.clinical_note_id as "clinicalNoteId",
        cn.title as "noteTitle",
        cn.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        sn.generated_by_ai as "generatedByAi",
        sn.subjective,
        sn.objective,
        sn.assessment,
        sn.plan,
        sn.updated_at as "updatedAt"
      from soap_notes sn
      inner join clinical_notes cn on cn.id = sn.clinical_note_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cn.student_id
      where sn.id = $1
    `,
    [id],
  );

  return rows[0];
}

export async function listTherapySessions(): Promise<TherapySessionSummary[]> {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<TherapySessionSummary>(
    `
      select
        ts.id,
        ts.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        ts.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        professional.full_name as "professionalProfileName",
        ts.session_type as "sessionType",
        ts.modality,
        ts.status,
        ts.summary,
        ts.started_at as "startedAt",
        ts.ended_at as "endedAt"
      from therapy_sessions ts
      inner join organizations o on o.id = ts.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = ts.student_id
      left join profiles professional on professional.id = ts.professional_profile_id
      order by ts.started_at desc
    `,
  );

  return rows;
}

export async function createTherapySession(
  input: CreateTherapySessionInput,
): Promise<TherapySessionSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into therapy_sessions (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          professional_profile_id,
          session_type,
          modality,
          status,
          summary,
          started_at,
          ended_at,
          updated_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9, now())
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.professionalProfileId ?? null,
        input.sessionType,
        input.modality,
        input.status,
        input.summary ?? null,
        input.startedAt,
        input.endedAt ?? null,
      ],
    );

    await client.query(
      `
        insert into clinical_events (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          actor_profile_id,
          event_type,
          source,
          occurred_at,
          payload
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, 'therapeutic_intervention', 'clinical_core', $4, $5::jsonb)
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.professionalProfileId ?? null,
        input.startedAt,
        JSON.stringify({
          sessionType: input.sessionType,
          modality: input.modality,
          status: input.status,
        }),
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "therapy_session",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "clinical_core.session_recorded",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        sessionType: input.sessionType,
        modality: input.modality,
        status: input.status,
      },
    );

    return getTherapySessionById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function createClinicalNote(
  input: CreateClinicalNoteInput,
): Promise<ClinicalNoteSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into clinical_notes (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          author_profile_id,
          therapy_session_id,
          note_type,
          status,
          title,
          content,
          signed_at,
          updated_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9, now())
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.authorProfileId ?? null,
        input.therapySessionId ?? null,
        input.noteType,
        input.status,
        input.title,
        input.content,
        input.signedAt ?? null,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "clinical_note",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "clinical_core.note_recorded",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        noteType: input.noteType,
        status: input.status,
        therapySessionId: input.therapySessionId ?? null,
        sourceContext: input.sourceContext ?? null,
      },
    );

    return getClinicalNoteById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function createSoapNote(
  input: CreateSoapNoteInput,
): Promise<SoapNoteSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{
      id: string;
      clinical_note_id: string;
    }>(
      `
        insert into soap_notes (
          clinical_note_id,
          generated_by_ai,
          subjective,
          objective,
          assessment,
          plan,
          updated_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, now())
        on conflict (clinical_note_id)
        do update set
          generated_by_ai = excluded.generated_by_ai,
          subjective = excluded.subjective,
          objective = excluded.objective,
          assessment = excluded.assessment,
          plan = excluded.plan,
          updated_at = now()
        returning id, clinical_note_id
      `,
      [
        input.clinicalNoteId,
        input.generatedByAi,
        input.subjective,
        input.objective,
        input.assessment,
        input.plan,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "soap_note",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "clinical_core.soap_documented",
      {
        clinicalNoteId: input.clinicalNoteId,
        generatedByAi: input.generatedByAi,
      },
    );

    return getSoapNoteById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function createClinicalReport(
  input: CreateClinicalReportInput,
): Promise<ClinicalReportSummary> {
  return runInTransaction(async (client) => {
    const inserted = await client.query<{ id: string }>(
      `
        insert into clinical_reports (
          organization_id,
          student_id,
          author_profile_id,
          report_type,
          status,
          title,
          executive_summary,
          payload,
          generated_at,
          signed_at,
          exported_at,
          updated_at
        )
        values ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8::jsonb, $9, $10, $11, now())
        returning id
      `,
      [
        input.organizationId,
        input.studentId,
        input.authorProfileId ?? null,
        input.reportType,
        input.status,
        input.title,
        input.executiveSummary ?? null,
        JSON.stringify(input.payload ?? {}),
        input.generatedAt ?? null,
        input.signedAt ?? null,
        input.exportedAt ?? null,
      ],
    );

    await emitOutboxEvent(
      client,
      "clinical_report",
      inserted.rows[0].id,
      "clinical_core.report_generated",
      {
        organizationId: input.organizationId,
        studentId: input.studentId,
        reportType: input.reportType,
        status: input.status,
      },
    );

    return getClinicalReportById(client, inserted.rows[0].id);
  });
}

export async function getClinicalReportExportById(args: {
  reportId: string;
  actorProfileId?: string | null;
  accessPurpose?: string | null;
  format: "html" | "markdown";
}) {
  const { rows } = await dbQuery<ClinicalReportDetail>(
    `
      select
        cr.id,
        cr.organization_id as "organizationId",
        o.display_name as "organizationName",
        cr.student_id as "studentId",
        scp.canonical_code as "studentCode",
        concat(scp.first_name, ' ', scp.last_name) as "studentName",
        author.full_name as "authorProfileName",
        cr.report_type as "reportType",
        cr.status,
        cr.title,
        cr.executive_summary as "executiveSummary",
        cr.payload,
        cr.generated_at as "generatedAt",
        cr.signed_at as "signedAt",
        cr.exported_at as "exportedAt",
        cr.created_at as "createdAt"
      from clinical_reports cr
      inner join organizations o on o.id = cr.organization_id
      inner join student_core_profiles scp on scp.id = cr.student_id
      left join profiles author on author.id = cr.author_profile_id
      where cr.id = $1
      limit 1
    `,
    [args.reportId],
  );

  const detail = rows[0];

  if (!detail) {
    return undefined;
  }

  const [result] = await withClinicalAccess(
    [detail],
    args.actorProfileId,
    args.accessPurpose,
    (item, context) => ({
      visibleReport: context.canReadFullContent
        ? item
        : {
            ...item,
            executiveSummary:
              item.executiveSummary === null
                ? null
                : context.purpose === "compliance_review" &&
                    item.reportType === "school_summary"
                  ? limitedClinicalNarrative(
                      item.executiveSummary,
                      "school summary",
                    )
                  : context.purpose === "family_review" &&
                      (item.reportType === "progress_report" ||
                        item.reportType === "school_summary")
                    ? limitedClinicalNarrative(
                        item.executiveSummary,
                        "clinical summary",
                        180,
                      )
                    : REDACTED_CLINICAL_TEXT,
            payload: {
              ...redactStructuredClinicalPayload(item.payload, context.purpose),
              reason:
                context.purpose === "compliance_review" ||
                context.purpose === "family_review"
                  ? "limited_summary_view"
                  : "elevated_clinical_access_required",
            },
          },
      canReadFullContent: context.canReadFullContent,
      purpose: context.purpose,
    }),
  );

  const markdown = [
    `# ${result.visibleReport.title}`,
    "",
    `- Student: ${result.visibleReport.studentName} (${result.visibleReport.studentCode})`,
    `- Organization: ${result.visibleReport.organizationName}`,
    `- Report type: ${result.visibleReport.reportType}`,
    `- Status: ${result.visibleReport.status}`,
    `- Generated at: ${result.visibleReport.generatedAt ?? "—"}`,
    `- Signed at: ${result.visibleReport.signedAt ?? "—"}`,
    `- Access purpose: ${result.purpose}`,
    `- Narrative scope: ${result.canReadFullContent ? "full" : "restricted"}`,
    "",
    "## Executive Summary",
    "",
    result.visibleReport.executiveSummary ?? "No executive summary available.",
    "",
    "## Structured Payload",
    "",
    "```json",
    JSON.stringify(result.visibleReport.payload, null, 2),
    "```",
    "",
  ].join("\n");

  const html = `<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <title>${result.visibleReport.title}</title>
    <style>
      body { font-family: Georgia, serif; margin: 2rem auto; max-width: 820px; color: #1d1d1d; line-height: 1.6; }
      h1, h2 { color: #153e3a; }
      .meta { display: grid; gap: .3rem; margin-bottom: 1.5rem; padding: 1rem 1.2rem; border: 1px solid #b8d6cf; border-radius: 16px; background: #f8fffd; }
      pre { background: #f4f4f4; border-radius: 14px; padding: 1rem; overflow-x: auto; }
      .badge { display: inline-block; padding: .25rem .6rem; border-radius: 999px; background: #153e3a; color: #f8fffd; font-size: .85rem; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>${result.visibleReport.title}</h1>
    <div class="meta">
      <div><strong>Student:</strong> ${result.visibleReport.studentName} (${result.visibleReport.studentCode})</div>
      <div><strong>Organization:</strong> ${result.visibleReport.organizationName}</div>
      <div><strong>Report type:</strong> <span class="badge">${result.visibleReport.reportType}</span></div>
      <div><strong>Status:</strong> ${result.visibleReport.status}</div>
      <div><strong>Generated at:</strong> ${result.visibleReport.generatedAt ?? "—"}</div>
      <div><strong>Signed at:</strong> ${result.visibleReport.signedAt ?? "—"}</div>
      <div><strong>Access purpose:</strong> ${result.purpose}</div>
      <div><strong>Narrative scope:</strong> ${result.canReadFullContent ? "full" : "restricted"}</div>
    </div>
    <h2>Executive Summary</h2>
    <p>${(result.visibleReport.executiveSummary ?? "No executive summary available.").replace(/\n/g, "<br />")}</p>
    <h2>Structured Payload</h2>
    <pre>${JSON.stringify(result.visibleReport.payload, null, 2)}</pre>
  </body>
</html>`;

  return {
    report: result.visibleReport,
    contentType:
      args.format === "html"
        ? "text/html; charset=utf-8"
        : "text/markdown; charset=utf-8",
    body: args.format === "html" ? html : markdown,
    fileName: `${result.visibleReport.studentCode}-${result.visibleReport.reportType}.${args.format === "html" ? "html" : "md"}`,
  };
}

export async function getClinicalCoreSnapshot(options?: {
  actorProfileId?: string | null;
}): Promise<ClinicalCoreSnapshot> {
  const database = await checkDatabaseHealth();

  if (database.status === "down") {
    return {
      database,
      stats: {
        therapySessions: 0,
        clinicalNotes: 0,
        soapNotes: 0,
        reports: 0,
        finalizedNotes: 0,
      },
      therapySessions: [],
      clinicalNotes: [],
      soapNotes: [],
      clinicalReports: [],
      organizations: [],
      students: [],
      professionalProfiles: [],
      sessionReferences: [],
      noteReferences: [],
    };
  }

  const authorization = await authorizeInternalReadPermission({
    actorProfileId: options?.actorProfileId,
    permissionCodes: ["clinical.read"],
  });

  const [
    therapySessions,
    clinicalNotes,
    soapNotes,
    clinicalReports,
    organizations,
    students,
    professionalProfiles,
    sessionReferences,
    noteReferences,
  ] = await Promise.all([
    listTherapySessions(),
    listClinicalNotes(),
    listSoapNotes(),
    listClinicalReports(),
    dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
      `select id, display_name as "displayName" from organizations order by display_name asc`,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
      `
          select id, concat(canonical_code, ' · ', first_name, ' ', last_name) as "displayName"
          from student_core_profiles
          order by canonical_code asc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
      `
          select id, full_name as "displayName"
          from profiles
          where role = 'professional' and status = 'active'
          order by full_name asc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
      `
          select id, concat(session_type, ' · ', to_char(started_at, 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI')) as "displayName"
          from therapy_sessions
          order by started_at desc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
    dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
      `
          select id, concat(title, ' · ', note_type) as "displayName"
          from clinical_notes
          order by created_at desc
        `,
    ).then((result) => result.rows),
  ]);

  const scopedTherapySessions = applyOrganizationScope(
    therapySessions,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedClinicalNotes = applyOrganizationScope(
    clinicalNotes,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedSoapNotes = applyOrganizationScope(
    soapNotes,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const scopedClinicalReports = applyOrganizationScope(
    clinicalReports,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.organizationId,
  );
  const visibleTherapySessions = await applyClinicalAccessToTherapySessions(
    scopedTherapySessions,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
    "operational_console",
  );
  const visibleClinicalNotes = await applyClinicalAccessToNotes(
    scopedClinicalNotes,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
    "operational_console",
  );
  const visibleSoapNotes = await applyClinicalAccessToSoapNotes(
    scopedSoapNotes,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
    "operational_console",
  );
  const visibleClinicalReports = await applyClinicalAccessToReports(
    scopedClinicalReports,
    authorization.actorProfileId,
    "operational_console",
  );
  const scopedOrganizations = applyOrganizationScope(
    organizations,
    authorization.organizationScope,
    (item) => item.id,
  );
  const scopedStudents =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? students
      : (
          await dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
            `
              select id, concat(canonical_code, ' · ', first_name, ' ', last_name) as "displayName"
              from student_core_profiles
              where organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
              order by canonical_code asc
            `,
            [authorization.organizationScope],
          )
        ).rows;
  const scopedProfessionalProfiles =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? professionalProfiles
      : (
          await dbQuery<ClinicalCoreReference>(
            `
              select distinct p.id, p.full_name as "displayName"
              from organization_memberships om
              inner join profiles p on p.id = om.profile_id
              where om.organization_id = any($1::uuid[])
                and p.role = 'professional'
                and p.status = 'active'
              order by p.full_name asc
            `,
            [authorization.organizationScope],
          )
        ).rows;
  const scopedSessionReferences =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? sessionReferences
      : visibleTherapySessions.map((session) => ({
          id: session.id,
          displayName: `${session.sessionType} · ${formatReferenceDateTime(session.startedAt)}`,
        }));
  const scopedNoteReferences =
    authorization.organizationScope === null
      ? noteReferences
      : visibleClinicalNotes.map((note) => ({
          id: note.id,
          displayName: `${note.title} · ${note.noteType}`,
        }));

  return {
    database,
    stats: {
      therapySessions: visibleTherapySessions.length,
      clinicalNotes: visibleClinicalNotes.length,
      soapNotes: visibleSoapNotes.length,
      reports: visibleClinicalReports.length,
      finalizedNotes: visibleClinicalNotes.filter(
        (note) => note.status === "finalized",
      ).length,
    },
    therapySessions: visibleTherapySessions,
    clinicalNotes: visibleClinicalNotes,
    soapNotes: visibleSoapNotes,
    clinicalReports: visibleClinicalReports,
    organizations: scopedOrganizations,
    students: scopedStudents,
    professionalProfiles: scopedProfessionalProfiles,
    sessionReferences: scopedSessionReferences,
    noteReferences: scopedNoteReferences,
  };
}
